                   President of the World Peace Unification Family, Hwang Seon-jo

1)
The Restoration
<Prayer> Heavenly Father, please be with us along with your gracious blessings. Though each of our hearts may be different, when you look upon us, may we all be recognized as your sons and daughters within your heart. Now, please allow us to become sons and daughters who can align with your desires and who cannot help but be loved by you. 
Before you, may we humbly lay bare all that we are and become those who seek the gift of compassion. Rather than lamenting our lowly and humble selves, may our hearts be filled with admiration for your high and precious holy gifts. 
Please allow our heartfelt desire to serve you to rise more fervently than anyone else's within our hearts. We earnestly wish to be in a position where we can truly feel your presence and admire you as our central Father. 
We are lacking and unnoticed by the world, yet we are grateful that you have chosen us through your high and precious gifts. Whenever we think about how much you have endured and persevered in seeking us, we wish to be children who can shed tears of gratitude before you rather than lamenting our shortcomings. 
February 19, 1971 (Friday), Seodaemun Church.
* This message was given during a night tour of the nine districts in Seoul at the Seodaemun district headquarters and was also published in the March 1971 issue of <Unification World>.

The Restoration
Today, I will speak under the title "The Restoration." As you all know, the term restoration refers to returning to the original state before the fall. 
The position of Adam and Eve, created in the Garden of Eden and immersed in the realm of blessings through God's love, was indeed a holy place, a victorious place that all creation could praise. Despite being the ancestors of humanity, Adam and Eve devoted their lives to receiving and living with the inheritance from God, yet they lost all the blessings granted by God due to their fall. 
God's Heart in Observing Fallen Adam and Eve
Before their fall, Adam and Eve could be with God, but after the fall, they could no longer be with Him. Before their fall, they represented God's love, and there was no created being in the universe that did not have a relationship with them as God's beloved sons and daughters. However, after their fall, all creation became unable to relate to them. We must understand that Adam and Eve fell into a miserable position because of their fall. 
How miserable was their position? They fell to a place where they could not receive the entirety of existence. They could not relate to any relative world and fell into a position where they could not even establish a relationship with God. This is what the fall means. 
In other words, they lost their position as God's sons and daughters, and they fell into a position where they could not relate to God centered on His love. They lost all created beings that they were meant to govern, lost the source of their own life, which is God's love, and lost all relationships centered on God. This is the fall. 
However, the story does not end with the fall; despite being fallen, we have come into this world with a destiny that cannot be abandoned. In other words, even if a parent declares that they will sever ties with a child who has committed a great sin, that parent cannot forget the first love or first connection they had with that child. Even worldly parents feel this way. How much more so does God, who possesses a love greater than any earthly parent? Even though Adam and Eve fell, God cannot forget them. 
The higher the value of glory granted to Adam and Eve, the greater the corresponding sorrow and misery must be. We cannot overlook this. 
If there is a way to meet Adam and Eve, who have fallen into a position where they cannot return to God's embrace, God, the Creator and Parent, would naturally want to seek that one way to forgive them. Isn't this the heart of God, who is in the position of a parent? 
Even though Adam and Eve fell into a position where they could never establish a relationship again, God cannot forget the feelings of love He had for them when He could freely love and interact with them before their fall. This was the standard of happiness God felt towards Adam and Eve before their fall, and we must recognize that He cannot forget that happiness. 
When we look at the fallen Adam and Eve, who are the result of a single sorrowful fall, we might wish that God could simply cancel out the consequences of the fall and forget everything. However, the conclusion of love does not work that way. 
Even today, when fallen humans form connections with one another, the farther apart they become, the more they yearn for each other, especially when similar circumstances or conditions arise. When we consider the feelings of fallen humanity, we must understand that God, who possesses the heart of love, is in a position where He cannot sever ties with Adam and Eve. This is God's situation and heart, isn't it? 
No matter how much God thinks of Adam and Eve with such feelings, if they cannot fully accept God's thoughts and instead stand in a position that brings Him sorrow, blocking the path He wishes to take, we must consider how immense God's emotional pain must be in such circumstances. 
God's Responsibility for Human Fall
Although Adam and Eve fell into a pitiful and miserable position, God cannot forget His sons and daughters who have fallen into such a state. Originally, Adam and Eve, as God's children, should not have fallen into such a position. 
Adam and Eve were meant to be the true ancestors of humanity, revered by all and standing in the absolute position as the source of life for the universe, receiving love from all. That was the value of a completed human being. 
If God were to cancel out the emotional differences between the high and low positions of fallen humanity, it would be easy to do so from a high position to a low one. However, in the emotional world, it is impossible to cancel such feelings. This is something everyone must understand. 
Therefore, we cannot help but think about how great God's inner struggles must have been in observing Adam. The motivation for their fall did not lie with God but rather with Adam and Eve's failure to fulfill their responsibility. However, God could not leave that responsibility to humanity. This is because fallen humanity, having already fallen into a position from which they cannot return, cannot rise to any environment or standard that is not self-destructive. God understood that humanity could not be entrusted with everything. He also knew that if He entrusted that responsibility to humanity, they would end in eternal destruction. 
Thus, God, feeling that the fall of humanity was due to His creation and His failure to fulfill His responsibility, resolved not to place the responsibility of the fall on humanity but to take it upon Himself. In other words, He decided to bear the responsibility for the fall and to prepare a way for forgiveness, which is a process that is difficult for us to comprehend. 
In this world, if a parent has a beloved son or daughter, especially an only child, they will pour all their love and effort into raising them. If a parent has raised a child with great care after experiencing all the feelings of the world and finally having a precious child, how great would their sorrow be if that child were to go down the path of fall and betray them? There would be no justification for the parent. 
Even if the parent has only reasons to scold the child, and even if they must expel that child, they still hope for a way for that child to be reborn, to return, even if it is just a glimmer of hope. Even fallen parents feel this way towards children they cannot sever ties with; how much more so would the original God feel? You must understand that God cannot help but have such feelings. 
For fallen Adam, the thought of being restored is unimaginable. Therefore, we can infer that God began to take responsibility for restoring fallen humanity, hoping that humanity would establish some condition for restoration. Although fallen humanity cannot restore themselves, God desired to restore them by establishing some conditions. 
Even if one's misery reaches its peak, one must establish a relative condition that shows sincerity towards God and fulfills one's duty before Him. You must understand how painful it is for God to be in a position where He cannot avoid requiring such conditions. 
Fallen humanity cannot establish a relationship with God. This is because humanity was born centered on fallen love, not on the ideal love of God. Therefore, the motivations for all life and desire are in opposition to God's ideal love, life, and wishes. Thus, the question of how to return to God's realm of desires, life, and love is an extremely difficult issue. 
For fallen humanity to stand before God
For humanity to approach God, there must be a foundation for mutual harmony, allowing for movement when one moves. If there had been even an internal motivation for this, a contact point could have been established. However, humanity stands in opposition to God. 
When God appears as a positive force, humanity appears as a negative force, and instead of expanding the basis for a cooperative relationship, humanity has manifested as an evil force before God's goodness. This is the problem. 
Positive cannot unite with positive. Even similar positive forces repel each other, and humanity has appeared not as a similar positive but as an opposing positive. How great must the repulsion be? How miserable must God be, who must present elements or conditions to draw humanity back into connection with Him? And how much suffering must humanity endure and effort must they exert to present such conditions? 
This is not normal; it is abnormal. Without making an abnormal resolution, nothing new can be determined.
At that time, can humanity itself act in a way that can correspond and harmonize with God from an abnormal position? It cannot be done. That is why God must guide humanity from behind, allowing them to set at least nine out of ten conditions. When considering the issue of needing to teach this, can God directly appear to humans and teach them? It cannot be done that way. It would be nice if it could be done, but it cannot.

There is no other being that can teach and relate to fallen humanity. Since humanity, which was once alone with angels, has fallen, if there were a third type of human, it is unknown, but there is no being that can teach humanity. 

What should those who have fallen and do not know the way do? If everything they desire unfolds naturally in a good situation, it ends there. It flows away just like that. However, in order to revive such people, God blocks their path. He makes them feel fear, saying, "You!" and presses down from above, causing their gaze to turn. That is why the path of life is a purgatory. How much of a purgatory is it? It is living without being able to die. If one just sits still with a predetermined method, they cannot return, so by blocking the path and providing a common route, they will unknowingly enter that realm and become surrounded. Such a strategy can succeed. Wouldn't it?

Therefore, humanity must suffer. People must be busy and endure hardships until the age of 30. However, if there are those who are resting in a comfortable position, they should not be left alone because they will fall if left as is. They must be pushed out onto a narrow path where they cannot go back or sideways. It is like kneading flour and putting it into a container with one side open; it can only be forced out that way. Is there any other method?

Then, who should be pushed out first? Should it be the men or the women? When considering this issue, you must understand that there cannot be a lack of coercion in the course of human history.

What happens if parents leave their children to do as they please? All ten will flow away. It is said that loving children should be sent on journeys and given the most humble thatched houses. There must be a coercive law that says, "Do it this way." If a child is allowed to go where they want, it will lead to disaster. If they go where they want, everything will be ruined.

So what should be done? They must be pushed towards what they dislike. Who pushes them towards what they dislike? It is not the devil that pushes them. Humans are bound within the realm of the devil, so if they just flutter about, they will be led to ruin. Therefore, God pushes the good spirits in the opposite direction to free them from that. If they want to eat, they are prevented from eating; if they want to go, they are prevented from going; if they want to see, they are prevented from seeing; if they want to go left, they are made to go right; everything works in the opposite direction. You must understand that God cannot help but do such things.

The more true the path, the more suffering there is.

Even if you say, "That family is a good lineage," the children of that family must be careful about everything. In other words, sons raised in a distinguished family must be cautious about everything. They must be careful even when taking a single step, when speaking a single word, and when taking any action. The etiquette is complex. Is there anyone who likes this? Nowadays, freedom has become excessive, leading to a state of indulgent freedom that has reached saturation and become very serious. Do young people today like such etiquette? If left as is, everything will be ruined. There is nowhere to go.

In a family with dignity, there are many resources to educate children. They gather children and teach them how to treat elders, siblings, and parents.

Students, do you like going to school? Do you enjoy studying at school? In reality, what is enjoyable about studying? Think about it. Going to school early in the morning and sitting for five or six hours listening to the teacher's words—what does it accomplish? It seems like nothing will come of it immediately. They say they are studying, but does it taste like food eaten when hungry? It is frustrating. From this perspective, everyone dislikes studying. However, since one must study, they do it reluctantly.

In our human world, if we want to live freely and act freely, there will inevitably be a brake applied. Why is that? Because if left as is, it will lead to ruin. The more true the path, the more the brakes will be applied in proportion. This is because humanity has fallen. You all know that God exists because you are members of the Unification Church, right? "Yes." This conversation should start from whether God exists, but since you know, I won't discuss that.

God carries out a history that completely blocks what humans want to do because without doing so, fallen humanity cannot be saved. The method of saving fallen humans, who stand in a position fundamentally opposed to God, cannot be sought by humanity itself. It is God who seeks it.

So how does God seek it? He does not leave humanity as is. He must draw them in and confine them within a city to teach them. It is akin to what the world calls kidnapping.

If an evil person kidnaps a good person and turns them evil, that is evil. However, if a good person kidnaps an evil person and beats them or subjects them to all kinds of humiliation to make them a good person, is that good or evil? If an evil person is kidnapped and, if they do not listen, they are beaten with a stick, have their legs broken, and are dragged around until they can say, "Ah! I am a good person," then that person becomes a good person.

If they are kidnapped, have their nose pierced, are made to suffer, and are beaten with a stick, causing them to become bad and ruin themselves, that is evil. However, if they are treated that way and still become excellent, would they be grateful or resentful? How would you respond? Would you be resentful or grateful? You should be grateful.

The method by which God leads evil humans to a good path.

Even if these young ladies study hard, there is no chance of becoming the First Lady. However, if you were kidnapped, beaten, trampled, and made to suffer until you became the First Lady, would you be grateful or resentful? You would have to be grateful.

Then is the kidnapping good or evil? Is the suffering and training good or evil? Kidnapping and giving discipline are the same, but why does it become good? Because God is absolutely good, even if He beats with a stick, it is done from a position of goodness. If He captures you at the brink of death, it must be done from a position of goodness; otherwise, it would be a false God. Therefore, no matter how ruthless God may be, even if He lashes out, it is from a position of goodness. If that is done not to annihilate but to bestow blessings, is it evil or good? "It is good." You must understand that it is good.

Is it good or evil for thugs to kidnap good people and turn them evil? That is evil. At that time, both the kidnapping and the beating are evil, and the result is also evil.

When viewed this way, God does not leave humanity as is but blocks their paths and attempts to drive them into one place, seeking to lead the evil groups to a place where they cannot be seen. Is that a good method or a bad method? If such a method exists, how wonderful it would be!

What strategy does God use to drive humanity into one place? He makes the evil ones draw themselves in. Do you understand? God leads those who are drawn in by the evil ones. When they are drawn in like that, would they want to follow the evil ones or want to break away? They would be in a pitiful state, saying, "Oh!" as everyone else goes along.

When looking at the ground, it is useless; when looking at the sky, it is useless; when looking across, it is useless; when looking down, it is useless; when all people are drawn into a place they dislike, most evil people will gather there. That is what you should try.

If God were to kidnap people, it would not make sense, but if He places them in a position where they can brake and break away from evil people, all those evil groups will push that person away and hate them. So can they join together? No, they cannot. Thus, they become solitary. "In history, there is no one to believe in, no nation to believe in, and no world to believe in. I cannot die, cannot go, and cannot live; what should I do?" This is how it becomes.

So if something other than a human were to take me away, how wonderful would that be? This is where faith begins to manifest. Unknowingly, a great power arises to pursue that something. To create such a foundation for a human and to lead fallen humanity to the garden of life, God has been working hard and hastening this path.

When one realizes this fact, standing in a lonely place is not an unhappiness. Standing in a lonely place and reflecting on one's past while thinking about the essence of humanity, when one looks at the sun or this universe, they will surely realize that it did not just come into being. If there is an absolute God, they will find a way or a path to connect with that God.

When all hope for humanity is cut off and that person becomes a dropout on the path they must take, even when they see the rising sun, it does not bring hope; rather, they spend the day in despair, looking at the setting sun. How many people have spent sleepless nights, groaning at the crossroads of life and death, saying, "Oh God, if You exist, please show me my path"?

As they indulge in such fantasies, will they automatically fall behind in the world and separate from the people of the world? They will automatically fall behind. Because God kidnaps them, they will automatically separate. That is why religious people become dropouts in the course of human life. Are all religious people dropouts? Yes, right? Why is that? Because that is the only method God has.

Then does that mean that Reverend Moon of the Unification Church is also a dropout? I am not a dropout. That feels unpleasant. I am Reverend Moon of the Unification Church.

In any case, God works that way. Without it, there is no way. There is no way. Fallen humanity does not have the ability to cut that off. As they go, they unknowingly head down a path of ruin. Therefore, God cuts off all paths so that they cannot go. Thus, they are placed in a situation of life and death, where they can say they are dying.

The time when God initiates a strategy.

Everyone, in this world, there are spring, summer, autumn, and winter, right? Similarly, there are seasons like spring, summer, autumn, and winter in humanity, and there are also such things in the world of the heart. When looking at humanity, there is the spring-like youth period, the summer-like adulthood period, the autumn-like old age period, and the winter-like death period. When looking at a day, morning corresponds to spring, daytime corresponds to summer, evening corresponds to autumn, and night corresponds to winter. The heavens and earth all operate this way.

When spring comes, flowers bloom. When the spring of your youth arrives, all plants become green, and new flowers bloom again. In the same way, when humans go through the path of suffering, they will periodically yearn for their homeland. There are times when the heart automatically rises, yearning for the Father in the homeland without knowing why. Do you understand?

At that time, the door of the human heart opens wide. Although 365 days do not go around in a year, the door of the heart does not align with God all year round. However, after three years or seven years, there will be a time when it aligns perfectly. Do you understand? There are times when the door of the heart aligns with God’s door. When that door of the heart aligns perfectly with God’s door, it becomes a time when it can respond like spring.

At that time, one can finally respond with a heart that is in accord with God and seek a new way of life. When the heart is filled with the desire to break through the environment that is looked down upon by humans, and when one faces difficulties and groans, saying, "Oh God, help me. Teach me my path," when this aligns with the heart's door and the heavenly door, God will say, "Oh," and at that time, He will finally initiate the strategy. Do you understand? That is when He initiates the strategy. Such times do not occur frequently.

At such times, God reveals the strategy to the people of this world, teaching them that God exists. He tells them to go forward. It is not only humans who go; He teaches that God goes along with them. At that time, God begins anew.

When pumping air into a car tire or a bicycle tire, if the valve is tightly sealed, air cannot enter. However, if it is removed and air is pushed in, the seal breaks, and air enters. God hopes that such an action occurs between humanity and Himself. God desires that at the climax of the final peak, what has been blocked bursts forth. That moment is brief.

If a person born as a good person and a descendant of historically good ancestors plays the role of the valve, they can even reach the position of the Messiah. When one enters such a realm, strength immediately comes.

This is how the act of turning over occurs within my body. A battle ensues. This villain, you know? Right now, they are fighting, each claiming to be the best, right? They are fighting to become the master. If one abandons the self that is stubbornly clinging to the body and establishes a victorious foundation to welcome the joy of liberation, that person can be recognized. Do you understand? Such a person becomes a prophet and a seer. The prophet emerges at that time.

Prayer is an effort and sincerity to become one with God. 

Now, does this period automatically return? Is it easy to align with that time? Once you align once and then twice, you can know the direction. After the sun rises high, everything becomes clear, and you cannot tell whether the sun rose here or there. However, when it is time for the sun to rise in the morning, the place where the sun rises gradually becomes brighter, allowing you to know where it rises.
are present. Similarly, when your heart begins to connect with heaven a few times and opens up, you will know the direction. The door of such a person's heart must follow where God is going. You must open the door of your heart and be prepared to open it when heaven passes by. The time when heaven passes is short, so if you just stay still when it's time to open the door, it will slip by unnoticed. You must capture that moment well and hold on to the connections of motivation, life, emotions, experiences, and sensations. If you follow, you will return. To do that, you must open the door. You must have that experience and enter that realm. To enter that realm of feelings and experiences and to strive and dedicate yourself to become one with God is prayer. This is tuning the dial, isn't it?

Everyone, radios have waves, right? The frequency of KBS radio is 710 kilohertz, isn't it? Just like tuning the dial to catch that wave, you must tune the door of your heart. When you turn the radio dial to find that frequency, you hear a buzzing sound as the waves come in. 

As you engage in religious life, there may come a time when you realize that there is a true God. When you see the waves coming in, you first hear a buzzing noise. As the noise is heard and the dial aligns with the reference point, you will hear a vivid sound. In the same way, you are to receive grace. When the channel is perfectly aligned, the sound sent from the broadcasting station comes through vividly without any loss.

If someone has tasted that flavor and knows that flavor, would they want to follow for just a day? For just a year? They would want to follow until they grow old and die. This is the nature of humans. Therefore, those who have tasted the flavor of heaven will go even if their heads are cut off, and they will go even if told not to go.

From this perspective, the fallen ones in life are not pitiful. Just because they have become fallen humans... If there is an end, a new beginning can be made. If they do not perish there, a new beginning can occur. Therefore, even if you enter a place of ruin, do not say, "I am ruined."

Ah, in this fallen world, where you cannot trust parents, spouses, friends, teachers, or anyone! Where can I find someone I can trust more than my parents or siblings? You must center around this issue. Let those who want to leave go. Help them to leave. Therefore, on the path of becoming a fallen one, if there is a God, you must struggle to connect and relate with God. If there is someone who harbors a wish on the other side and does not despair but struggles to have new hope, a new beginning that does not perish will occur. You must be like that.

The era of religious people ruling is coming. 

So, for fallen humans to walk the true path, they must enter a path that is 100 percent opposite to the fallen world. Shouldn't it be that way? When asked whether people who are well-off in the world are happy or those who are not well-off, in the satanic world, it is said that those who are well-off are happier than those who are not. So, will God put a brake on those who are well-off globally, or not?

Today, we must recognize that the advanced country of the United States will not continue to dominate the world. When the time changes, those who were high will be brought low. According to communist theory, the time will come when workers and farmers will rise. In the past, it was the intellectuals, the smart people, who held power and succeeded. Now, it is the time for those who are strong and physically capable to succeed. Isn't that right? Now, strength is necessary. We are in the era of warlords. Before strength, everyone submits. However, if you think that submitting by strength will end there, it is not so.

What comes next is hands and feet. The time will come when workers and farmers will dominate. Isn't that so? The world is heading in that direction. Initially, smart people ruled. Then, those who used strength, that is, those who used their fists, ruled. After that, the time will come when hands and feet will rule. Now, workers and farmers are trying hard to succeed.

Smart people once ruled the world, and now those with strength are ruling the world, and now even workers and farmers are trying to rule the world, but the ones with nothing to show for it are the religious people. 

Those who believe in religion have never succeeded and ruled the world. However, do not underestimate them. As the fallen ones in the human world, they have been treated like waste, but to whom could they easily become a tool? To God. Because they are people who can have brakes put on them by God and can hope, when they finally establish themselves and stand tall, taking a deep breath and commanding the world, then even the smart people, the strong people, and the communists who tried to mobilize workers and farmers to dominate the world will all perish.

Currently, there are over 2 billion people within the religious realm. Now is the time for religious people to rise. Communism is trying to mobilize workers and farmers to dominate the world, right? In the future, a great army of religion will emerge in this world, calling for the mobilization of conscientious people among humanity. When that day comes, there will be no place for smart people, no place for strong people, and no place for communism that tried to mobilize workers and farmers to dominate the world.

Then who will rise? God will rise. With whom? With the religious people who are in the position of the most fallen among humans. Do you understand? That is how the world will be. Now, who is left with the final right to rise? The era of workers and farmers will also pass. Now, the Soviet Union and China are fighting each other. Religions are also fighting each other. Because such times are coming, the Unification Church has raised the banner that "All religions of the world shall become one."

That is commendable. The Unification Church may or may not unify religions, but just the fact that it claims to unify religions and has planted its flag is something Korea can be proud of. This is the only thing Korea can be proud of. Since this flag was raised by Reverend Moon of the Unification Church, we must inevitably commend Reverend Moon of the Unification Church.

Prepare for hardship. 

The followers of the Unification Church say that even if they want to follow Reverend Moon, they are worried to death. So-called college students are making a fuss about this and that, but they should not be so loud. I have gone through my college days too. It is nothing special. They are just showing off and making a fuss, but when you look inside, there is nothing there. To me, it seems like there is nothing but a rotten skull. Even if you feel sad about it, there is nothing you can do. Those who want to protest can protest. I have dug into all that and am doing this now.

In the future, when a politician in the world, such as the President of the United States, raises the flag saying, "I am a member of the Unification Church," and the day comes when the Unification Church unifies religion in the United States, no one can become the President of the United States without the approval of the Unification Church. This is because two-thirds of the 180 million citizens of the United States are registered Christian believers. If these people are unified, then even the President of the United States cannot become President without the signature of the one who unified them. Isn't that so? In Korea, there are over 15 million religious people. More than half of the population are religious. How wonderful it would be if we could unify all of them!

Then, in what position should we unify? If you unify in a position that you like, it is meaningless. Do you understand? A person who wants to unify in a position that they like is a child of the devil; it is unpleasant to say, but it cannot be helped. You cannot unify in that position. Even if you try to unify in such a position, you will fight again and break apart again. Therefore, to unify, you must strike from the opposite side. Even if you strike from the opposite side, you must go at it with determination. You must climb up with the resolve that if you lose your mind while going, you will die if you do not go.

Not just anyone can enter the Unification Church. Even if they do enter, they cannot withstand Reverend Moon's training. Whether they are gentlemen or ladies, they will work hard until their spines stick out. You should never think that it will always be good. Have you seen established church pastors say such things? They all advertise for people to come, but they do not advertise for people not to come. They only say to come, so you do not know what the circumstances are. It is less disappointing if something goes wrong in a place that says not to come than if something goes wrong in a place that says to come. It is less frustrating. However, if something goes right in a place that says to fail, there is nothing better than that.

Looking at it this way, isn't it more interesting to go to a place that says not to come than to a place that says to come? In middle and high school, sneaking into a movie theater to watch a movie while avoiding the teacher who is standing guard saying not to watch movies is much more fun, isn't it? (Laughter)

Therefore, a person who says they will walk the good path while trying to find goodness in that position is a mad person. If you say you will find God in that position, it absolutely will not work. If the roots are already planted in evil, do you think goodness will come out of there? If there is goodness there, it will be eaten up by evil. The root must be changed. Isn't that so? If the foundation started in evil, you cannot just say it is good.

When you go to the market, there are peddlers selling fake medicine who advertise, "It's good, it's good!" and excite the hearts of the ladies passing by. Therefore, all descendants in the form of the archangel must be captured on God's side. After that, He must find Eve, who can become God's daughter, and He must find Adam, whom He has lost.

Finding these must be done individually, within families, within clans, within nations, and globally. This is the path of restoration. Restoration cannot be achieved by finding individuals alone. First, individuals must completely unite to create a new family. That new family must create a new clan, that clan must create a new nation, and that nation must form a new ideological world. This is the path of restoration.

Fallen humanity must unconditionally obey God.
This world must be turned upside down. What happens when you turn a bag inside out? Is it upside down or right side up? When you turn a bag inside out, does it look like the old days or the opposite? "It is the opposite." That is the kind of world that must be created. Therefore, when new things are put into it, God will be with us. So what must you do? You must reach this standard of grief.
must be. Fallen humanity must unconditionally comply with whatever strategy God employs. 

Taking away good things and giving bad things is evil. When good things are taken away and bad things are given, everyone dislikes it. Isn't that right? That is evil. We must understand what good and evil are. Taking away good things and giving bad things is evil, while taking away bad things and giving good things is good. 

So, are you living correctly in this world, or incorrectly? You are living incorrectly. When it is said that you will have the opportunity to take away the incorrect way of living and be given a better way to live, is it good to accept that or not? To accept it is good. Is it a good thing to try to take away what belongs to you? Is it a good thing to say, "Oh, I will not let that be taken away"? 

When they try to take away your things, they take everything. For example, when it comes to taking off clothes, if they have to take off your innerwear too, and you say you will not take it off even if you die, what should be done? If they are going to take off your clothes, shouldn't they take off your innerwear as well? What should be done when you refuse to take it off? You have to make them half-dead and stretch them out to take off their clothes. Then, they will be dressed in wonderful clothes that will not change even if worn for a thousand years. Will they dance in those clothes or not? They will dance. So, they are taking away what they like. The Unification Church must do such things. However, taking away good things and giving bad things is evil. If bad things are given, the whole community should rise up and drive them away. 

Today, in the Unification Church, Reverend Moon is doing such things. Looking at the blessed 1,200 families, they are living difficult lives. The members of the Unification Church have truly suffered a lot. Because they have lived difficult lives, they had the hope of living well after receiving blessings. They tried to prepare pots and bowls to live, but they are told to throw everything away. Having gone out to evangelize like this, when they think quietly, if they have lost everything and received only bad things, will Reverend Moon be driven away or will he stay? Even if they say they will stay and perform rituals, they cannot remain. However, if they have lost everything and have been driven out but return to a situation that is several times better, can those who have complained and fantasized in their hearts see the teacher's face? At that time, they will come in with their heads bowed low. You must understand that. 

To gain life, one must go to the place where life is taken away. To save life, one must go to the place where life is taken away. Did Jesus think about dying beforehand? Jesus did not think even in his dreams that he would die at the age of thirty-three. He was not destined to die. There is no need to explain that. Jesus never thought of dying. When Elijah and Moses suddenly appeared on the Mount of Transfiguration and spoke of Jesus' death, it was like a bolt from the blue. All circumstances were arranged so that he could not avoid death. 

Thus, Jesus went to the Garden of Gethsemane and prayed, "My Father, if it is possible, let this cup pass from me; nevertheless, not as I will, but as You will." (Matthew 26:39) How pitiful is this? Is this a prayer a child should make? "If possible, let this cup pass from me. If possible, do not let me die…" How urgent must he have been to pray like this? Looking at this, did Jesus think he would die? Jesus did not think of dying even in his dreams. It was a sudden change. 

After praying like that, feeling sorry, he said, "But let it be according to Your will, not mine." It would have been enough to say it once, but he said it three times, which is how pitiful it is. He faced a situation where his bones were tightening. Even after praying twice, hoping for news, there was no news, and even after praying three times, he waited for news, but it was completely silent. If he had prayed three times, wouldn't he have known? Was there a need to pray again? So, he had no choice but to choose the path of the cross. 

By sacrificing his one life, Christianity remains globally today. Isn't that so? At that time, people only saw Jesus as a young man. Who would recognize the son of a carpenter? They saw him as a worthless person. When Jesus was arrested, Peter fled at night, didn't he? Even Jesus' mother and father could not approach the cross where Jesus was hanging and watched from a distance. Do you know how imposing the power of the Roman Empire was at that time? The fact that the dead Jesus can move the world today is a great fact. If he had not died like that, nothing would have been accomplished. 

Therefore, what is evil? It is taking away good things and giving bad things. Therefore, to resolve God's sorrow, what must be done? Giving my good things to God and taking away God's bad things is what resolves God's sorrow. Isn't that right? If you give bad things and take away good things, that causes God to accumulate sorrow. If you do that two or three times, you will accumulate that much more sorrow for God.

When God sees a son who puts in more effort than anyone else, He cannot help but respond.

That mother may appear pitiful, grieving for her child, but when Adam and Eve, who had the highest hope to give infinite happiness and ideals of goodness to humanity, suddenly find themselves shattered, what must God's heart have felt? No matter how great human sorrow is, can it compare to that? That is why those who know God's will cannot shed tears even if their child dies suddenly; even if they face something that makes their teeth chatter, they must comfort God. We must understand that this is what humans should do.
In human relationships, those who try to take responsibility for each other's difficulties and leave good things for others can fulfill the responsibility of resolving God's sorrow in the human world. Do you understand what I mean?
You must understand that joy and glory can only be elevated when you stand in a position of joy in suffering. Therefore, to resolve God's sorrow, you must be certain that you cannot do so without going the path of suffering, without going the path of sacrifice, and without putting a burden on others.

2)
Advancement and Stagnation
<Prayer> Father, please allow us to praise you within the realm of meaningful daily life. May we become sons and daughters who walk a profound path of submission before you as the embodiment of joy that can comfort you centered on the hope of tomorrow.
We, who are bowed down in this place, may appear inadequate before you, but please guard each of our hearts so that we may become true children. Help us discern what kind of appearance pleases you and what kind of appearance remains as a condition of evil. Thus, I earnestly hope and wish that you will fill us with a burning desire to become the appearance you desire.
Father, we always long for you. Therefore, please embrace us with your love so that we may become children who can please you. May we become your children who are not forgotten in your heart, in your will, and in your love.
This morning, please bless your beloved children scattered across the land of South Korea. May your holy love and merciful touch be with those who bow toward this place and pray with all their hearts and bodies. I earnestly hope and wish that your infinite love and compassion will be with your children who continuously pray for heaven.
Father, please take care of all our circumstances. We, who are welcoming a new era with new intentions, earnestly hope and wish to be your children who walk the path of heaven with a heart that yearns for you.
Father! You know the tragic state of this land, divided between the South and the North. Please take charge of the fate of this country. When considering the principle of indemnity and restoration between Cain and Abel, we know who Abel's position is today and who Cain's position is. We also understand how heavy the responsibility is for us, who are in the position of Abel. When we think about the tremendous fact that we must first find Cain and make him bow before you before we can fulfill our duty of filial piety before you, we feel that we are inadequate to stand before your will. However, we cannot delay before your will, so we will go out to the battlefield with the hope of tomorrow, so please allow us to achieve a victorious day of making Cain bow before you.
Even in the same life, in an environment that is easy to become habitual, please help us remember heaven and yearn for heaven as we advance. May we become your beloved sons and daughters who can dedicate the entirety of our daily lives before you, promising victory together with you.
Please remember your children in Korea, and comfort your children who bow their heads toward this land, which is one country in Asia, while struggling in lonely places and being trampled by difficult environments, yet longing for you and appealing their lonely circumstances before you.
I know that you have worked in such positions until now. I have come to understand that unless we break through such lonely battlefields, your will cannot be fulfilled, so please protect those lonely children and bless them.
Father, may we become children who reveal our exceedingly low and humble selves before your great and high presence and earnestly desire your merciful and compassionate touch.
You, who are the source of power, you, who are the driving force of life, you, who are the foundation of love and heart, we, as a single entity before you, as branches and leaves, entrust everything to you, and if you are sad, we must also be sad; if you are happy, we must also be happy; if you are busy working, we must also be busy working. In this regard, may we become your sons and daughters who engage with all living environments alongside you.
When we reveal our appearance before your presence, we must reflect on whether we are in the appearance you desire, one that you can delight in and approach, and whether we have become sons and daughters who can receive your personal guidance and whisperings on the path we should take. To become such sons and daughters, we must fulfill our duty of filial piety and loyalty before you more than anyone else, and we must be able to offer even our lives before you.
When we lose the connection of being your sons, we realize that we cannot remain before your will in the stage of life, so please melt our hearts, which are like stone, and make them resemble your heart. May the circumstances of the Father and our circumstances meet so that we can form a bond that allows us to be absorbed into you.
We must not be left lamenting our lives with the passing of time, but as your sons, we must have the authority to greet a joyful day, a delightful day, and a proud day, filled with hope for a vigorous tomorrow. But how pitiful are the sons and daughters who have not yet experienced such days!
Having understood your will, we know your power and experience your amazement, and we must stand confidently and authoritatively as victors of tomorrow, as builders of today, and as victors of history. Therefore, may we become your sons and daughters who can always resolve to not become pitiful people who sigh and cannot present ourselves.
Now, may our hearts be equipped with the appearance that can please you, and may our bodies be equipped with the appearance that you desire. May our bodies become the altar of victory, and may our hearts become the sacrificial offerings of victory, eternally dedicated before you. Thus, may we become the sons and daughters who are not ashamed to be presented before the universe as the offerings you have longed for and the embodiment of your wishes. How much have you longed for such sons and daughters? We must not forget this.

As pitiful humans who cannot live outside the realm of heavenly connections, if we can make everything the motive for our connection with you and live in the joy of being able to harmonize with you, even if we live a day and die, we will feel that we have nothing more to wish for as humans. Please allow us to become precious sons and daughters who can feel this.
We must become your sons and daughters who bring joy, hope, and victory before you to greet a new day. Thus, we must become your holy group that can prepare ourselves to lead the charge to subdue enemies scattered throughout the world, including the North and South, and bow before your will.

<Words> The most problematic thing in our faith life is whether we take a step closer to the desired goal centered on ourselves or retreat. 
The path of restoration that God has walked in the way of advancement.
In order to welcome a better tomorrow than today, one must pursue something more valuable, and the more one pursues it, the greater the content of that pursuit, the more one must have the mindset to double the degree of progress that can be made. Without this mindset, it becomes difficult to achieve the purpose of that pursuit. If one finds themselves in a position where they should be advancing centered around such a purpose but instead are unable to move forward and come to a standstill, then they cannot avoid the path of retreat. This is a fact that we can often feel within our daily lives.

For example, when meeting a friend and having a conversation, if there are words of encouragement and more valuable content today than what was exchanged yesterday, then one can surely resolve to advance internally, and along with that resolution, one can elevate their own environment on the stage of life. However, if the content of the conversation between the two people brings disappointment rather than encouragement compared to yesterday, then there will inevitably be an internal story that leads to retreat. When that happens, the relationship between the two people will naturally distance, and oneself will fall into a position that is worse than not having a conversation at all, which we can clearly feel through our daily lives.

The fate of a nation is no different. Regardless of which nation is considered, whether that nation is advancing, in a state of stagnation, or retreating is undoubtedly the most significant issue.

From this perspective, the same can be said about today's world. In today's world, two camps are fighting against each other with opposing ideological systems, each presenting a different appearance. When considering which of these two camps will achieve victory and which camp will guide the world forward, we cannot help but think about whether these opposing camps are advancing, stagnating, or retreating. If either camp stands in a position of stagnation, it becomes extremely difficult to advance from there. Furthermore, if they are in retreat, they will face even worse outcomes than simply being stagnant.

Regardless of any ideology or thought, if it continues to advance, ultimately all of humanity will unite around it, and this united humanity will not only end it in one generation but will leave it as a tradition that connects to future generations, allowing it to shine even more as history flows. A claim or ideological system that has such a multi-dimensional content cannot help but follow the path of development. In other words, in order to develop, it is not enough to merely consume all the conditions that have gradually developed throughout history; rather, it must serve as the foundation of life from which new branches and leaves can sprout, requiring some contribution to be made. Otherwise, it cannot advance.

From this perspective, when we look at God's providence, we see that God has been developing providence through the past, present, and future, and is undoubtedly taking steps forward in the present that are more advanced than in the past.

Then, considering how far we have advanced until now, we must think about whether we can continue to advance in the future that lies ahead. If we conclude that we can no longer advance, then a state of stagnation will ensue from there, and we must understand that a path of retreat is inevitably waiting.

The question is whether we can continue to advance.

Everyone wishes to avoid failure and hopes for success. All people hope for and pursue the day of success with their hearts and bodies, but no one desires failure. The environment itself does not wish for it either, but we cannot deny that in our daily lives, the frequency of failure is often greater than that of success.

Moreover, when we consider that we are in a position to experience and feel this in our daily lives, retreat becomes something akin to an enemy to us. Therefore, we must hold onto an absolute position that says we will overcome this and that retreat has nothing to do with us; this is an inevitable requirement for those who hope for tomorrow.

Thus, having a point of victory today should not lead to boasting, but rather we must consider the possibility of stagnation and retreat that may occur tomorrow and be able to analyze and critique today's victory. Therefore, even if we achieve some victory today, we cannot simply rejoice in that victory; we must hope that the position of those who are advancing will improve.

Thus, if there is a victory today, that victory must become the new foundation for tomorrow, and if there is an advanced foundation today, it should not end there but must become the basis for tomorrow's life and the ideological requirements. Therefore, if we have achieved any victory today, we must have the ability and autonomy to digest that victory into a foundation from which we can pioneer a broader tomorrow. If we cannot do this, then no matter how much victory we achieve in the present and how progressive our path may be, we will not be able to realize our hopes and will find it difficult to achieve greater goals.

We are connecting moments that have passed through the processes of the past, present, and future. Therefore, we must recognize how precious today is and how valuable the present is.

Joy can only be felt in the midst of advancement.

Today, in order to maintain life, we must continuously breathe. We must also supply nutrition accordingly. If the nutrients supplied differ from yesterday in the circulation of our bodies, our physical condition will not be good. However, if we provide even a little more nutrition today than yesterday while maintaining a normal bodily rhythm, our bodies will naturally become healthier. From there, we can see that a new foundation for advancement is being established.

Similarly, in your spiritual life, something akin to nutrients is essential. A normal attitude toward life, akin to breathing, is also necessary. In other words, one must have a personal standard of faith centered around the thought, "I must proceed like this," and must walk the path of faith as if breathing. There must be a normal standard that can supply life force. Then, accordingly, it becomes possible to supply nutrients. The question then becomes how to supply those nutrients and how to reinforce the pathways for supplying normal nutrients in front and behind, from all directions. The issue is how to supply better and more valuable nutrients from today compared to yesterday, and from this moment to the next.

In your spiritual life, joy can only be felt in the process of advancing and developing. Therefore, one must always think about how to receive such content.

When a person works, if the outcome is worse than before they started, they will inevitably suffer a blow. To say it is bad means it has retreated a step, while to say it is good means it has advanced a step. From this perspective, we must recognize that it is extremely difficult for us, living in this sinful world, to leave behind results that can be called joyful in all areas of our daily lives.

How to handle real issues is important.

When facing ten people, we often feel that more often than not, they bring more negative results than positive ones. Therefore, how can we reinforce this negative outcome? If there is no way to reinforce it, then in the environment where we are active, our spiritual life or our path forward cannot yield progressive results, and we will inevitably encounter the path of retreat.

Thus, what must always be emphasized is that it is not a matter of how I have done in the past, but rather that today, from this moment onward, is the issue. It is extremely important to understand how to handle the realistic problems I am facing today.

When faced with someone we do not wish to meet, we must first consider how to deal with them and what to do with the results that appear afterward. Therefore, even if we find ourselves in a sad and lonely situation, we must draw a line and not go any lower or suffer any further blows, maintaining a relationship with others that does not cross that line.

When working in a job, one must also understand what position they are in while working. They must consider whether they will advance or retreat in that job. It is essential to think about whether the workplace can serve as a foundation for tomorrow's hope and whether it can remain an indispensable relationship today.

However, if the relationship between work and oneself does not remain as necessary and appropriate content for one's spiritual life but merely serves as a source of comfort, it will lead to a step of retreat rather than stagnation. Therefore, it is crucial to clearly understand that your current position influences your life and death.

A clear purpose and good motivation are necessary for advancement.

Even when holding a pen at work and writing a single character, one must have a clear sense of purpose regarding for whom they are writing. Living for the will of heaven and establishing a relationship with it yields more effective results than living for oneself. Therefore, what I live for must be concluded in relation to heaven rather than merely for myself; only then can we find joy in our lives. Ultimately, since I am not the subject but heaven is, we must build content that can please heaven, so that we, in our relative positions, can feel joy. This is a natural principle.

The motivation for all actions is related to oneself, but the outcome should not center around oneself; rather, it should be based on a greater purpose that adds to that purpose. How much of such elements we leave behind while living each day is important. As we accumulate more and more of these elements, higher and greater hopes will also rise.

The same applies when we engage in evangelism. The mindset we have when evangelizing today must differ from the mindset we had yesterday. In other words, if we set out with a certain mindset yesterday, today we must start with a new mindset and determination; if we embark with such a different resolve from the outset, it will undoubtedly yield good results. However, if we start from a lower position than before, with a mindset that is worse than yesterday, we will inevitably walk the path of retreat. The more we continue to work in such an environment, the more we will bring about a breakdown. Moreover, if this is not one-sided but generates feelings of retreat from all sides, no matter how great the purpose or how firmly we resolve ourselves, we will experience a state of stagnation, a completely fixed position where we cannot move.

Whether we advance or retreat is up to ourselves.

When we consider the issue of advancement and stagnation, the question becomes who stimulates this. No external environment can make us advance. Likewise, no external circumstances can cause us to retreat. Who is the foundation that makes us advance or retreat? It is not some relative condition but rather ourselves. Ultimately, it is a matter of ourselves. It is not because someone we interacted with was bad that we find ourselves in this situation; it is because there is an issue within ourselves.

Therefore, you must always feel that your retreat is due to yourself and that your advancement is also due to yourself. The foundation that causes you to advance or retreat is precisely yourself. Do not think that such issues arise from others. Do not consider them as issues that arise independently of yourself. You must understand that all issues that arise are necessarily related to you. Whether these issues determine the meaningful value of your life or lead to unfruitful results also depends on yourself. Therefore, you must think of a solution to resolve these issues.

From this perspective, you must always stand in a subjective position and engage with all issues and relationships, handling them to achieve victory as a result. Without adopting this attitude and position in your spiritual life, no matter how excellent that life may be, it will yield only passive results. You must clearly understand that you cannot achieve direct victory with passive results. Therefore, you should not say, "I retreated because of someone," or "I am like this because of someone."

Digest sorrow into joy.

To achieve greater results, one must first go through the corresponding negative environment. Why? Because we live in a fallen world. Therefore, before grace comes, the work of Satan occurs. After the period of trial passes, the day of grace will surely come. This can also be seen in the history of Israel.

Thus, when sorrow comes, we should not simply be sorrowful. If we start with sorrow and end with sorrow, that person's life journey will continue in sorrow. However, if we start with sorrow but manage to end with joy, joy will emerge from there. Moreover, no matter how great the sorrow that comes, if we can digest that sorrow into joy from the beginning, that person can bear the fruit of victory over past and present sorrows. When we face our environment with a joyful heart, the foundation of historical hope will bear fruit there.

Therefore, we should not face the path of sorrow that approaches us with sorrow. Even if we start with sorrow, when the outcome brings joy, tomorrow can bring a joyful beginning before us. If we proceed with a joyful heart from the start to the end, we will become the central subject that can connect joy across the past, present, and future. When we stand in such a position, God cannot help but intervene.
God is not one who only thinks of past victories, nor is He one who merely pledges future victories. He does not want us to disregard past victories in the face of today's reality. Because God seeks to establish the foundation for future victories in the present reality, He urges you not to let that reality be pushed into sorrow. If you stand in a position of joy and appreciation from the beginning and can digest the results with joy, then no matter how great the sorrow you encounter along the way, you can assimilate it into joy and grace. The concrete scope related to this, namely the spiritual world and the past, present, and future centered around oneself, can be harvested as victorious results before Heaven.

Considering these facts, the more obstacles you encounter, the more you can say you are making brilliant progress. After passing through those difficult obstacles, you will reflect on how you overcame them, and those past days will always become a new motivation and a source of encouragement, forming a solid foundation for a hopeful tomorrow, which we frequently experience through our faith life.

Today, you must clearly understand that all the connections in which you advance or retreat are not due to relative conditions, but rather arise from your own subjectivity. Therefore, when Jesus found Himself in a position where He had to bear the cross, He prayed, "My Father, if it is possible, let this cup pass from me; yet not as I will, but as you will." (Matthew 26:39). The center of that prayer was God. In other words, Jesus prayed not centered on Himself, but centered on God.

What path does God take? God seeks to find the path of joy starting from the path of sorrow. Because God began from the day of sorrow, He must always first pass through the path of sorrow in the process of restoration. You must understand God's position in this regard.

In the struggle between good and evil, which side must suffer? It is not evil that must suffer, but good must bear the loss. This is because the path that begins with suffering is the path of good. In other words, because God is in a position of suffering, He must always pass through a sorrowful history and then settle it. However, ultimately, it is the heavenly providence of restoration to eliminate sorrow while looking forward to a moment of joy tomorrow. Nevertheless, if the results do not bring joy and instead manifest as greater sorrow than at the beginning, you must understand that the person who brings about that sorrow cannot rise again. This is the historical process that those responsible for the providence of restoration have gone through.

To comfort the sorrowful God, we must recognize that God did not start with joy but with sorrow. Therefore, it is undoubtedly true that God comes to us not to meet the day of sorrow but to meet the day of joy. If today we start from a sorrowful position and end up with sorrowful results, that would mean we are completely betraying and expelling God right in front of Him. Thus, we must prepare our hearts to welcome God, who comes in sorrow, with joy, no matter what difficulties we face.

If we adopt such an attitude, even if God comes to us in sorrow, at the moment He interacts with us, we can forget that sorrow and establish joyful results. Furthermore, as the standard of joy rises, restoration occurs here. It is in that place of joy that a creative and new history of advancement can begin. God seeks to expand the foundation of providence centered on those who are willing to lay that groundwork and create such an environment. We must understand that this is God's inevitable desire and requirement to bring the providence of restoration to victory.

Today, many people, when walking the path of purpose, pray, "Heaven, please bless me because I am lonely. I am walking a difficult path, so please block this path and lead me to an easier one." However, we must recognize that God is suffering more than anyone else and is enduring greater pain than we are at this moment. Instead, we should stand in a position to say, "Please share Your difficulties with me," and comfort the great pain of God.

If a mother has a beloved son who has died, she will be indescribably sorrowful. At that time, her heart cannot be understood without experiencing a sorrow beyond that. If someone who has experienced less sorrow than that mother tries to comfort her, she cannot be comforted. However, if someone who has endured greater pain than her comforts her by saying, "I have also been through this. In such times, doing this will only lead to loss, so do it this way," then that mother can begin to heal her sorrowful heart. But if another son of that mother, feeling even more sorrow than her, steps forward and says, "If I could take your sorrow upon myself, I would overcome any difficulty," then that mother can find new hope and stand in a position to comfort that son.

Similarly, if God suffers from such a position, we must think about how great God's sorrow is and, with tears, encourage Him not to be too sorrowful. We must stand in a position to comfort God, setting aside our own circumstances. When that happens, God will comfort us even from a place of sorrow.

If there is someone who stands in a position of suffering greater than God and says, "I will take on all responsibilities," dedicating themselves and enduring persecution and suffering as their mission, God will find comfort there and will want to share all His stories with them. This fact can also be understood by looking at the emotional world of humanity, that is, the static world.

Therefore, today, we must always think about how we can comfort the sorrowful God on the path of purpose and have the heart to work harder than God to comfort Him. When that happens, God will instead stand in a position to comfort us, and the God who stands in a position to comfort us will forget His sorrow and treat us with a joyful heart.

When we understand God's sorrow and stand in a position to comfort Him with the heart to take on His sorrow, God will see our state and will instead stand in a position to comfort us. By serving in such a position, that moment may indeed be a moment when God can overcome sorrow and forget it. Considering these facts, you must understand how precious such an attitude is in your faith life.

We must recognize that the time we spend in prayer is not a time for boasting but a time for offering. "God, if You have sorrow, please forgive that sorrow because of me. Moreover, forgive all the sorrows of our church because of me," and if someone resolves to be an offering and seeks that position, then no matter how far they try to distance themselves, God will come to that person. Even if they do not want it, God will surely seek to establish a connection centered on that person. This is because the heavenly work can only advance through such a person, and God cannot help but engage with those who have such a foundation.

To advance in our faith life, we must stand in a position to comfort the sorrowful God. To comfort the sorrowful God, we must not be in a sorrowful position. In a sorrowful position, we cannot comfort a sorrowful God. Therefore, we must always maintain a heart of gratitude. We must not have a heart of complaint or dissatisfaction. For the sake of the purpose, we should be able to be grateful even if we die a million times, and if we can rise again a million times, we should have the mindset that we would die again for the sake of Heaven's purpose. A person with such a heart can represent dozens or even hundreds of people in their lifetime.

If we can look back on the path we have walked with that heart and say that we have lived to comfort God and do what pleases Him, then that person is not truly dead even if they die. They should not only fight in their personal battleground but should expand that heart and fight in the familial battleground. If my individual self fought to embrace my family with such a heart in the past, then I must also embrace my tribe, and then my nation, and the world, and fight.

By expanding the stages of indemnity in this way, the fields in which we can advance can gradually widen in all directions, and through that, we can continue to develop. However, if in dealing with the purpose, today is less than yesterday, and tomorrow is less than today, then that position is undoubtedly one of stagnation and retreat. You must understand this.

Those who retreat are disliked not only by the world but also by God. Behind a person who retreats, Satan always follows, trying to block that person's advancement in every way. Because of that position, that person walks the path of retreat. Therefore, a person who retreats is not in a good position but stands in the position of evil Satan.

In faith life, the times are important. No matter how confidently one practices their faith and vigorously walks the path of purpose, if that time requires them to advance to the next stage of familial providence and take on familial responsibilities, they must adjust accordingly. One cannot push forward into the realm of familial providence with the results of victory from a personal era.

When comparing past faith life with present faith life, even if the forms and realms appear the same, there are differences. In a more advanced era, one must also advance themselves. However, if one stands in the same position as when they were only fulfilling personal missions, they are not advancing but retreating.

For this reason, those walking the path of purpose cannot complain or grumble. They must always bow down and take the position of a sinner who has committed a great sin, taking the position of an offering. This is the sorrowful path of restoration. The indemnity of this sorrowful path of restoration is not completed in any moment today or tomorrow. It must be completed centered on reality, on this very moment. Therefore, we cannot view reality as meaningless. Reality is the crossroads that determines whether we live or die, always threatening our lives. You must clearly understand that this is the reality.

If one becomes a loser in reality, they cannot be a winner in the future. Furthermore, a person who has tasted the sorrow of being a loser in reality cannot claim it as the result of past victories. This is why our greatest enemies may appear in reality, and happiness may also be elusive. The serious question is how we can defeat this enemy and seek the factors of happiness. If one unknowingly falls into the path of retreat after one, two, or three obstacles, it is incredibly difficult to return to the path of advancement. Moreover, when one realizes that their heart is cracked and tries to recover it, it is challenging to do so alone.

For this reason, in walking the path of faith, having a beloved son or leader is an immense blessing. If at that time one asserts their own opinions or views, they will find their path blocked forever. Therefore, if one has a beloved son or daughter, they should share all their stories with them and discuss how they feel and what they think should be done. If there is a teacher, they should honestly share all their stories and consult with their teacher on what they think. Thus, one must seek a second object through which to resolve problems, as it is difficult to do so alone.

In a position of retreat, how can one find the motivation to advance? It should not be sought within oneself but rather through a third object. This is why parents are needed, teachers are needed, and beloved sons and daughters are needed. You must clearly understand this.

When such people are absent, one must negotiate with Heaven. However, when trying to negotiate from a position that has already suffered a blow and retreated, the difficulties that follow will be several times greater than those faced during the time of advancement. You must understand that our path of faith cannot be resolved even with several times the effort.

You must understand how important this moment is. Those who have experienced a life of fighting against the clock know how terrifying an hour can be. Anyone who suddenly appears and speaks can either bring me down or provide the motivation to advance. They know in their hearts whether something can bring joy or sorrow. This is an important issue in today's faith life.

Living such a life does not mean moving carelessly. It revolves around oneself. Therefore, a believer must not be struck by anything. No matter how shocking the words may be, they must not be struck. Even if something occurs that puts them in an unjust position, they must think that it is not meant to ruin them but to uplift them. The more such events occur, the closer the time of their own moment approaches. They must pray with a humble heart and put forth all their effort to overcome that environment.

When Pilate asked Jesus if He was the King of the Jews, Jesus had sufficient content to defend Himself, but He understood the nature of the position He was in and knew that no defense would be accepted there, so He did not defend Himself. If Jesus had opened His mouth incorrectly there, it could have resulted in a lack of faith in Heaven, so He thought coldly about how to create the heavenly lineage.

The stronger the opposition from the surrounding environment, the greater the heavenly lineage grows in proportion. This is why He left behind appropriately necessary words for establishing a historical tradition centered on the purpose. When Jesus answered "Yes" to Pilate's question about being the King of the Jews, that was it.
This content determines historical victories and establishes the center of the era, presenting the direction for the future. If one cannot take responsibility in such a position, the foundation of the normal gospel that Jesus Christ intended to establish cannot be laid. Therefore, what we must always consider is that this time, today, is important.

How lonely and pitiful God is
The time when a leader stands on the platform and delivers a message to a large crowd is a serious moment. When a leader stands to deliver a message, they must think about how to connect people to heaven through the ties of life. That is the leader's responsibility. They must also clearly know whether they have retreated or advanced from that position. If they have retreated but do not conceal it and remain as they are, there will be no way to recover from it. Thus, the seriousness and pitifulness of the path a leader takes is something that those who have not lived such a life cannot understand.

A leader is in a position to be responsible for each individual's life while also being at the forefront of all matters as a pioneer. They are a protector of life and a leader to those in fragile positions. You must understand that a leader stands in a pitiful position, always comparing tomorrow's relative foundation to today's foundation.

If our human leaders are like this, how much more so is God's position, who is responsible for the universe? God knows about the future, but at the same time, as the Father of humanity, He must correspond with the people on earth and decide everything accordingly; otherwise, He cannot advance. Therefore, how anxious must God's heart be as He seeks out one person on this earth?

You must feel how lonely and isolated a leader's life is, and through that, you should be able to sense that God is also lonely and pitiful.

Then when does corruption come? Corruption is not something that came in the past. At any moment, even a small problem that trips me up today can determine my life or death. Corruption does not come all at once like a flood. It begins from a certain motive, seeping in through small gaps, leading to the breakdown of the path of advancement. You must clearly understand that such terrifying things are happening in this reality today, not in the past.

You must recognize that the place where heaven and Satan are both fighting for life and death is reality. If you find yourself in a position where you cannot advance and are retreating in reality, then friends, children, neighbors, and family will all disappear. Therefore, you must establish this foundation correctly, no matter what.

What must be done to become God's eldest daughter? Who must take charge of the church? Must the earth administrator take charge? And to become God's eldest son, must the earth administrator take charge? They must fight to take responsibility for each other. One must have the heart to take on difficult tasks first and be willing to go to the place of death first. If that happens, God will be pleased.

Heaven will surely elevate what is good and bring down what is evil. This is unavoidable. There is movement of rising and falling. Therefore, in the journey of faith, it is extremely important whether one focuses on goodness and continues to advance based on the horizontal line.

When attending church, one must think about whom they are going to meet and what they are going to do. That is the issue. When you go out to advance one step further or to gain something, what must you do? To become a person of greater value than yesterday, your attitude must change from the start.

Thus, you must work from dawn. When coming to church, do not come with a casual mindset, and do not engage in idle chatter. You must devote your intellect to a single purpose. As you take the tram or taxi to church, you will see many people coming and going. At that time, do not just pass by their appearances; you must discern and feel them, absorbing them as materials and nutrients that can be plus factors on your path.

As you walk, you will see all kinds of people. What appears before you is a silent teaching. Therefore, when you see such figures, you must receive more feelings and realizations than from any preacher's sermon. You must understand that all of those things show you your path. And you must reflect on whether you have given your all for the purpose. When you see such things, you must eagerly accept them as materials that can help you advance based on that one moment.
