When you first stand on the platform, you may have felt a sense of anxiety to get there. At times, it may even feel burdensome. Therefore, when that position is a public one, you must think about how much God behind it is anxious. The more you feel your own shortcomings, the more you should try to connect with God's heart that is grieving. When you feel the God who is in a miserable and pitiful position, you can captivate the audience present. No matter how large that gathering is, when you preach with sympathy for God and explode with sorrow or a moved heart centered on God, you can captivate the audience.

However, if you abandon God and try to do it alone, even if you sit in the position of the earth administrator, you will easily fall. This means that you must always live with content that can receive God's cooperation centered on God.

When you pray, saying "Father," it is not merely the words of an individual, such as Kim or Park. God has come and gone through many ancestors who sought to achieve the purpose they desired, and He wants you to pray with a heart that is anxious through the decisive moments they faced. That is God's desire and request. Therefore, you must always think about how you can become a recognized person before such a Father and fulfill your mission. In doing so, you must forget yourself and pray from the original position that can represent heaven. Then, that prayer may come from your mouth, but it is not your prayer. Through prayer, you can receive grace. You must understand that you cannot move others unless you are moved yourself.

The attitude of a faithful person who advances
You must understand how precious the present moment we are in today is. Here, the question is whether you are advancing or stopping. You must not stop. Stopping is absolutely not desired. Stopping occurs in an instant. When climbing a steep slope, if you stop even for a moment, you will roll down without fail. The path of faith is the same. You must always think about this and remain tense. The steps you take while climbing a steep slope are the most precious things that can replace the heavenly principles. It is not easy to take a single step upward. When you cross the seven-tenths, eight-tenths, and nine-tenths of the slope and head toward the summit, you cannot think of anything else. You must climb with a single-minded focus toward the summit. Once you reach the summit, everything in the world becomes yours. All beings that come into your view are embraced in your arms, and all beings that unfold before your eyes establish relative connections with you as the subject. Thus, they joyfully enter as objects of joy and glory before you. In such a place, where you share such joy with God and experience such victory in your life, God cannot help but be present.

For those who have many such moments, God cannot help but be with them. Centered on their historical life, if a person who has a standard of 100 acquires a standard of 200, that person will always be protected by that standard of 200, no matter how corrupted their path may be. When they seek to go to a difficult place and do difficult work, their heart and spirit, that is, their inner self, already knows whether it will succeed or fail.

Before you become a living being, where does that living being grow? It does not grow in the air; it grows in your heart. The spiritual body and the living spirit do not grow in the air; they grow in your heart. Therefore, we have the senses of the living spirit, the senses of the living being, or whatever the spiritual body perceives. Thus, you must use that as a standard to discern whether you are advancing or retreating on the path of purpose. If you cannot discern that, you will come to a stop. The more people there are who stop, the more they become enemies to those who have just come in.

If such a lifestyle and faith attitude become habitual and traditional, even if new people come in who should play significant roles, they will not be able to set an example or provide stimulation before them. Those who came in first must set an example in both lifestyle and faith for the new arrivals and lay the foundation. If they fail to do so, they must understand that they will face severe judgment.

Therefore, we must fight in reality. To advance, you must sense through all your senses, that is, through your five senses, whether you are advancing or retreating. The entirety of the sensations that come through your five senses allows you to know whether whatever you are doing can lead to advancement or retreat.

Thus, what serves as our standard of faith is living a sacrificial life. We must live sacrificially. Therefore, we, who practice faith, cannot boast of ourselves or have a position to boast about if we only meet joyful and happy days. This is because beyond the individual restoration stage, the family restoration stage awaits, and after passing the family restoration stage, the tribal restoration stage awaits. Beyond that, the national restoration stage and the global restoration stage await.

Therefore, we must be able to dedicate our lives before heaven. We must walk the path of the cross, which is heavier in the future than in the past. The attitude of being able to humbly dedicate your entire life from the position of sacrifice becomes a motivation to elevate and advance to a higher stage in the journey of faith. You must clearly understand that without such an attitude, you will inevitably continue down the path of retreat.

Do not be absolutely arrogant; sacrifice for others
You must understand how precious today is. The enemy of today is the most frightening. It is not the enemy of the past that is frightening, nor is it the enemy approaching tomorrow that is frightening. It is the enemy you are facing today that is frightening. You must understand that you are judging each other. Therefore, you must recognize that you are each other's objects of judgment and create motivations to cooperate and develop from that judgment.

The boundary of death and the boundary of life are intertwined around the focal point of this reality. Therefore, the question is whether you will establish a connection with the life-giving or with the death-bringing. In other words, the question is whether you will connect with heaven or with Satan, and this is determined in the reality of the foundation. When you think about this, you must understand that nothing is more frightening than reality.

Those who have made such things a part of their lives can discern whether something is satanic or heavenly. Thus, if it is something that heaven does not want, they will ruthlessly cut it off. There is no need to hesitate at all. Those who cannot do this may appear to be strong on the outside, but in reality, they act oppositely. However, they do not know why they are doing such things. They have no way of knowing. They engage in actions that can fundamentally disrupt God's providence and yet do not understand why they are doing so.

You must throw away all personal glory and fame and stand in the position of Jesus, who hung on the cross saying, "Not my will, but Yours be done." By having the motivation to give up yourself, by throwing yourself away, establish a standard that heaven can sympathize with. That is the only way. The lessons that can be gained through a life of faith can only be resolved on such a foundation, and only on such a resolved foundation can heaven's wishes be fulfilled and the quest for advancement be re-established. When you see this, you must understand how frightening today's reality is.

In the morning, do you ever think about what you will do today? Whatever you think you will do, it must be resolved in your real life. Therefore, you cannot live a single day without worry.

The teacher can tell just from one word whether what the person is about to say is sad or happy. When someone comes to report, they can immediately sense it. If it is sad news, a cold wind rushes by. Whatever it is, it is not normal content. There is a reaction. Isn't that so? The same goes for good news. As soon as they hear the report, they can tell immediately. There is a reaction. Therefore, if you lose in today's reality fight, you cannot advance. You must clearly understand that you will inevitably walk the path of retreat.

However, the time spent being stagnant on the path of faith is not long. When stagnation begins, it indicates that a saturation point is approaching. Saturation means that I can no longer do more than this as myself, and that my influence can no longer extend beyond this. It is at such times that one comes to a stop. At that time, you must be ready to pass on your inheritance. Just as Isaac passed on to Jacob, you must be prepared to inherit.

What appears before you is all about thinking of how to squander it immediately, right? You must have the mindset of a guest who gives away everything they have while blessing others and returns empty-handed. You must have the mindset of a traveler who enters a house with precious things and shares everything before leaving.

Such a person is someone whom heaven can sympathize with. A person who gives away even the portion of their possessions will be sympathized with by heaven. Because such a person has a standard of blessings that they are destined to receive, even if they seem to give everything away and have nothing, heaven will grant them even more blessings at once.
I am. When you share everything you have, you receive even more in return. Ultimately, giving is not a losing business but a profitable one. Therefore, when you reach a saturation point, be prepared to share everything. Even when sharing, you should not hold back anything precious that you possess. You must be able to share all the valuable things you have. Then God will have compassion and sympathy for you. He will replenish the blessings you need to receive. So, in the end, it is not a loss but a gain. That is why you must never be arrogant. You must sacrifice for others.

<Prayer> Beloved Father, can the position of the Unification Church, which is currently in, be remembered before You? When considering whether to stop, advance, or retreat, we are facing inevitable circumstances in the process of our Unification Church's development today. There are matters that cannot be resolved without a life-and-death determination.

Father, we know well that You have cared for this insignificant church and protected this insignificant child until now. Please help us remember how much effort You have put into raising someone as inadequate as me. The more we think about whether we can fulfill this tremendous mission entrusted to us today, the more we realize how weak humans are. However, because humans are weak, we know that Your merciful and compassionate hand is always with us.

The path we are taking is not a path to destruction but a path that can be a source of pride for You and a target for Your meaningful cooperation, which we have realized while pioneering this path until now. We understand how frightening it is to have groups coming out with connections to other subjects. Therefore, whether it is day or night, if You move, we will move, and if You decide, we must also decide. When we think that if we do not absolute this relative position, Your victory cannot be established on this earth, we come to know that this path is indeed a difficult one.

Father, even when we rejoice, we must not rejoice centered on ourselves, but we often find ourselves rejoicing centered on ourselves without realizing it. We should rejoice centered on You, yet today we are being governed by emotions felt through the reality stage. We must become Your sons and daughters who live with a heart of repentance at all times rather than having a separate time of repentance during prayer when we feel our sinful selves.

We know that feeling breathless and tired is not a matter of the past or the future but a matter of the present. We must realize that the motivation to sustain the present lies in our current attitude. Instead of boasting about having something of high value, if we struggle to offer it all before Heaven and share it with all people, we know that we will never fail. We also know that in such a position, we cannot help but advance.

Father, please help the children gathered here to develop a lifestyle and faith attitude that cannot part from Your heart of compassion before they love You.

<Advancement and Stagnation> Father, are we not the descendants of fallen humanity? We know well that it is not easy to indemnify the tremendous efforts You have made over 6,000 years to restore the fallen individuals, families, tribes, nations, and the world. When we think of this, we must realize that the miserable heart of the Father who has woven countless sorrows is connected to our lives, and we must feel the loneliness that cannot be shared with anyone.

Without You, we cannot exist. Because You exist, we can feel our value of existence, and because Your inner heart flows into our hearts, we can pledge for tomorrow for Your hopes. Every time we think of this, we cannot forget Heaven and feel that we cannot live without Heaven. If there are sons and daughters who can feel this path of destiny, they will undoubtedly not fail, as history has shown.

When we look at our pitiful and shabby selves in a position where we have nothing, we realize that we are not even worthy to bow down before You, and tears blur our vision. When we call upon You, we must become Your sons and daughters who cannot freely say "Father," feeling the tangled moments of our lives.

Father, we dislike stagnation and only demand advancement. There must never be a fate of stagnation and retreat before Your will. To avoid the sorrows of tomorrow, we must stand in a position that willingly walks the path of sorrow. We must understand that only in such a position can the victory and advancement of tomorrow begin.

When we feel lonely, if that loneliness is centered on ourselves, we must realize that we are a shameful self that cannot reveal our form to Heaven. Therefore, we must stand as representatives of Heaven, which represents the world's loneliness. Thus, we should be bold against evil but humble and reverent towards Heaven.

We feel that the infinite heart of compassion and sympathy from You flows deeply into our hearts and is connected to our hearts. Gracious Father, when we think of You, who has come with a story that cannot help but cooperate with us, tears blur our vision. Therefore, let us be sons and daughters who realize Your comfort is with us.

May You come and dwell in the heart that has received Your deep and profound voice. May there be many of Your children who can make resolutions and commitments in their hearts upon receiving Your commands and orders.

Father, complicated environments do not help the path of life. We know that the path of life is a lonely and solitary path that must be walked alone. We also understand that if we do not take the commitments made between You and Your sons as the standard of hope for the future, the atmosphere of life will not be recreated.

How heartbroken and sorrowful must You have been to see us with compassion? When we think that You can no longer treat us with a heart of compassion, we feel how many times we have expelled You from our presence. From now on, we earnestly hope and wish to become Your sons and daughters who will not be unfilial like this, but who will struggle to become a source of life and comfort in reality.

Even if we shed tears, we must shed them on behalf of the nation. We must comfort You and worry about Your will from the position of replacing the tears of the nation and the world. If that happens, all people will want to walk the path of those who have shed such tears, they will want to be friends, and they will want to discuss with us.

Father, please take charge of the path that the Unification Church will take in the future. Here, no one is a teacher. We must follow in Your footsteps step by step like children, and we cannot look around because this is the path the Unification Church has walked until now and the path it must walk in the future. Even if the harsh trials and great waves of the environment come crashing down upon us, even if we are swept away by overflowing waves below the calm horizon, we must not lose our position and must prepare a foundation where we can comfort You by embracing You in Your deep embrace. 

We earnestly hope and wish to become sons and daughters who correctly feel that this is our mission. Father, we know that advancing is good, but we must understand that to take one step forward, we must go through the path of struggle that sheds blood and tears and the path of miserable sacrifice. We must also understand that if we love the Unification Church, there has been an unspeakable struggle behind it. Therefore, let us always have a heart of regret before You, our ancestors, and our teachers, and if we have conditions to boast about, let us humbly return them before You and to all people. We earnestly hope and wish to become Your sons and daughters who can directly knock on Your door to connect our current positions with You.

Father, please remember the children who have gathered here today. Let us be able to dedicate this day as a day of joy and victory, and let our understanding become a holy day. We also hope and wish that our lives become holy lives. May the history of Your providence through us become a holy result. We earnestly hope and wish that this nation and this world can be remembered before You and can take responsibility for Your will and mission. With all these words, I earnestly pray in the name of True Parents. Amen.

<Welcoming Tomorrow> <Prayer> It is the last Sunday morning of February. Father, please bless this day. As we welcome the year 1971, we must firmly establish that we must lay the foundation that You have connected to individuals, families, tribes, nations, and the world for the "establishment of the Unification Foundation."

To lay that foundation, there must be a clear goal, and we must understand that we must create the foundation of the object centered on that goal.

Father! We must sincerely accept Your holy will. Even if countless people spend their lives, Your will must be fulfilled, and if the historical sorrow that You had to walk through is the greatest desire, we must fulfill that one wish. No matter what sacrifices may follow, whether through individuals, nations, or the world, we must pay the price of sacrifice to achieve Your will.

The children gathered here must become those who, before pledging for their own victory tomorrow, are concerned that there should be no sorrow in Your heart depicted in the path of Your will.

Every time we welcome a new day, when the morning sunlight shines upon us anew, we must hope that it becomes a new day centered on Your will, and we must become those who can long for Your hopeful will like bright sunlight. We know that there should not be any gap between You and us in our daily lives.

The path You walk is the path we must also walk, the place where You stay is where we must also stay, the place where You fight is where we must also fight, and the place where You confront the enemy is where we must also confront the enemy. We must realize this as we go forward.

Father! How many times have we called You "Father" with our words? How much have we truly longed for You in the true sense, and how many times have we become children who have truly bowed before You, who have become unforgettable in the path of Your will, and who have stood in a position where You can command us with all Your hopes and wishes?

The position You require is one where You earnestly wish to connect with us and pursue a historical mission, yet we are foolish humans who wish to discuss with You while living a Cain-like life centered on our personal desires.

Father! At this time, please come to this place. Although the historical ancestors who have gone forth for the path of Your will walked a painful path, they could not raise the flag of victory in the final battlefield and failed to accompany You. When we think of this, we must clearly understand whether we will become victorious sons today or unfilial children who add sorrow to You with the bitterness of defeat.

Father, we are nothing, yet we have bowed before You. When You look upon us, we should be in a position that brings You joy and allows You to command us, but we have not been able to do so. Please forgive us.

Father, today is the last day of the second month of the year 1971. We must not let this year pass without doing anything. Whether it is day or night, if we do not have a place where we shed tears and shed blood with You, and if we do not have many opportunities to participate with You, we cannot connect much with Your will, and without going through the process of pledging our lives before Your will, we cannot establish a heart connection with You. We have often sought out comfortable positions for ourselves and thought centered on ourselves, but we have not stood in a position where You can rest. We earnestly hope and wish that You will forgive us for not being able to establish the standard of life while relying on You.

The few children who are bowed down here must know where they are going and where they are staying. They must ask themselves whether they are in the right posture centered on the attitude of moving towards tomorrow, and whether they are standing in a position where they can take responsibility while facing the East like You. They must know where the environment You are passing through is going and whether they are standing in a position to participate in that environment. If they are not in that position, they must realize that they need to follow again with a sense of urgency.

The path of life is not a path that is walked because someone advises you, nor is it a path that is walked because someone leads you. We must especially understand that we cannot go without taking responsibility ourselves. When we are hungry, we must eat ourselves, when we are thirsty, we must drink ourselves, and when we are lonely, we must stand in a subjective position to find comfort.

We must realize that this is the natural principle. We must know that in our lives, we must stand in the position of the subject. We must not stand in a passive position, and we earnestly hope and wish to become Your sons and daughters who can make resolutions and exert the power of life.

At this time, we have honestly bowed before You, and may You look upon us.
When we look upon the gods, if we are in a wicked place, may we be whipped, and if we are in a good place, may You hold our hands so that we may greet tomorrow with the hope of tomorrow's meaning, appearing as sons and daughters. Therefore, I earnestly ask and desire that You allow us to inherit Your battlefield, taking full responsibility for all conditions that hinder Your will, so that we may become sons and daughters who can pioneer a place of loyalty and devotion that You can trust.

This morning, I earnestly hope and wish that You bless the children gathered in Your name, and that You be with Your sons and daughters scattered across the nation. Please bless the beloved daughters who are out in the provinces. Whenever they take steps to defend against what comes from all directions with all their sincerity, may they align with Your heart and become daughters who can stand by Your side, sensing Your sorrowful heart.

As Your children living in a world that can easily become complacent, I earnestly hope and wish that You allow us to be a group that can take responsibility with enthusiasm before Your will. Grant them strength this morning. May Your hand of power be with them so that they can fulfill their entrusted responsibilities. Make them strong and courageous against the wicked. Center them on goodness and establish a firm position. May they know that without You, they cannot make any decisions or move forward, and may they become Your daughters who rely solely on You.

Please bless Your sons as well. They will be proud sons who do not lose to Your daughters, so I earnestly hope and wish that You remember them and bind their hearts and lives together, blessing them so that they can align with the foundation of hope that brings joy to heaven.

This morning, please be with the countless children around the world who are praying towards this place. For the hope of the future nation and the world of unification, I earnestly ask and wish that You allow us to be Your sons and daughters who can fight vigorously with confidence. I earnestly hope that You take charge of everything this morning. Today is a day to hold a special gathering, so Father, I earnestly hope and wish that You be with us.

Over the course of today and tomorrow, I will be delivering messages to many professors at the university, so I earnestly hope that many of Your children will appear, able to open a new era and welcome a new period according to Your providence. Thus, may they be able to create an important opportunity to pioneer a new path on behalf of the nation's hope, the future of this country, and the direction the world can go, Father, I earnestly ask and wish for Your guidance, protection, mercy, and interest to be with the entire gathering.

As we welcome March tomorrow, may it be a holy time to reaffirm our positions in preparation for the coming month. I earnestly ask and wish for this, and I offer all these words in the name of the True Parents. Amen.

<Words> We are spending days connecting our daily lives. As one day passes, tomorrow comes, and as tomorrow passes, the day after comes again. If we spend each day meaningfully, we know that the hopeful tomorrow will come. If today can correspond with tomorrow and both can align, that will be the absolute foundation for seeking such a tomorrow.

The relationship between yesterday, today, and tomorrow
Knowing that today serves as the foundation for tomorrow, we look towards a future that can be better than the present, pursuing more valuable content for the future than what we have now. However, tomorrow is still in an undecided state as it stands apart from today. Who will move what is in this undecided state to a decided state? This is not something a third party can do; it must be decided by the current self.

Therefore, if we do not firmly establish our position at this point today, securing a foundation in our daily lives that relates to tomorrow, tomorrow will remain a place unrelated to us. Thus, we must live with hope. To realize that hope, there must be a plan that can align with that hope in our daily lives.

However, no matter how much we have a plan that can align with that hope and how conducive our living environment may be, it must not pass by without substance. The desire to achieve that hope must surely rise within my heart. Tomorrow appears as a dream, as a treasure, within my daily life. Dreams can serve as conditions for us humans to fulfill our hopes, but conversely, if those good dreams do not come true, they can bring despair and disappointment, which we have often felt in our lives.

When we look at ourselves here today, the question is how much we are living a life that can sustain tomorrow throughout the process of going from morning to night, through the 24 hours of the day. Today, we have welcomed the last day of February 1971. We have already passed January and February this year. During these two months, we must reflect once again on how much we have lived with enthusiasm centered around the hope of tomorrow. If we lived yesterday and today without any difference, we will not have anything that can differentiate today from tomorrow. Such a person cannot be considered to have developed.

When we look at the relationship between yesterday and today, and today and tomorrow, the greater the daily development and change, the closer success comes to that person. The more effort is made, the more time is shortened and approaches. However, when we live without any difference between yesterday and today, the goal of "securing a foundation for unification," which we resolved at the beginning of 1971, remains as a goal, and I remain as I am, unable to relate to that meaning.

To relate to meaning, today must serve as the foundation for tomorrow, and tomorrow must secure the foundation that can be a friend of today. The question is how to secure this. For that, today must be more enthusiastic than yesterday, and tomorrow must be more enthusiastic than today. To do this, we must be filled with enthusiasm centered around a certain purpose. However, conversely, if we become complacent, we must recognize that achieving the hope of tomorrow and welcoming its true form becomes an unforgivable enemy.

To engage in true faith with more enthusiasm tomorrow than today, the question is how to enhance worthwhile time. To be in such a position as one who welcomes tomorrow is valid; if not, then we must understand that tomorrow will become unrelated to us.

What we need to live today
As those who engage in faith, we are always going through a continuous struggle. Struggle is a war of attrition. We must inevitably expend something. Whether in external material aspects or internal aspects, struggle requires some form of expenditure. The question is what we will use to recover what is expended in this process. In this process, something is inevitably expended, whether in external material conditions or internal spiritual conditions. When something is expended, it diminishes compared to yesterday. Therefore, to stand in a position today that can be better than tomorrow, we must intensify a continuous second struggle to replenish what has been expended. If we do not overcome this pit of expenditure, a better tomorrow cannot follow. If that happens, we will find ourselves in a place of unwanted results, which we often feel in our lives or in our living environments.

Thus, we must establish the groundwork for tomorrow centered on today’s work. Also, we must understand that we need to study how to enhance our more enthusiastic posture while spending today.

Just because we ate breakfast does not mean we skip lunch and dinner. Even if we had breakfast, we must replenish at lunch, and even if we had lunch, we must replenish again at dinner to carry on the day of tomorrow. Our faith life is the same. In continuing our daily lives or in nurturing the enthusiasm to achieve our goals, the question is how to avoid complacency. In other words, just as we eat to avoid hunger, complacency cannot be a hindrance when we are always centered on enthusiasm to fulfill tomorrow's purpose.

How to enhance our enthusiastic posture at every moment is the most important thing for us living today and tomorrow. If you cannot stand in a position that can enhance that enthusiasm, then you cannot enhance it from that position. When you cannot stand in a subjective position that can lead the enthusiastic standards of the past, present, and future, how to maintain and secure that subjective position becomes an extremely important issue. If you cannot stand in a subjective position, you must choose either a relative position or one of the two.

Additionally, in looking forward to tomorrow, we must always examine who among the members of the Unification Church, who live centered on the purpose today, stands in a subjective position. If I cannot stand in a subjective position, I must definitely stand in a relative position and align with the environment and direction where the subject moves. That is the issue. To align, we must establish a position that can relate to the environment through which the subject moves, in harmony with the direction the subject is moving.

If we cannot directly relate to the subject, we must increase the degree of our relationship according to the actions and directions the subject aims for. The important question here is how to do that.

Currently, the Unification Church is promoting women over men in its direction. Therefore, we must recognize that women are in a subjective position, leading the entire Unification Church, while men are not.

Thus, we should not stand in a position opposing those who are at the forefront but rather stand in a position that corresponds with those who are in a subjective position, becoming the object before the subject and taking the same steps as the subject. Otherwise, you must understand that we cannot inherit and develop a new enthusiastic environment centered on the relationship between the subject and the object.

To overcome reality
If you cannot form this foundation within yourself, you will neither be a subject nor an object, and the question becomes what to do. If you stand in a position where you cannot approach a subjective position and cannot enter a position of the object, you will inevitably find yourself in a complacent position. You may experience this every day in your faith life and daily life.

If you find yourself in such a position, what will you do? You must discern whether your past or present is the subject based on your past and present. If the past and present are not formed in the relationship of subject and object, you must take the future as the subject of hope. However, if you are in a complacent position where you cannot serve the hope of the future as a subject, you must understand that you can only take the past as the subject and the present as the object.

Thus, in our faith life, we must not let the grace we received in the past flow away. As we walk the path of faith, we inevitably encounter complacency. At such times, we must think about how to manage the current reality by taking our past faith life as a subject.

You should revisit the diaries you wrote during the time you experienced grace or recall what you experienced in prayer, reviving those feelings from back then. By repeating what you did at that time, you must resolve to be in a more stimulating position than before. The degree may be lower, but you must delve deeply into that feeling again and struggle with how to reproduce that experience in your body; otherwise, you must understand that there is no way to resolve the complacent position you find yourself in today.

In dealing with the purpose, there will be a subject representing the entire church, a subject in the aspect of truth. If you cannot align with the relative relationship that can match the subject, what will happen? When comparing your past life with your current life, if the past is better than today, you must reproduce that past life in your current life. The question becomes how to seek that resolution you had back then, how to feel again what you felt at that time, and how to recreate the environment you were fighting in back then. You must understand that this is the issue. If this cannot be resolved through your own prayer, you must find a way to resolve it in your actions.

As we walk this path of purpose, we can easily become isolated from the church. When considering the church and myself, there are times when I am not within the church but rather living a church life centered on myself. If I do not become the self before the church centered on the whole church and instead stand in a third-party position isolated from the church, I will distance myself from the church and lose interest in it. There is no stimulation. If that happens, the relationship between the church and myself will gradually weaken. Consequently, I will inevitably fall into a position where church life becomes complacent. When thinking from this position, the question becomes what to do this year, so you must act subjectively on behalf of the entire church, ensuring that you do not isolate yourself in that activity. Do not stand in an isolated position; rather, align with the subject and move forward together. When you fight while taking steps together, you will be able to discern the environment that those at the forefront feel, adopt, and are enthusiastic about.

Then, you will not only follow those who are moving from a subjective position representing the church but also stand in a position where you can lead ahead of them. When that happens, you will be in a position to establish the time of heaven, and God will surely establish a relationship with you. When you stand at the forefront, there will be no despair or complacency.

If you have found yourself in a complacent position compared to the past, how will you escape from that position? You know well the faith experiences you had back then. How earnest was my heart at that time? What was my heart like when I thought of the headquarters? Centered on the teacher, how did I serve heaven? You must discern your state based on these reflections.
must be established on the foundation of the past. You must recognize that without embodying your past in your actions and daily life, you cannot revive the gracious position of the past in front of yourself. If you find yourself in a lax position, you must consciously or intentionally break free from it. You need to set conditions that are better than the past. If you used to visit the headquarters church once a day, now you should go at least twice. If you used to receive grace through prayer, and now you feel that grace is lacking, then you should increase your prayer time from 10 minutes to 20, 30, or even an hour.

No matter what, you must revive the heart you had at that time and transfer those feelings to today, so that they can be inherited as a foundation for the future. If the past and present are disconnected, God cannot provide new purposes, hopes, or motivations, nor can He extend His grace directly. This is a natural principle.

Therefore, if you have a heart that is deeply moved by grace, even more than anyone else, you must seek out a lonely place for that purpose. If you have experienced injustice more than anyone else, you must not lose that experience. If you have experienced joy, you need to revive that joyful heart, and if you have experienced sadness, you must not go to a place of greater sadness without receiving greater grace than before.

In faith, what you need to be cautious about is the position from which you started your faith journey. Some may have started when they were sad, while others may have started in loneliness or joy, during despair, when discussing with someone, serving someone, or standing on the front lines for a cause. Each person has their own unique starting point.

You need to recall when you experienced grace during your faith journey. You must take responsibility before others and act with the dignity of a responsible person in mind. You must go out to the most difficult places and even if you are pushed to a position of injustice, you must be able to overcome it. The place you are pushed into is not one that brings tomorrow's sadness; rather, it is a place of grace that can amplify tomorrow's new blessings.

You must understand the true meaning of "you reap what you sow." If you start sowing with sorrow, you will reap with sorrow. If you start with the cross, you must reap with the cross. You cannot sow with the cross and expect to reap joy. There is no way to sow with the cross and reap joy.

If you have sown with the cross, you must first reap with the cross and then rejoice. Seeds sown with joy must be reaped with joy and then go back to the path of the cross. In other words, if you sowed with sorrow, you must reap with sorrow and then go towards joy. If you sowed with joy, you might think you will reap with joy and go towards joy, but that is not the case. If you sowed with joy, you must reap with joy and then face sorrow.

Look at the history of Israel. After grace, there was always a trial. When there is a trial, there is always grace. A trial does not start with a trial and end with a trial. The greater the grace that is to come, the longer the period of trial is not shorter, but proportionately, there is a period of trial that matches the grace. The greater the grace, the longer the trial period. Only after overcoming this trial period can you reach the time of grace that brings joy.

This is a natural phenomenon. Just as morning comes after night and day comes after evening, nature continues to maintain itself through relationships of give and take, either vertically or horizontally. It is a principle that if something has risen, it must fall. Just because something was good does not mean it will end well. After reaping something good, you must face sorrow before a foundation can be established.

In laying the foundation, it does not happen easily. Difficulties follow. To lay a foundation, you must overcome difficulties. Only when there are desires left beyond the difficulties can you remain as an existence on that difficult foundation; otherwise, a foundation cannot be formed.

Similarly, in our faith life today, you must understand that you reap what you sow. If there is a husband who opposes your faith, the degree of opposition may intensify, but that does not mean the wife's faith will weaken. When faith starts in persecution, it does not weaken when the opposition is severe; rather, it is when the opposing party begins to understand that faith may weaken.

In cases where there is no opposition, nine out of ten will easily weaken. Where is the enemy? When opposition is severe, it is not the case that enemies arise in the position of strengthening one's will to prepare for it; rather, enemies arise after a foundation is established where one can rest in the fulfillment of their purpose. You must understand that when you are on such a foundation, the enemy will attack.

Therefore, those who start their faith life with tears must reap with tears. If you started with the cross, you must reap with the cross. To what extent should you inherit that? Those who started on the personal path of the cross must inherit the family path of the cross. Those who have walked the family path of the cross must inherit the tribal, national, and global paths of the cross.

Humans must walk the path of the cross that has been intensified. If you started with the cross, you must inherit with the cross. If you started with grace, you must inherit with grace. What does this mean? In the past, during the personal providential era, if one walked the path of suffering of the cross but did not fulfill their purpose and fell, to inherit that, one must go beyond the position of the suffering of the cross at that time.

Just as personal missions are like that, so are family missions. The same goes for tribal, national, and global missions. There must be personal indemnity, then family indemnity, then tribal indemnity, then national indemnity, and finally global indemnity.

This is the path of sorrowful restoration. If you do not connect this, can you develop from the individual to the world? Without a new resolution to be made in the path of intensified cross, in other words, without being stronger than before, more confident in front of the purpose, and more passionate in front of God, a group that can take responsibility for the era cannot emerge, and you must understand that it is normal that this path of indemnity cannot be developed.

Today, the problem is that members of the Unification Church acknowledge their own laxity but cannot enter the same faith path as the past. The starting point of our Unification Church is sown with the cross. Therefore, you must reap with the personal cross to meet a day of personal victory. However, just because you have met a day of personal victory does not mean it ends there.

After achieving personal victory, you must leave the second path of the cross. From then on, you must start the path of the family cross. Personal victory becomes a foundation for the family path. What acted as strength for me in the personal path of the cross becomes the nourishment for advancing the family path of the cross. The joy found in this way does not end with my personal joy; rather, it becomes the most precious thing that cannot be lived without giving something to me, and you must remember this fact deeply in your heart. You must build pillars on that foundation stored deep in your heart. If you do not stand on that foundation, it is like cutting off the branches of the grace you received in the past. If you ignore this and do not stand on that foundation, it will surely collapse. Even if you have started the path of the family cross, if you do not repeat the foundation of victory of the personal cross, you must do so.

The joy of the fruits obtained in the personal path of the cross must be guaranteed as eternal joy. You must firmly stand on the foundation that solidifies that. The broader the family field, the larger the corresponding cross will be. You must overcome this.

If you have won in the family cross, the result of that victory will surely be joy centered on the family. This is because God is with that family. The sons and daughters of that family who have gone through such a process will surely advance with heavenly fortune. However, just because there is family joy does not mean it ends with family joy. If you settle for that and remain in a place of rest, a place of laxity, that family will come to an end.

There is a mission required by the purpose that must go through the path of the tribal cross, and even if the grace permitted by God at the family level is great, you must not settle there.

No matter how much victory you have achieved at the family level, do not let it end with family victory; it must connect to a higher level of tribal victory. However, if you remain on the foundation of family grace, you cannot connect to the time of the tribe and cannot move towards the time of the nation. If that happens, you will lose your way. If you wander here and retreat, you must understand that no matter how much the purpose develops, it will have no relation to the purpose. If you cannot establish that relationship, you will inevitably become lax.

You cannot develop because you do not have a lifeline with heaven. You cannot grow. If you cannot grow, you will retreat. The path of indemnity and restoration is to expand the scope of the path of the intensified cross centered on God's will. In expanding the scope, it is not done carelessly. You must go through the personal path of indemnity, family path of indemnity, tribal path of indemnity, national path of indemnity, and global path of indemnity. In this path, the range of the environment differs. There is a difference between the personal and national aspects. However, while the difference between the time of family providence and the time of national providence is vast, the content is the same. The content is determined by the relationship between me and family issues, me and the expectations of my in-laws. Although the scope and position may differ, the content is the same.

The path of intensified indemnity can only be traversed as one. So which is harder to overcome, the personal path of the cross or the family path of the cross? While the scope of the family is broader, it is more difficult to overcome the personal path. If you have a foundation of personal victory, overcoming the family standard becomes easier. In the case of family, since it has escaped the realm of personal satanic accusations, it is not directed at the individual. This is because it is a content experienced in the individual era, so it can be managed. It can be managed. Therefore, it is more difficult to overcome the personal path of indemnity.

When comparing the family path of indemnity and the tribal path of indemnity, while there is a vast difference in scope and position, in content, the tribal path is easier than the family path. If you unite around parents in the family and achieve the expectations of your in-laws, you can overcome it. If you pray for the nation and strive to overcome it, you can surpass the time of tribal providence.

Therefore, even if the family is in a difficult environment, if you hold onto the subject from the perspective of the family and overcome difficulties, you can surpass it because you are already on the expectations of your in-laws. There are times when my emotions become intense, but whose emotions are they? Are they the emotions of someone in the Unification Church? They are the emotions of heaven, the emotions of humanity, the emotions of the nation. We must run even if the swords of countless enemies block our way. This is the unification thought. I am the one who proclaimed the unification thought. It is natural for district leaders and regional leaders to live hard. We must go hungry because we have not fulfilled our responsibility to the nation. That is the way to live.

Even after liberation, true patriots had no words. Those who have a heart for the nation, who do not want to tarnish that heart, and who do not avoid lonely places, are those who have lived lonely lives both inside and outside. At first, they were patriotic, but as time went on, those who became sycophants pretended to be patriots.

To greet tomorrow, we must unite and fight. You must know this and inherit tomorrow. Let us greet tomorrow! Am I creating an environment that can greet tomorrow? The question is how I lived in the past and whether I have a solid foundation in the present. Therefore, this year, we have set the slogan "Securing a Unification Foundation." First, we must unite body and mind. In the past, we only wished for it, but now we must unite body and mind. Men and women must become one, and the in-laws must become one. Families must unite around the center. Furthermore, tribes must unite around the center of the family. In that unification, we must center around those who can act joyfully and hope for good actions; otherwise, we will never unite. We must center around those who sacrifice, who shed blood and tears for the sake of many on the path of the cross.

You must understand this. You will reap what you sow. The Unification Church has sown in persecution, so it will reap in persecution. Therefore, do not rejoice just because there is joy. You must turn that joy into God's joy first, and after God rejoices, then you can rejoice. When this happens, you will inherit more than the current joy, beyond the joy that heaven rejoices in.

That is why you must always be sensitive to the sense of the times. You must be sensitive to the situation. We must prepare an environment that can greet tomorrow centered around these issues. That tomorrow cannot exist apart from the present and the past. Tomorrow must be connected to the present and the past.

In the midst of fighting for the restoration of individuals, families, tribes, and nations, you must recognize that although my family is like this, there are families like that. Although I am like this, there are individuals like that. Centered around a universal family that represents all humanity, I must have a heart of gratitude, anchoring myself as a branch, and I must go forth centered on the tremendous purpose of restoring the nation, the state, and the world that heaven desires. If we go that way, no matter how difficult the position, heaven will be with us.

Therefore, when you pray to God, do not pray trivial prayers like, "Father! I am in such a difficult position, so please be with me." Only those who can bear the trials and pains for the nation and the state, and who have a strong character and a strong heart to overcome them, can become representatives and successors for heaven. You must become an individual who can leave behind loyalty and filial piety. That is the issue.

What good is it to receive a reward? Rewards in the process are unnecessary. What good is it to receive praise? Praise in the process is unnecessary. You must receive praise at the very end. In fact, praise received in the process can ruin you.

In that sense, the path of the Unification Church is increasingly the path of the cross, and although it is becoming a more difficult path, it is a rewarding path for the Unification Church and its leader. It is not a path of retreat but a rewarding path. Because we have fought that way in the past, we continue to go that way now. The words of the teacher can present issues that surpass those spoken by any world politician. The results of the teacher's actions can become the driving force that influences the world situation. We go with that conviction.

When you listen to the teacher's words, they may seem tremendous, but God creates an environment where you can act. By doing so, the world is changing. It is not politicians or historians who change history. Historians only record history, and writers only record social environments. It is heaven that develops the emotional world. In that sense, we feel rewarded.

To recover your lax self, the way to do so is to sense the subjective and mainstream direction of the Unification Church and align yourself with it. And if there is a subject who stands at the forefront, you must have a stronger conviction than that person. Then you will not need to pray. You will not need to say, "God, help me." If you are in that position, God will help you without you having to pray. If you cannot be in that position, you cannot go alone. It is heaven and earth, right? It cannot be done with just people. There must be heaven and earth for there to be people.

Therefore, if there is no counterpart or subject, there is no joy. Isn't it a principle that strength comes from the relationship between subject and object? That is why you must act with the will as the subject and from the position of the object. If not, it means that you should act according to the commands from the position of the teacher as the subject. It is simple.

If that is difficult, when you start on the path of the will, think about when God has given you grace, and when heaven has saved you. So, you must go down to a position more miserable than that one. If you go down, heaven will help you. To put it in feminine terms, if you are chased out by your husband in the middle of winter with your hair cut and barefoot, stamping your feet on the snow and calling out to heaven in despair, if you cannot forget that grace, then you must go down to a position even greater than that. Even if it means being chased out for the day of liberation of this nation and this people, even if it means being imprisoned, those who can be grateful for that position will not perish.

Grace is like that. You reap what you sow. Since it started with the cross, it must be reaped with the cross. If you have feelings of longing for someone, you must long for them until the end. If you do so, the time will come when you will bear fruit. Therefore, you must overcome that critical moment. <Words> As you all know, today is March 1st. Fifty-five years ago on this day, our nation rose up in the midst of unforgettable oppression from Japanese colonial rule, seeking a new liberation or independence. When persecution and suffering are viewed as fate, they are sad and miserable at that time, but when a point of overcoming that persecution and suffering is established, all the content and results of that overcoming can become a source of power that can resonate within that nation and historical era, or can become an object of remembrance. We can see through historical events that the suffering and hardships endured at that time established the origin for that nation to become a nation of ideals.

In this light, the March 1st Movement was truly an unforgettable spiritual moment for our people, serving as a turning point for the nation to advance toward a new ideal and to embark on a new beginning. Now, when we consider whether there has been a similar nationwide uprising centered on heaven in the providence of restoration, we must acknowledge that such an event has not occurred. Even in the history of Christianity, while Christians have always been in positions of persecution and oppression, there have not been many times in Christian history when the entire body was mobilized to overthrow satanic nations.

From this perspective, we feel that our church has a responsibility to undertake a significant mission before many nations of the world and before the overall providential will of God, similar to the March 1st Movement. Therefore, we must once again reflect on the fact that the path the Unification Church must take in the future will inevitably involve struggle and overcoming.

Currently, our country is divided into North and South. The boundary line of the 38th parallel is an obstacle blocking the path our nation must take in the future, and this is no small matter. We cannot overcome this with the attitudes and ways of life we have lived since liberation. As time goes on, North Korea is strengthening its military capabilities and targeting South Korea. In this situation, we realize that we cannot overcome the difficult national fate unless we have a stronger spiritual unity and a stronger fighting spirit.

This is not something that can be resolved solely by our nation’s hope. We cannot push back the united communist states, which are armed with powerful communist ideology and are ideologically unified, without having a stronger spiritual unity and content than they do. We also know that South Korea cannot overcome this alone.

From this perspective, we must recognize that this nation should not remain in a position of the Republic of Korea alone, but rather how to connect the Republic of Korea with the Asian empire and the world is the issue. Considering that the United States, which is leading democracy, is currently retreating from Korea, we cannot overlook the urgent situation our Republic of Korea is in.

In this environment, we know that there is no organization other than our church that has the posture to protect this nation or to develop a new national spirit and establish a new foundation to enhance our capabilities.

From this perspective, we must unite as members of the Unification Church. Whether it is a great crisis or trial, when we face this trial, we must decide whether we will retreat or fight to overcome it. We must align ourselves with the providential will in the future. We must recognize that there is a significant mission that we must fulfill.

Today, you must understand the meaning of celebrating March 1st and must overcome this crisis. To overcome this crisis, we must have a mental posture that can support our ability to overcome, and we must be filled with the conviction that we can overcome any trials that may come our way.

In this sense, even if an individual overcomes a trial alone, it cannot change the fate of the nation. Evangelism and Devotion
Upon returning this time, we must quickly strengthen the principle study group centered around the professors who came to Seoul. Next time, we plan to invite only those who are deans or above. If possible, try to do it in the local community. Try it once in Busan.

Effective Evangelism Methods
From now on, we will have no choice but to evangelize. If we focus on the evangelism team for just one year, I believe the number of members will increase significantly. Then, among them, the young women will team up with young women, and the young men with young men, forming teams of ten to create revival teams to be deployed nationwide.

The wives of the evangelism team members will return home after two years. Therefore, we must prepare successors for those positions from now on. Each church must not simply remain idle just because the wives have returned. We must always have ten people stationed to carry out evangelism activities. Then, naturally, the number of members will increase. That is the only way to increase the number of members.

If we carry out activities centered around the mobilization team, it will not cost much and can be done anytime. If we have over a hundred, it will be quite easy. We must prepare for that in the future. The headquarters must do the same. District leaders must manage the team members and visit the families of members to conduct evangelism. If we maintain communication among members while doing such activities, we can achieve a double effect.

Established churches have systems like elder systems, deacon systems, and district systems. There are also evangelism teams that build relationships and conduct evangelism activities through visits. There are always people who support a pastor's plans from below.

However, our church does not have such systems. When people come, they are only given principle lectures, but that is not enough. We must create detailed organizations so that all personnel can be managed from the central level down to the detailed staff. New members cannot engage in activities if they do not understand the church's content. Therefore, to convince them, we must have many personal interactions. Since the responsible individuals cannot do such work, we need someone who can substitute for them.

If there are ten mobilization team members, each of them should receive contact information about who the new members are and immediately visit them, connecting them with their relatives. This is the fastest way to evangelize. Evangelizing on the street or meeting individuals is not as effective as evangelizing through relatives or friends.

Why is that? Because they are friends, they know what kind of person the other is. Therefore, they believe, "If that person is going there, it must be right," and they follow with 100% trust. They know that they will not be led to a bad place because they care for each other and trust each other.

However, if we go out to evangelize individually, it is different. Can we trust everyone just because they are Unification Church members? We cannot. Even if they acknowledge that the principle teachings are good, it takes more than a year and a half for them to believe and follow. To build a personal relationship with someone, it takes more than three months. Only after frequently visiting their home and nurturing their faith can we finally say, "The truth is good, and the person is good, so let’s give it a try." However, among friends or relatives, since the connection is already established, just giving a lecture can quickly turn them into members. Therefore, evangelizing centered around relatives or friends is the fastest method.

Daily Evangelism
So how should the evangelism team members evangelize? Instead of wandering aimlessly every day, if they visit a hundred homes, they should select ten homes from those and then choose one home to focus on delivering the message. Aim to evangelize one person a month. If you manage to evangelize one person in a month, it is undoubtedly true that that person has devoted themselves and worked hard during that month.

Once that one person is evangelized, the next step is to tell that person, "You should also put in the same effort to evangelize your relatives as I did with you." Establishing such a tradition and guiding them will surely yield results. If we proceed with a uniform method of evangelizing one person each month, horizontal evangelism will unfold from one person to the next, leading to an unlimited increase in members.

For example, if the parents have not been attending church and the father starts attending, the mother will automatically come as well. And when the parents attend, the children will naturally follow. If the mother is firmly rooted in our ideology, relatives will naturally be evangelized. Thus, expanding the central foundation while evangelizing is the fastest method.

The evangelism team members currently out there must not wander aimlessly. If they focus on three homes over the course of a month and visit those three homes to deliver the message, they will likely be able to evangelize one person among them. Alternatively, they can select three homes as a standard from among a hundred and visit them. If they cannot go every day, they should make sure to visit those homes when they return. By putting in that effort, a heartfelt bond will be formed where they will wait for you and want to see you if you do not go. Therefore, the first person is crucial. You should devote the utmost effort to that one person for three years. If that person is evangelized, you will reap results threefold or more.

Devotion is not something that is put in all at once. Even when preaching, do not think of preaching to a crowd; think of preaching to one person. If one person receives grace and sheds tears, that will spread to the whole group. The reason district leaders or regional leaders have not been able to develop the church until now is that they have been preaching without roots, floating in the air. If there is no foundation to absorb, how can there be evangelism? District leaders must also clean their own foundations. When the teacher gives a directive, the district leaders must show an example of moving with their lives on the line, and only then will the general members also move.

When evangelizing centered around a month, even if you face a hundred people over the course of a month,
Through which person will the fruits of harvest be realized? You must choose one person and invest your sincerity to bear fruit. Only then can you set the conditions for evangelism, even if the other ninety-nine fall away. You must establish such a strategy for evangelism; you cannot afford to go a month without converting even one person. It is absurd for those responsible for evangelism, who should be doing it daily, to fail to convert even one person in a month. This is because they did not invest their sincerity.

Evangelism team members should not think that their activities are over just because they have visited every household in a region divided into east, west, south, and north. They should rotate regions and visit again. Each person has a different personality, background, ancestry, and current feelings, so just because person A was rejected at a house does not mean person B will be rejected there as well. Even if A was rejected, B might be welcomed.

District leaders say there are no places left to evangelize, but that should not be the case. If you think there are no places to evangelize, it means the evangelistic strategy was poorly devised. 

Once the groups have gone around, the next step should be for individuals to visit the entire town. If they visit more than three times, they will roughly understand the circumstances of the townspeople. From there, classify the people into those to visit in a week, a month, three months, or six months, and develop a long-term evangelism plan. You must not lose heart just because it does not happen at once. If you do it this way, why would there be no places to visit?

You must understand people well in advance. Identify those who need to be visited daily, those to visit in a week, in two months, or those you might stop by for a drink when passing by, and categorize them in various ways to evangelize while uplifting your spirits.

By doing this, you should narrow down twenty people to ten, and then from those ten, select three to bear fruit. Then why would evangelism not succeed? If you focus on the person you want to evangelize and invest your sincerity morning and night, they will naturally be drawn in. Even after going out for evangelism, if you pray, your ancestors will surely get involved.

We must utilize this multidimensional background to strategize and engage in the battle. Just as in battle we need artillery fire, rifle fire, and cover fire, evangelism is the same. How enjoyable would it be to evangelize in a spiritual atmosphere where our ancestors are mobilized, backed by a multidimensional spiritual realm?

Do not think about evangelizing ten people at once; instead, plan to evangelize one person at a time. Through that person, draw in their friends. Provide only the principle lecture to that friend, and then let the evangelized friend take charge of guiding them. One must nurture their family to become a person.

By delegating the tasks they were doing in detail and expanding their responsibilities, the number of family members will naturally increase. However, if our family members are just hanging in the air like pine cones, how can leaves or roots emerge from that?

When the teacher was in Pyongyang, there were countless works of Satan. Yet, even amidst that, the teacher invested sincerity for the family. In the morning, praying for a certain family member and waiting to see if they come or not, they will surely come. By praying in such a spiritual atmosphere, one can understand how valuable and effective prayer is. This way, work becomes enjoyable, and one gains the conviction that God is with them.

God is the same. Even if grace is given, if one keeps squandering it, God will depart from that person after just three times. People are the same, right? They cooperate only when they benefit from what is given to them. Who would like someone who keeps squandering what is given?

When the teacher helps the headquarters and regional offices, everyone looks to the teacher, saying money, money, but is that how it should be? God would not be pleased with that either. Each church must develop itself and solve its own problems. But what good is it if a church cannot develop and only builds a regional headquarters? The real issue is how to fill the family. Therefore, evangelism must begin.

People generally move when they feel sadness that brings tears or joy that brings laughter. They must feel either sadness or joy to move. You may have experienced tears in your life alongside your purpose. There may be a capital that overcomes the hardships of melting away one’s bones to fulfill a public mission. That is a precious foundation that even God cannot deny.

When you think about why you did that, it was not to save a hundred people, but to save one life. Therefore, when saving ten people, you must approach them with ten times the sincerity and effort. If you lack confidence here, you should throw away the title of district leader and stand in the most pitiful position, saying, “I am lacking. Please help me,” and pray with a serious heart. When you lower yourself to such a position, God will lift you up. Thus, you must evoke such feelings and appeal to emotions.

When you sacrifice for others from a public standpoint, everyone will sympathize with you. This will move their hearts.

No matter what question you receive, do not be flustered. When you truly feel that God is with you, you will have a sense of what the other person is trying to say as soon as they open their mouth. When you experience this through interpersonal relationships, you cannot help but feel that God is present there. If you push in such a situation, anyone will be broken. There is a pressure there that is more frightening than lightning. If you approach with this conviction, everyone will be pushed away. This is a spiritual battle, and the difference in action depends on the weight of spiritual power.

Then, what will that power be centered around? It must be centered on a heartistic standard. Generally, people try to avoid sad things and seek out joyful things. You must test whether God is with you based on this. Moreover, if the leaders do not understand this, nothing will work.

Resurrection cannot happen unilaterally. All roots must be pulled out from all sides for the work of resurrection to occur. Only then will heaven cooperate. Therefore, even in the principled journey, you must adjust your conditions day by day.

Pastors must pray for the family at least once every three days. The teacher spent nearly three years in Hungnam prison, but even during that time, he never failed to pray for certain family members from mealtime to bedtime. Even for those who have fallen away, he continued to pray for them. Then, spiritually, they would come to the teacher, reporting sorrowfully about their fall. The pitiful scene of someone who, due to physical weakness, had to leave the teacher while saying goodbye is something one cannot help but sympathize with. Even if they have left, one must continue to pray for that person.

Why? Because that person left without fulfilling their responsibility, one must pray until a successor emerges. As long as that foundation of sincerity remains, no matter how many family members fall away, God will surely send someone with a purpose.

Therefore, you must never lose heart just because a family member has fallen away. It is truly strange that when one family member leaves, someone with a similar personality, speech, and even gait comes in. It is astonishing how someone so similar to the one who fell away can come in, yet be superior in every way. Seeing this, one can understand that sincerity is never lost. This is an undeniable fact.

We must not let any encounter end with just that. Especially when meeting someone centered on heaven, one must never forget that connection. Just because that person has stopped coming to church does not mean you should cut ties or curse them. Even if that person has fallen away, you must not discard the connection you had with them.

The standard of sincerity that our Unification Church has invested for Korea must be recognized by heaven and positioned to relate to the world. If that is the case, there is nothing to worry about. With such a standard, even if there are no people, we can reap globally, so there is absolutely no loss.

That is why the sincerity of a leader is terrifying. In the past, the teacher prayed with tears of blood, with his forehead on the ground, for thirty million people. When the day comes that the sincerity of the teacher and yours is recognized before God, thirty million people will surely come to us. Then, the fate of Korea will revolve around one central figure.

You are the leaders of the way; have you invested sincerity for the way until now? You must invest sincerity. Evangelism is proportional to sincerity, not to knowledge or skill. Did you not experience this in the 1960s? Was not the person who evangelized with sincerity better than someone who graduated from university and claimed to know a lot? The issue is how much God sympathizes with you.

Have you ever placed your life on the line for one person with sincerity? 

What is it that district leaders must do with single-minded devotion? Is it just about eating? No. It is about how to resurrect each life as sons and daughters of heaven and transfer them to the heavenly kingdom in this sinful world. With such a sense of responsibility, go out and see if there is anything that cannot be done.

In front of a perfect subject, a perfect object emerges. Therefore, the subject must pray for the object. When praying, if the object wakes up at dawn, you must wake up even earlier to invest your sincerity. When a person invests sincerity for themselves, they will immediately understand.

Leaders must maintain their positions and invest sincerity. If you are a leader, when you pray in the morning, you should think of at least twenty people. Thus, you should pray for more than seventy people each day. You must eat with the family and live with them.

The most serious times for a person are when they eat and when they sleep. When they are hungry and eating, and when they are sleepy and about to sleep, all their nerves are focused on that. In contrast, when they wake up, all their nerves are relaxed, so it is not serious. Therefore, the three meals a day and the times of sleep are the most serious times in daily life. You should pray for the purpose during such serious moments. At that time, one prayer is better than several prayers done at ordinary times.

You must always think of your family with the heart of eating and sleeping together. Then you will get a sense of how each person is doing. When your sensitivity increases, you will see those far away as close, and those close will seem even closer. You will be able to tell at a glance. How can those who guide the hearts of others do so without that level of ability? The issue is how much sincerity one has invested in one life.

When Jesus said, “What good will it be for someone to gain the whole world, yet forfeit their soul?” (Matthew 16:26), you must understand that he placed the heart’s anchor on one life, valuing it more than the universe. When you reach the heartistic realm of Jesus, who fought one-on-one for a life while forgetting the world and sought the valley of human value, only then will you gain the connection of a new family member.

What have you done with the heart of a parent centered on the purpose? You must not neglect those who comforted you when you were struggling among those you had connections with. You should think of that person and pray for them throughout your life. Thus, God will always be the subject. When you go out with such connections, those who have such connections will come to you even if you tell them not to. That is why you must pray.

Should family members pray sincerely while the leader sleeps? That is a life of debt. You cannot develop like that. Sincerity cannot be given all at once; you must take turns investing sincerity in each person you know. You must pray for each person one by one.

Jesus’ failure was due to not having time to pray for each person while traveling with the twelve. He could not share the internal stories that pierced his bones with any one person.

Until you fulfill your responsibility, you must push forward no matter what anyone says. If you have invested sincerity and prayed for something, you must fulfill the set amount of prayer no matter what happens. Even if the person you invested your sincerity in leaves in front of the purpose, you must go find them and fulfill your responsibility. In other words, do not incur debt.

Have you ever invested your sincerity for one person with the serious heart that if this person falls away, I will go to hell? Have you thought that if this person listens to me, we can both go to heaven?

You must stake your entire life and engage in a game that holds onto the history of six thousand years and heaven and earth. How much sincerity must you invest? Have you thought that if one person can overcome such a critical moment, hundreds will follow?
