Study the targets of evangelism.
When evangelizing, you should not speak carelessly. You must assess whether the person is of a negative or positive nature and speak accordingly. Among people, there are those with a negative personality and those with a positive personality. You should never speak to a person with a negative personality when they are feeling down. You should speak to them when they are in a positive state, that is, when they are feeling good. When they are feeling bad and curled up, you should absolutely avoid saying anything exciting. Instead, you should sympathize with their feelings.
Also, when speaking to a person with a positive personality, you should not speak to them when they are in a positive state. Instead, you should speak to them when they are in a negative state. If you speak to them when they are in a positive state, they will not be able to retain what you say and will spill it all out. Therefore, at such times, you should avoid them and speak when they are serious.
To evangelize, you must study people's psychology. Just by observing their expressions or walking styles, you should be able to tell whether they will like it or dislike it. You must be able to officially assess their emotions.
You can even tell whether your wife or those living with you have good or bad things happening just by hearing their footsteps. So when your wife comes into the room, you can say, "Why are you not feeling good?" Then your wife will be speechless because you already know everything without having seen her. You must live with such keen awareness.

Such people will never feel sorrow or loneliness. As the time approaches, the spring breeze will blow. However, for those who did not receive the devotion given to them, the autumn wind will blow. This indicates that their time is drawing near.

<Prayer> Father, today is March 7, the first Sabbath of this month. May Your desired will be fulfilled today together with the Unification Church and this nation. To achieve this oneness, the leaders who take on the main roles are indispensable, and the greater the responsibility entrusted to them, the more central figures must overcome the path of indemnity.

It is human nature to want to avoid the path of suffering. However, human nature should be in the original position that is not fallen, where one can fulfill Your desired will. We must become those who can empathize with Your lonely and sorrowful heart, which cannot bestow such a position upon us today.

Now, as the mission entrusted to us grows larger, we must solidify our current position, so that no matter what trials come from around us, we can overcome, digest, absorb, and eliminate them, becoming the foundation of subjective strength. Therefore, Father, we rely on You.

We know that You have endured trials and hardships that are even more difficult than the suffering we face today. As we receive lessons from You and live according to Your commands to victoriously fulfill Your purpose, whenever we are swayed by our environment, we look to Your loving care that guides and manages us, so please remember us, Father.

This morning, please have compassion on Your lonely sons and daughters scattered across the Korean Peninsula. Look upon those who bow down in one place and submit before You. Consider those who, feeling the pain of Your inner heart that no one knows, report their stories to You as a holy group. Their wishes are Your wishes, and their desires to go forth are also Your desires. If You do not accompany them, there is no one more pitiful than them, so please be with them wherever they are.

To have a heart that overflows with love for the nation and the world is a distant thought, and because it is so far away, if there are children who can shed true tears and appeal to You from such a position, they will never perish with this era, but will establish a new era and leave behind a new source of blessings that has not yet appeared on this earth. We know that throughout history, everyone who has come and gone has sought to walk that path, but no one has been able to practice it. However, we stand at the forefront today, taking a position that aligns with the path You desire. We earnestly hope that You will look upon this and be with us.

Father, because You commanded such a will, we have been able to lay this foundation today, and because You have been present, we have been able to endure and lay this foundation even amidst numerous trials. We thank You for leading us with Your love until now, and we ask that You continue to guide us in the future.

As we consider that the stage of trials approaching is not shrinking but rather growing larger, we realize that the weight of the strength we must invest must also increase. Father, we earnestly ask that You lead us with Your great and wide heart of love as we go forth.

Father, among the few children gathered here, are these truly Your sons and daughters? We must ask ourselves. When we ask what kind of sons and daughters we want to be, we must confidently say that we want to be sons and daughters who can serve You in such a position.

We must not become people who lose our positions as time flows by, swept away by the currents. No matter how strong the flowing waves may be, we must become a rock that can break through and rise above, revealing our true selves even amidst the harsh currents, and we must be Your children whose identities are clear.

I must become a son or daughter who can pledge to fight for this result with the heart to dedicate my life to it, and I must be able to affirm the results of victory for today.

Father, please come personally to our hearts. When we look at our inadequate selves, we know that You may want to separate from us a thousand or ten thousand times, but knowing that there is no one like us on this earth, please encourage us. If we do not want to go, even if it means using a whip, let us go, and if we do not act, please pull us to act.

Without this, we cannot achieve the goals we must accomplish and the path we must walk. Let us unite in heart and look toward the standard of the righteous path left by You, and allow us to fulfill the mission of pioneers day by day without delay, Father, we earnestly hope and wish for this.

At this time, we bow down, so please come and allow Your earnest heart that we cannot forget to dwell in our hearts, and let us become sons and daughters who cannot help but express our longing for You in tears, just as You long for us. Allow us to have a heart as desperate as a parent searching for lost children.

Let us know for sure that we cannot do without You. Even if we die a thousand or ten thousand times, we must hold onto this, possess this, and leave this behind. We must become those who can clearly realize this.

Let us not think of You conceptually or believe in You conceptually, but let us have a sincere and earnest aspect of life where we can discuss and express our stories with You in our practical living space, and let us be Your children who can steadily seek You no matter what anyone says.

Father, let us greet spring when spring comes, summer when summer comes, autumn when autumn comes, and winter when winter comes, and let us be Your children who can meet the new path of indemnity again with the vitality to do so.

After the path of individual indemnity, we stand on the path of restoration that must go through family, tribe, nation, and even the global stage. We should not go with a sad heart, but knowing that our ancestors walked the path of indemnity with sorrow, we should go with a joyful heart. Let us be in a position where we cannot help but call You Father, filled with longing that springs forth from a joyful heart, and let us have a heartfelt yearning that cannot help but embrace You and share our stories.

When approaching You, we must not have hesitations or reluctance. Let us leave behind the position centered on ourselves and forget our inadequate selves in the longing for You, and let us be Your sons and daughters who can run toward You, Father. We earnestly hope and wish for this.

Father, please come to this place and allow us to be sons and daughters who can open the doors of our hearts wide and participate in Your high realm of connection.

Father, please remember all Your daughters who bear the responsibility of this era. Let them know that the difficult place is a grateful and blessed place.

Let us praise the gift of mercy granted within Your will, making each day a path of purpose, so that we can leave behind blessed days and become holy children who have the conditions and connections to be praised before You. We earnestly hope that we can become a Unification Church and a nation that can overcome all trials that come in the future.

No matter how strong the forces of evil may be, we must realize that when there is a heart of earnestness that follows Your heart and Your connection, evil will surely crumble because of that heart.

Father, please look upon the current situation in Asia. When the forces of evil move and block our path, we know that our time is drawing near. Let us resolve to be bound as offerings of life before You, united in heart, and allow us to fulfill the responsibilities entrusted to us in this era. We earnestly ask for this once again. May Your grace, mercy, and love be with us all, and we pray all these words in the name of the True Parents. Amen.

<Words> I would like to speak for a moment under the title "The Wise and the Foolish."

**Human Happiness and Unhappiness and Environment**
A person without hope cannot overcome any difficulties in their daily life. On the other hand, a person with strong hope can endure and navigate their daily life well, no matter the difficulties they face.

Among people, there may be those who have hope in ordinary circumstances, but there may also be those who have hope in difficult situations. However, you must understand that there is a significant difference between hope in ordinary circumstances and hope in difficult situations.

A person who has hope in ordinary circumstances can pursue their hope with just ordinary stimulation and ordinary determination. But if there is someone who has hope centered around a difficult situation, that person must invest elements of overcoming that are proportional to that difficulty. Therefore, one must have the capacity to overcome and surpass the difficult environment they are currently in to have hope in such a situation.

Thus, if there is someone who has new hope in the face of adversity or in a lonely situation, that person may seem to most people to be extremely pitiful and deserving of sympathy. However, we must recognize that those who sympathize with such people may themselves be the ones who are truly pitiful.

When people in ordinary circumstances are placed in the position of someone suffering in a difficult situation, most will retreat from that position. Therefore, if there is someone who can overcome that difficulty and carry even a small hope with the capacity to overcome, such a person can inherit the future, overcome the trials that lie ahead, and have the motivation to fight and advance against those trials. In contrast, those who are in a position of criticism and sympathy cannot stand in such a position. 

Considering this fact, we can understand that being comfortable does not necessarily mean being happy, and being in a difficult and lonely situation does not necessarily mean being unhappy. 

At any time, a loyal subject appears in a nation during its emergency, and a filial child appears in a family when it is on the brink of collapse. In such extreme situations where the environment is unfavorable, true character is proven, and the essence of truth is revealed as a solid reality, as we know well through historical facts or our own living environments.
However, if there is a person who understands that they must take on the fate that the monarch should not bear, and willingly chooses the path of death to prevent the misfortunes of their nation, vowing to save the country with their life, we know that such a person will join the ranks of loyal subjects praised by history.

The same applies to a filial son in a family. In an environment where many people serve their parents and show filial piety, it is not difficult to honor one's parents. However, when everyone rejects their parents and chooses their own path, if one stands ready to sacrifice their only life for the sake of their parents, that person transcends their environment and fulfills the duty of filial piety, thus earning the title of a filial son.

When we think of this, the question arises: where is happiness and where is unhappiness? In today's world, will those who are well-off and in good positions, as seen by many, truly be happy? No matter how favorable their circumstances may seem, those who lack the hope to inherit tomorrow and the strength to overcome the present will undoubtedly vanish without a trace when misfortune arrives.

In this light, it is not the happy people of today who will usher in a new era, but rather those who, despite being in a state of utter misery and pity, struggle with hope. You must understand that it is these individuals who will pave the way for the fate of their country to be newly established and for its miseries to be resolved, leading to a new era.

Who is a wise person? Generally, a wise person is not someone who simply aligns with the good aspects of their era and environment. Thus, a wise person is not someone who merely goes along with the current environment, living in harmony with what others enjoy, but rather someone who possesses the heart to overcome any current difficulties for the sake of the future and lives with such intentions.

Yet, in the face of such trials and tribulations, he did not regard them as enemies but faced them with laughter and hope, and even had compassion for them. If he were foolish, he would have been the most foolish of all. If he had no purpose, he would have been seen as mad or merely a fool.

Despite being confronted by unforgivable enemies who pierced his heart and sought his death, he maintained a generous heart towards them, praying blessings upon them. What did he hold onto when he prayed for his enemies? He did not pray for the doomed era he was in. The nation of Israel that killed Jesus fell into the fate of a ruined nation and became a wandering people, as we know from historical evidence. However, Jesus did not pray for the doomed nation of Israel, nor for the failing Roman Empire, nor for the declining Jewish sect. He prayed for the future nation and world that must not perish, holding onto that hope for his enemies.

Did that nation and world recognize him? Not at all. They did not form any relationship with him. In the reality of his environment, he was in a profoundly lonely position, a place of deep sorrow and resentment. Yet, because his love for the future nation was so great, he refrained from blaming them, fearing that resentment would lead to the sorrow of that nation. He carried his sadness without succumbing to it, fighting with joy instead. Even if he were to die, he wanted to go joyfully to that nation, to connect with it, and to be sown as a seed of sacrifice for that nation. It is because of this that the world has developed into a new world.

From this perspective, Jesus was seen as the most foolish person of his time, the most ignorant and lonely individual whom no one regarded. Yet, from that lonely position, he held onto hope, and even if it meant losing his life, he cherished the value of that nation and world above his own life. Thus, the blood of Jesus was shed for that nation and world, and because hope was sown there instead of loneliness, a new foundation of hope for the future was established. Therefore, if there is a heaven, it cannot help but witness the horizontal development of the world from that point. This is the principle of nature.

Those who enjoyed comfort and held authority in that era treated Jesus, a mere individual, as if he were nothing. 이러한 마음가짐은 개인적인 차원에서만이 아니라, 민족과 국가, 나아가 세계적인 차원에서도 적용되어야 합니다. 우리는 서로 다른 민족과 국가 간의 갈등을 해결하기 위해서도 이러한 마음을 가져야 합니다. 원수를 사랑하고 용서하는 것이야말로 인류가 진정으로 평화롭게 공존할 수 있는 길이기 때문입니다.

이러한 길을 걸어가는 통일교회가 되기 위해서는, 우리 각자가 개인의 이익을 넘어서는 마음을 가져야 하며, 민족과 인류를 위한 희생과 봉사를 실천해야 합니다. 이러한 마음가짐이 있을 때, 우리는 진정한 행복과 평화를 이룰 수 있을 것입니다.

We know that there is a path of overcoming where individuals can represent nations, families can represent nations, tribes and nations can represent nations, and that the nation with the authority of victory has the responsibility to overcome on behalf of heaven.

As we understand that the history of suffering and struggle accumulates in all paths of life, history, and humanity, we must recognize that behind all of this lies your history of struggle and overcoming. We must realize that the crossroads of blood and tears are intertwined here.

We understand that your history of restoration, which has come through such a path of suffering, has reached this Korean land in Asia, crossing over many nations and states. Although this nation did not understand your intention in coming to seek the pitiful Korean people, we must recognize how much you have endured and how earnestly you have hoped while touching our hearts.

Father, when we approach you with sincere hearts, that sincerity is merely an act or word limited to our own lifetime. However, when we think about how you have walked the path of historical grief with the utmost sincerity to fulfill the mission of restoration, we must understand how long and painful that path has been.

Your insufficient children have gathered here today. Before the path of suffering you have walked, before the path of bloody struggle you have traversed, before the agony of the cross you have endured, what are we seeking here? We are not here for our own glory or success. We must go out to be a stepping stone on your pitiful and sorrowful path, to correct the way.

In your sorrowful journey, may you receive comfort through us. Before your powerless appearance, we must become a fresh stimulant filled with hope as loving sons and daughters. Therefore, we earnestly hope that we will not remain as pitiful children, but rather awaken to a new day and, while pledging our hope for tomorrow, become the sons and daughters who can inherit the holy historical foundation before you this morning.

When we think about the path of suffering you have walked to find points of unity not only in hierarchical relationships between you and me, but also in the relationships of before and after, we realize that humanity is always in a detestable state. Humanity always thinks from a self-centered perspective, draws conclusions centered on itself, wishes to be the source of blessings through itself, and seeks something fruitful through itself. We understand that this is the detestable nature of humanity that you do not desire. It is because we are fallen descendants, and because our ancestors were like this, we find ourselves in such a position. Therefore, Father, please remove all elements of evil, and let this time be one where the heart of heaven that can align with goodness can permeate our bodies and minds.

Father, please watch over this place. If there are sons and daughters who can welcome you with joyful faces before the hope you have sought, please embrace those children with a joyful heart. Bestow your blessings upon them with the blessings you have granted. We earnestly hope that you will grant them a time of joy along with the high and precious hopes of tomorrow. If this is not possible, please look upon us with fiery eyes and uproot the bitter roots of sin that live deep within each heart. We earnestly hope that you will remove them with your authority of judgment, Father.

Blessed are the meek, and we must be meek. May a deep yearning arise in our hearts, like a child longing for its mother's milk. May this place, where we struggle and bow down before you, become a holy place. We earnestly hope and wish for this.

Father, we know well that you have woven the history of the Unification Church until now. We know that the master of this altar is none other than you. You alone must be the center here.

When people meet each other, they often become disappointed and leave behind conditions for mutual despair. Father, you are the high and precious one in the harmony between you and humanity, and you are the center of absolute authority. May we always have faith in this, and may we not forget that we are lowly and lonely beings, living in the awareness that we follow you.

Through all the emotions we feel, may every expression of longing for you become a symbol of our yearning, and may that entirety manifest in the form of a son’s life and a daughter’s life.

Now, we are well aware of our own kneeling posture. In this position, when we say that we have come this far, we know that our current hearts are in a position contrary to you, in a lowly position. Please allow us to bow down before you. When we realize that we are not what you desire, let us lay ourselves bare before you and be filled with a heart of repentance. May this hour be one where we earnestly appeal for the touch of mercy and compassion to come before your lofty and precious holy will, connecting us with the ties of life.

Father, March is now reaching its midpoint. We understand that we have responsibilities remaining under the title of 'Securing the Foundation for Unification' as we welcome the year 1971. We must ensure that your steps, which carry all blessings and glory, do not turn away in regret, but rather remain here, not wanting to leave.

If your steps, which have sought and found us in the year 1971, are to remain here, they must be steps that do not wish to leave, filled with a heart that desires to stay forever. This place must become an eternal resting place for you, where you can rejoice forever and bless us.

We feel that we are too far from you and too insufficient, longing to be accepted before you. Now, in this time, may this morning be an opportunity for us to once again resolve our responsibilities along with your command.

Father, this morning, as your children bow their heads towards the headquarters in Seoul, please bless those children who seek the ties of life towards this place. We know that at this time, no one will hold us back. We know that we must go forth on our own. This is the time when we must exert all our sincerity, so we must become those who can offer all our sincerity before you. May the days that come in the future stand by you, and may we be a group that can meet those days according to your name, remaining in the glory of your presence.

We know well that your beloved daughters are fighting on the front lines. Please listen to their heartfelt appeals as they desperately cling to you. May they be allowed to offer their sincerity on behalf of the nation, and may that sincerity never cease. Today, upon that sincerity, for a month, for a year, and until 1972, we have responsibilities to fulfill, so Father, please encourage them. May the support they offer be matched by you. While you protect the rear with your beloved sons and daughters, may we be filled with a deep desire to expand your eternal foundation. May we not let this time pass by without preparing a prayer that can give you glory and praise.
I have discovered that I must bear the responsibility entrusted to me as a filial child, and I have come to understand that I must become a confident son or daughter who is not lacking as a successor for tomorrow. 

In this era where the authority of evil is expanding, we know that we must gather the heavenly authority that can surpass evil and establish a unified form, so that we can become a strong and courageous bulwark against evil and lay the foundation to enjoy the glory of our Father. 

As we look at the numerous religious communities in this world and the many nations, we are aware that the responsibilities imposed upon us are increasing. We earnestly ask and hope that the days to come will not lead to sorrow but will open paths of desire and hope. This morning, we sincerely wish for You to be with us, and we pray all this in the name of True Parents. Amen.

<Words> Humans desire to touch good things without blemish. If there is something most precious, it is in our human nature to seek out and protect that most precious thing. If this is true for objects, it must also be true for people. If there is a true person in the history of this world, we know that our hearts desire to find that true person, serve them, and place them in an unchanging position.

The most important issue for believers
If this is the case for us humans, then it is undoubtedly true that the God who created us also wishes to show what is precious and holy in the sacred places of heaven and earth. Therefore, just as our hearts long for a precious and true environment to emerge from the place where precious and true things exist, we come to understand that God's heart cannot be any different.

When we consider this, we realize that we humans desire many true and precious things. We feel in our daily lives that we want to be with good things and separate ourselves from bad things. We want to be with good things for a long time, and we reject bad things as something that should not be with us. Thus, it is easy for us to express rejection toward bad things and to have a desire to welcome good things.

Then, when we think about why good things do not remain and why bad things invade our lives, we find that it is because we do not have the foundation to accept goodness within ourselves, and our situation is not one that can harmonize with or rejoice in such an environment. Even if there are precious or good things, it is only natural that they cannot remain with us if there is no foundation or environment for them.

This is something we cannot overlook. The reason is that the more precious something is, the more we desire to possess it. Therefore, it is only natural that if what we seek is precious and good, the surrounding environment and foundation must also be precious and good.

When we pursue goodness and truth, we think of precious and good things as our goals, but for those precious and good things to relate to us, we must be something that can be more precious and better. Otherwise, we cannot avoid being in a contradictory position. Even if we place good things in such a position, those good things will diminish in value.

In other words, if I myself become a foundation that has nothing, even if I place something of great value before me, that valuable thing will not manifest as its true worth but will instead diminish to a lesser value. If we fall into a position where we cannot even establish a normal standard of value, then no matter how much God wants to give us good things and precious things, it is impossible for Him to do so.

So, where is heaven? Heaven is in a holy place and in a true place. Therefore, for that holiness and truth to dwell, we must first discover our own holiness and our own preciousness. This issue is of utmost importance for us believers.

Jesus said, "The kingdom of God does not come with observation; nor will they say, 'See here!' or 'See there!' For indeed, the kingdom of God is within you." (Luke 17:20-21) Thus, it is only natural that if my heart, which can house the heavenly kingdom, is not exceedingly high, holy, and precious, the precious, good, and exalted heaven cannot dwell within me. Therefore, we must think that discovering something precious within ourselves is more critical than praising the preciousness of heaven.

Before knowing that heaven is precious, the issue is how to discover the high value within ourselves. Before knowing the precious things of heaven, how much do we recognize our own value as the object that heaven seeks? This is the foremost condition for occupying and ruling that heaven. This cannot be overlooked.

When we think about our lives as we seek great and precious things, everyone desires them, but the reason we cannot find what we seek and achieve our desired goals is not because goodness is bad, nor because goodness distances itself from us, but because that most precious thing stands in opposition to us. It is not that the precious thing does not want to relate to us, but rather that we ourselves do not have the internal connection that can allow us to relate to it. In such a position, no matter how much goodness or preciousness exists, it has nothing to do with us.

So, where do goodness and preciousness dwell? As you know from your daily lives, goodness dwells in good places, preciousness in precious places, and evil in evil places. Therefore, how to create a precious place, a good place, and a high and holy place within ourselves is an issue of utmost importance for us fallen humans today.

How to sustain a good heart
When you consider whether you have a precious heart, a good heart, or a holy heart within you, is there anyone who can boast that they possess such a heart? Even if there are people who can live with such a heart, can they truly maintain that heart for a year? Or if there is someone who can live with such a heart for more than a year, can that person maintain such a heart for ten years as if it were just one day? The question is whether anyone can live their entire life with such a heart. There is no one on this earth who can say they can.

Because we are fallen humans, it is impossible. 

With the heart that desires to accompany a new destiny, we have come to look toward heaven, and although our original hearts may temporarily stimulate our minds and make us aware of ourselves in our daily lives, we cannot boast that this foundation of goodness will remain as an internal connection that influences our hearts and lives for many days.

Therefore, if we have discovered that good heart, the question becomes how we reflect and retain that discovered heart in our daily lives, in our monthly lives, and in our yearly lives, and how we can remove all opposing and conflicting conditions, not succumbing to them but overcoming them to establish a proactive foundation of goodness within ourselves. This is the most difficult issue for believers.

If there is someone who possesses such a precious, good, and holy nature, then even if that person is told not to let goodness accompany them, goodness will still be with them, and even if the place is not precious, it cannot help but be precious. Can evil occupy such preciousness? It cannot. Can evil digest goodness? No matter how evil the world surrounds it like a fortress, it cannot digest goodness and preciousness.

Because the sage stands on a good foundation and in a good environment, the good subject and the good object unite to establish an absolute direction of goodness, which can create a new history and serve as a motivation for transforming into a new humanity. We cannot deny this fact.

Therefore, today, we fallen humans did not start from goodness. However, we know that we were humans with a foundation of goodness but began from a fall. We started from evil. Thus, the foundation of goodness is always surrounded by evil. We must recognize that the evil environment surrounding us is entangled and fixed in a way that is dozens or hundreds of times larger than the good environment.

Therefore, the good heart acts upon my heart in an instant. It is felt through my living environment. It is easy to let go of what is merely felt; however, this feeling must become the center of my life and the embodiment of goodness that can remove the evil environment.

To lay the internal and external foundation of goodness
To form a foundation as a body of sacrifice that can remove evil, we must know how to establish our own internal foundation that can pair with goodness and become a foundation with goodness, as well as the external environmental foundation. This is the most important issue for believers.

Thus, you must understand that it is more difficult to conquer the environment given to you than to conquer the world. It is not the opposing Satan or society that is frightening, but rather the existence of 'me' that directly confronts goodness, surrounding my true heart, that is truly frightening. Therefore, how to overcome this 'me' is the most important issue for believers.

To overcome this, we must engage in a war of attrition. We cannot wage a war of interests for this purpose. For heavenly fortune to turn, we must pay the price of sacrifice proportional to the struggle. You must understand that without sacrifice, no matter how much you pursue goodness, that goodness will have nothing to do with you.

When we pray with our true hearts or strive toward heaven, we may feel joy and excitement resonating within us and may even have hopes, but once that environment is severed, it disappears in an instant. You may have felt that in human relationships, a single word can cause something to vanish forever.

After going through a day or an hour of unwanted living conditions in society, when you compare your true heart's foundation with your own essence, you may have experienced being thoroughly defeated in your daily life. Therefore, as those who have the mission to pioneer such environments, it is the attitude of believers to completely analyze and criticize the foundations of the strong Satan and remove the foundations of evil.

So, where is the one path that believers must take? It lies in the voice of the heart. Therefore, how to expand the good heart established in the heart outwardly is directly related to laying the foundation to possess the most precious and good things of heaven. You must understand that setting this as a daily life philosophy and daily life goal to strive for is more precious than influencing society, nations, or states.

Sin does not attack and occupy me from the relative world but rather invades my heart from my environment. Therefore, at the front line where it invades from the environment, I must decisively cut off the opposing elements that manifest as negative thoughts with the good thoughts of my heart. Without going through the ongoing bloody struggle for justice, eternal goodness and the most exalted and precious things cannot dwell in my heart. 

While this may temporarily leave joy or serve as a stimulating foundation for hope, the question is whether it can become the foundation of my life, the origin of eternal life, the source of eternal happiness, and the leaven of goodness. You must understand that this is impossible.

Therefore, to overcome this appeal to the true heart, we must fight against our environment. However, no one wishes to fight. It is a position that no one desires, but it is a responsibility and duty that we must bear.

By developing this area from the current position to the position of hope, today can inherit the foundation of tomorrow's hope. However, if we lack the autonomy to develop the current position into the environment of tomorrow's hope, then no matter how much there is a good hope for tomorrow, it will have nothing to do with the current me and that hope for tomorrow.

Then, how can we relate it? In your environment, how can you address the good and precious things that your true heart demands and create environmental conditions that can correspond and align with those demands? This is not something to be resolved through fighting with weapons like in the world. The question is what can prevent this war of attrition. It requires effort and sincerity. It must be sincerity.

To what degree must the degree of sincerity go? If there is a friend in this world whom you can cherish, is that friend someone who cannot be separated from you for thousands of years? A good friend is one who is better than anything expensive, even better than self-denial. It is not a relationship that can be discarded with a single word of daily emotional life. Even if life itself is taken away, it is a relationship that cannot be severed. 

Such a place of compassion is the foundation of goodness, and all the connections that were related to goodness in my true heart are eternally unbreakable. It is impossible to part ways.
Then, has such a connection been established in an environment that can align with my heart? Have you become a friend in that environment, or have you formed a group where you can put in effort from a good position? You must understand that the question of whether you can become a subject of goodness in your place, or whether you can become a foundation, and whether you can bear a creative history is determined here.

For this reason, when you say that you have truly received Heavenly Father, you must realize that it cannot be done merely with words. How much sincerity do you have in your heart when you serve the Father? All sensations through our five senses are directly connected to our emotions. Through the five senses, how much can you love the Father, how much can you realize the precious value of the Father, how much can you long for the holiness of the Father, and how much can you praise Him? This is the issue. It is not something that can be felt during a prayer session with an audience or during a gracious time; rather, we must receive constant feelings through every moment in our living environment. The question is how to discover a resulting self that cannot help but resonate with Heaven, centered on that feeling.

Sincerity is the element that saves me. Therefore, what you need to think about again here is that if you do not approach with sincerity, you will end up fighting against evil. The place of sincerity is not the place that has overcome the struggles of battle; it should be a place where there is no fighting. Only a sincere heart and action remain in the eternal place. That is why you are praying.

So, what kind of prayer should you offer? You must pray to control yourself. You must pray to overcome yourself. You want to be more comfortable, you want to be happier, and you want to make everything about yourself the center of your motivation. Because you lack the strength to negate this self-centered environment, the place where you struggle to receive God's strength is the place of prayer.

Therefore, when you put in sincerity to overcome the environment through prayer, the value of that sincerity in goodness will proportionally remove the conditions of the evil environment. In other words, because you stand in a position where the heart of good motivation can expand to eliminate evil, when you stand victorious in that struggle, your heart cannot help but be joyful. So why are you joyful? Because your nature has been cultivated with the good environment and a foundation has been established to give and receive, and as it expands, you will feel joy, satisfaction, and value that you have not felt in your life until now.

This joy is not determined by the degree of prayer time but varies according to how much sincerity you invest within that time frame. You must understand that sincerity is the foremost element that can save us. The principle may serve as a motivation or stimulus that can save you, but whether you receive salvation or not is not determined by the principle. Therefore, you must understand that unless you stand in a position directly connected to sincerity, you cannot complete your own salvation.

How should you offer sincerity? Who actually caused the fall? We humans possess a fallen lineage. Therefore, humans are beings with evil bodies that cannot be accepted before God. I am not a corresponding being before the holy and precious God; I am an opposing being. It is undoubtedly a wrong appearance that pursues opposing connections. If such fallen humans are to harmonize with the high and precious God and become His sons and daughters, it cannot be done merely with words.

Are you truly a son or daughter of God? That is something you know yourself. Your heart knows. You do not need to hear a third-party explanation; you know it yourself. If you are truly a son or daughter of God, no matter how negative the environment is, you should be able to say, "I am a son or daughter of God." You should have a steadfast belief that "I lived like this in the past, I live like this in the present, and I will live like this in the future." You must understand that a good environment and a foundation of goodness are absolutely necessary to say, "That heart has become one with the environment. The environment has become one with that feeling." Therefore, it is not enough to have just the heart; you must take action. Through this, there is only one way to unfold words and actions to connect with a new resurrection and to reinforce and spread the power of struggle in your life, and that is to invest sincerity. You must understand that without sincerity, you cannot overcome.

So how do you offer sincerity? Is it by offering it like a medicine vendor selling medicine in the market? No, it is the opposite. In such a place, you are your own enemy. You become a factor that can cause discord, jealousy, suspicion, and destruction.

In what place should sincerity be offered? It should be offered in a place where no one is present, a place known only to me. When one's true heart yearns for Heaven, that heart is not something everyone should know; it is something only I should know. Centered on that heart that only I know, I cannot resolve my own foundation in a place where everyone knows. Sincerity must be offered in a place that no one knows, a secret place. What is established through sincerity cannot be boasted about.

When you look at the Bible, there is a passage that says, "I know a man in Christ who fourteen years ago was caught up to the third heaven." (2 Corinthians 12:2-7) You must understand what Paul lived by for fourteen years. When you consider the ideal of the third heaven shown by Heaven through sincere gifts, that ideal must be directly connected with me and my life. After fulfilling the practical process to affirm that environment, Paul finally declared such facts.

What has been seen should not be transferred as it is. What has been seen must be purified as my own. To do this, as the kingdom of Heaven is great, it must become a great activity, and it must establish a relationship with humanity as much as it is global. Thus, by denying all of one's own being and fighting to overcome all conditions centered on the theory of the third heaven with joy, the noble character of Paul was formed. Looking at Paul's actions, he had a noble character. He had a foundation of sincerity that only Paul could possess. You must understand this.

Sincerity is not something that is offered to be known by others. It is about establishing a relationship with Heaven, which exists among humans, and with goodness. The existence of 'I' is an individual existence. Therefore, to establish a connection with the absolute existence, you must offer sincerity in a secret place where no one can participate. The joy felt with the sincerity offered in a secret place cannot be anything less than great joy. It is the joy that Heaven rejoices in. When that joy is full and influences others, you must understand that the authority to act on behalf of Heaven's command begins from there.

To serve Heaven, you must offer corresponding sincerity. A person who offers sincerity does not speak. Within the essence of that sincerity, there are contents that no one can know. The path of a person who possesses such content and steadily offers sincerity is the right path. Sincerity must be offered secretly. Do you possess God, who welcomes you with body and mind along with sincerity? Therefore, if you want to see God here, the question is how much sincere heart you have in longing for Him. If you want to meet Him, the question is how much sincere heart you have in wanting to meet Him.

You must ask yourself how much you have served the Father, who is good and precious, with your own internal connections that can accommodate Him. You may see, hear, and feel through your five senses, but how much sincerity did you have when you listened? How much did you see with that kind of heart? And how much did you feel in a place where you exerted all your sincerity?

You should not think, "This much sincerity is enough." When you ask whether the environmental conditions that can welcome the most good being have been established by the foundation of sincerity, you must understand that saying, "This much is enough," cannot stand as an absolute standard of sincerity. When God, who is the subject of the highest goodness, considers such sincerity as a relative foundation, it cannot be accepted. Therefore, even if the place where tears are shed and sincerity is poured out is a lacking and lowly place, God can come there.

Rather than looking for a high and glorious place of the flesh to hide one's shameful appearance, if you seek a place where you would rather go to hell with the heart that can cover your shame, and if you shed tears there, you must feel that a connection with God is established in such a place through your faith life. "I have offered this much sincerity, so Father, now You must help me. I have offered enough sincerity, yet Heaven remains indifferent and does not understand my situation." Can you say that? You cannot.

Since the day our human ancestors Adam and Eve sinned, God has worked for 6,000 years to uproot the sin that cannot be resolved at will. We must understand that we have the mission to uproot this root. Since God has walked for 6,000 years, I must also go somehow. Therefore, you must understand that there cannot be a path of faith that does not involve tears while offering sincerity.

No matter how handsome or beautiful one may be, no matter how much one possesses a glorious appearance and can face the world, that alone is not enough. It may hinder sincerity rather than help it. You must stand in a position where you can feel the historical misery that there is no one more wretched than you among the sinners of the world. Even if I were to extinguish at once here, even if I were to be utterly destroyed, if Heaven exists, then if it is to burst, it should burst without leaving a trace, and if there is anything left, I hope that it can be molded again from that which has been scattered. In other words, it is in the place of struggling with the heart that hopes for the benefits of resurrection centered on the life that remains after death that the connections of life intersect and the connections of life are determined. In a position where one confidently says, "I have done enough," God does not accompany you, and you will feel this through deep prayer life.

Then, how much sincerity have I offered to the Father? When I say I want to see the Father, how much of a price have I paid with sincerity to want to see Him? Even if I want to walk with the Father, live with Him, and welcome the country and environment that the Father desires, the question is how much sincerity I have in my heart when I approach Him.

Have you ever risked your life and offered sincerity to save a single life? The enemy is not in the world; the enemy is within oneself. The Bible says, "Greater love has no one than this, that someone lay down his life for his friends..." (John 15:13). What does this mean? If you lay down your life without any connection, how can it be great love? To risk your life for a friend, with a heart that offers more than life, and to say that if you do not save that person, they will go to hell... This is love, feeling the pain of death yourself and saying you would die in their place. Is it love to die without even thinking about it? A sacrifice without sincerity, especially if it is for oneself, is worthless.

If you have laid down your life for a friend, why did you do it? To be saved... Then that person cannot go to heaven. Such a person may say they laid down their life for a friend, but in the end, they are using that friend to go to heaven. That person cannot go to heaven.

If you go to the spiritual world, there are many martyrs. However, those who think, "I must die like this to go to heaven with Jesus," cannot enter heaven. "Because this precious and high being died for me, I am indeed one body, one flesh, and one blood with Him. Therefore, I must disappear with His death and be resurrected with His life. Because I am one with Him, the path He walked is the path I must walk. Just as He died for all people, I must also die not for myself but for all people." Those who think this way will enter heaven even if they are told not to.

The fundamental issue lies here. The question of whether it is love or not is where the divergence occurs.

Therefore, you must be able to say, "Laying down my life for a friend is not for the sake of salvation or to receive any blessings. I do this solely to save him." You must offer sincerity for him, on his behalf. A person who prays with their life on the line for a single life, who sincerely offers their life, is the one who loves that person.

So, how much sincerity have you offered centered on a single life? This is the issue. No matter how much external content you can boast about living gloriously for seventy or eighty years in this human world, when asked, "Did you love people?" can you say, "Yes, I did"? And when asked, "How did you do it?" can you respond, "I did it this way"? Knowing his death as my death, feeling his pain as my pain, shedding the tears he must shed, and enduring the suffering he must endure, I am resurrected.

Try praying. How much sincerity have you held onto for a single life for a year, two years, three years, or even longer? This is the issue. Since that life is undoubtedly within the realm of death, how much sincerity have you offered for that life among all humanity living on this earth? How much sincerity have you offered for anyone? It is not for my own benefit but to save them... Have you approached people with a sincere heart, knowing that without my touch, they will undoubtedly go to hell?

God is offering even more sincerity.
If it is an individual, have you ever put in effort for that individual? If it is a family, have you done so for that family? If it is a neighborhood, have you done so for that neighborhood? If it is the Kim family, have you centered your efforts around the Kim family? I have saved individuals, but I have not saved families, so I must save families. Have you ever sincerely put in effort for any family? God has carried out the restoration history in this way. How much effort has the Father put in to find the lost children? He has risked His life and put in sincere effort. That is why there is no face to show before the Father, no way to lift one's head, and no way to make any objections or counterarguments.

So when we ask whether fallen humans have put in effort or if God has put in effort, it is not the fallen humans who have put in effort. It is God who has put in effort. That is why God is necessary. That is why God is appreciated. That is why we want to follow God. That is why God is precious. I may say that I am precious because I have put in effort, but God has put in more effort than I have, which is why God is more precious.

Things made with sincere effort are considered valuable. Isn't that right? When asked what valuable items exist in my life, they are the items made with effort. Even if something can be made in a few hours, if it has taken one year or ten years of sincere effort to create it, it is considered valuable, regardless of its actual quality.

Isn't that true? People say that handmade items are precious, while machine-made items are not, right? Why is that? The shape may be better, but in places like America, handmade items are expensive while machine-made items are cheap. In fact, machine-made items may be better in terms of shape and all aspects. However, they lack sincerity. True value is revealed in proportion to the sincerity put into it. That is the manifestation of conscience. This is not because humans are crafty, but because it is the way of heaven. You must understand this.

Therefore, God is putting in more effort than humans. God puts in effort for individuals, for sons and daughters, and then for the families that those sons and daughters seek out. God puts in effort for the tribes that those families seek out. If a family is found, then the descendants should do well, right? So, God is putting in effort for those descendants. And if they have formed a family, God puts in effort for that family; if they have come together to form a nation, God puts in effort for that nation. In this way, God is continuously putting in effort. That is why humanity has not perished today.

What is the reason humanity has not perished and continues to survive? You must understand that this has allowed for the path of development to continue. No matter how much effort humans put in, it cannot compare to God's effort. Therefore, when you go out to evangelize, you cannot just go without preparation. The question is how much sincerity you bring with you. If it will take a week, a month, or even a year or two to evangelize someone, then you must put in sincere effort during that time. Whether it rains or snows, whether you eat or sleep, whether you come and go, or whether you rest, you must give your entire heart to that person. If you give completely, you will receive completely. This is the principle.

Thus, the question is how much sincerity you put into loving God and how much sincerity you put into loving humanity. This is what becomes your personality in the spirit world and becomes the foundation of glory.
