The Wish of the Absolute Being
If the history of the Unification Church has fought until now, that history must not remain as a history of struggle for a specific individual. Whether that history has value or not depends on whether it can represent heaven and earth... If anyone does not go along with the one absolute will centered on the one wish that humanity desires, the history of the Unification Church will shine.

Today, the Unification Church is not walking the path of the will for a specific nation alone, but if it goes forward centered on the one and only wish that humanity has longed for, that all people living in this era desire, and that future descendants can pursue, the Unification Church will never flow along with the circumstances of this era.

Whether the Unification Church can appear as the harbinger of happiness in the future world and as a warrior establishing a new history depends on whether the convictions held by the Unification Church can stand in harmony with the will that humanity desires. We can infer that the question of whether the Unification Church can shine historically is determined by this.

From this perspective, this will is not only the wish of humanity. If there is a historical master who governs this humanity, it must be the wish of that master, and if there is an absolute being governing the current history, it must be the wish of that absolute being. When we look at the historical process of humanity, we may see the fluctuating masses of humanity flowing with the changes of the times, but when we look at it centered on the will, those who go along with the will are supported by the absolute being behind them and stand clearly as the center of the times, and such individuals will never find themselves in a position of failure.

The wish of the absolute being is to establish goodness in the world. To achieve that wish, it is necessary to remove all conditions that oppose it and prepare conditions for victory. Therefore, the process of those who go along with that will, no matter how rough and miserable it may be, is merely a process and cannot be seen as a decisive appearance that can replace the whole.

Those walking the path of the will, even if they fall into a miserable environment, will find that it can serve as a stimulus for their development and a foundation for expanding the territory of their wishes. However, no matter how many sorrows there may be, they cannot become the motive that prevents the future will or collapses the path of the will.

From this perspective, when we look at the providential history today, we know that there have been many ups and downs. In some eras, there was progress, while in others, there was regression; at times there was ascent, and at other times there was descent. We have learned that history has gone through such processes, and we too will go through such processes throughout our lives. Even when we look at our daily lives centered on the will, we will feel that there are strong aspects of self-determination as well as times when we stand in the opposite position.

At such times, we should not merely rejoice in the times of ascent, nor should we grieve in times of descent. Therefore, if there is a time of descent, we must digest and absorb it as a period of rest where we can determine the hope for tomorrow. If we have such a life philosophy, even if we are in a very low position, we will not pull ourselves down to an even lower position but will absorb it as a foundation for determination for tomorrow.

We must understand that we cannot avoid such playfulness.

If there is night, there is day. Night is a period of preparation for the day to shine, a period of rest, and a period of further refinement. When we consider this, we realize that there are fluctuations in the process of suffering.

How can one stand in a position that does not perish? If one forgets that when one is in a position to ascend, one can also descend, then when one finds oneself in a position of descent, one becomes a person who has lost the path to ascend, thus losing the foundation to start again toward the hope of tomorrow. If one stands in such a position, a state of stagnation will inevitably occur. When stagnation occurs, the path to self-development is also blocked.

If that blocked position becomes a place that God does not desire, then one will be removed from there. This is an undeniable principle before the heavenly law.

Therefore, even if we find ourselves surrounded by difficult circumstances during times of descent, we should not be discouraged. The more we descend, the more we must confront the difficulties of the internal environment, and we must cultivate a tenacious self that can push forward with a concentrated heart that holds the core standards of the will and has conviction in facing the external environment. Even if such a period lasts for a year, ten years, or even a lifetime, if we maintain a tenacious internal heart and push forward, there will always be a way to start again toward the path of the will.

If we do not do this and instead succumb to loneliness, difficulties, and trials, forgetting the will and abandoning it, and standing in a position to criticize and give up everything we have walked in the life of the will, then the path to the will will come to an end. This is an undeniable fact.

That is why believers must never have the notion of failure on the path of the will or the thought of departing from the path of the will. When facing the will, there will be a time of utmost significance. If there is a person with a higher spirit than others, there will be a time when they can first encounter the will. For example, just as a higher antenna can better receive signals from afar, a person with a higher spirit will be the first to know the new will.

However, knowing the will first is not the issue. The issue is how long one can hold onto that will with value, based on how much one knows it first.

When going forward centered on that will, if there are fluctuations in one's life, one should not abandon the will when descending and think to embrace it again when ascending. No matter how much one may find oneself in a time of ascent, if there is no motivation to hold onto the will during times of descent, one cannot claim that time as their own.

For example, we know that the four seasons of spring, summer, autumn, and winter cycle. When spring passes, summer comes; when summer passes, autumn comes; when autumn passes, winter comes; and when winter passes, spring returns. If a seed or a plant with life is present, when spring arrives again, they can start anew with a form that is larger and thicker than the previous spring. In the same way, walking the path of the will is also similar. If one stands in a position where one is completely dead in autumn, that is the end. No matter how great that being is, it is of no use by itself.

Even if, in autumn, only bare branches remain externally, if one does not succumb to that environment but possesses the concentrated life force within oneself and has the readiness to overcome the external environment, that tree will reveal itself anew before heaven and earth when spring comes again.

Thus, when one comes back to life with new life, it does not mean becoming smaller than the previous year, but rather becoming greater. Here, a new experience is born.
is. A new layer is formed, establishing a solid foundation of defense that no one can invade. This is a fact that anyone can understand.

Therefore, trials are an inevitable part of life’s journey or the path of purpose. No matter how happy a person may be, there is no one who is happy from the day they are born until the day they die. There are always ups and downs.

The place of prosperity and the place of ruin

So, what is it that you need to know about the turning point of prosperity and ruin? How do people end up in ruin? Those who are ruined are the ones who, when faced with trials and suffering on the path of goodness, completely give up. Such people meet their end there.

However, those who recognize their goals as precious and strive towards them, no matter what trials and suffering they encounter, can gather their inner strength to overcome and commit to starting anew on that foundation. For such individuals, there is no path to ruin.

On the path of goodness, when the time comes, strength is surely added. This is the path of goodness. A good person is never in a state of despair. After overcoming a hurdle, there is always a time for revival. When that time comes, heaven will lead goodness once again. Therefore, even in the saddest, most difficult, and painful times, the path that heaven takes, the path of purpose, and the path of goodness are surely paths that can be revived. We must always keep in mind that God comes to find us and leads us. For this reason, we should not be complacent but should prepare ourselves, gathering our hearts in anticipation of that day, no matter how painful or lonely it may be. Even if we are in the lowest position, if we carry a heart that hopes for that time, we will surely meet the time of goodness. This is something that can be experienced by those who have had mysterious experiences today or in our daily lives. Therefore, we must always hold onto a heart of hope. Even if we find ourselves in dire straits, we must carry a heart that is directed towards purpose or goodness. Even if it means sacrificing ourselves, if we move forward in that way, you must know that the purpose we hold will remain.

The saints and enlightened ones who have come and gone in the course of history did not abandon their convictions when faced with unfortunate circumstances in the world. The more difficult the environment became, the more they held onto their inner convictions, believing that if hope did not come in this era, it would surely come in the future. Such individuals eventually emerged as great figures or saints in history.

Therefore, no matter how difficult the environment becomes, we must not stand in a place of despair. We must not stand in a place of despair. Goodness is eternal. Goodness does not develop unilaterally; it develops through ups and downs. After crossing one peak, you meet the plain, and after passing through the plain, there is another new peak. Everything develops through this cycle of rising and falling, giving and receiving. We must understand that everything develops in this manner. It is difficult to go straight.

For this reason, even if there are hierarchical relationships or biases in our faith life, we should not be discouraged. No matter how skewed the environment may be, our inner heart towards purpose must not change, and we must carry the mindset that “the purpose I pursue will surely be fulfilled. Trials will inevitably come on the path I take.” Thus, the more difficult it becomes, the more we must prepare for that difficulty, and the more we are pushed, the more we must not yield our inner stance. When the time comes to push back against that difficult environment, you must understand that you will see a new beginning.

So, what is the place where one can fall into ruin? It is the place where one gives up while pursuing goodness. It is the place where one completely cuts off the path of goodness and turns back. Such a person will be ruined.

What is the place where one does not fall into ruin? It is the place where, no matter how difficult it may be, one believes that what they have done is good and that what they have lived until now is undoubtedly true. Even when faced with a negative environment, one must carry the historical evidence of the past and move forward with the conviction that “what I have done is surely true.” When one moves forward in this way, they can feel joy and happiness that they did not recognize before. By focusing on those moments and not losing the connections that brought them, if they proceed with sincerity and a heart that hopes for the right time, spring will surely come.

Then, is there no way to prevent such ups and downs from coming before us? In our faith life or our life journey, as we develop and progress along these curves, is there no way to prevent it beforehand? There is indeed a way to prevent it.

If you are in a position to solve this problem, and you carry the connections you have held in your heart thus far, if you do not abandon them and instead carry the connections that help you overcome, you can meet that time. However, if you find yourself in a difficult environment, what is the one method to overcome it? You need companions or comrades, and you must receive guidance from a teacher. That is necessary.

The way to avoid the path of ruin

If you are faced with a cliff due to such and such a problem, what should you do to overcome it? For those who find it difficult to solve things individually, they should seek out someone who is higher in faith than themselves and openly discuss their issues. They must say, “I will not be just myself but will be a follower.” If they say to go right, they go right; if they say to go left, they go left. If they say to go up, they go up; if they say to go down, they go down. If they say, “I will not be for myself but will be in place of the one guiding me,” then there is a way to evade that environment.

For this reason, comrades are needed in faith life. A person without comrades is a lonely person. If there are comrades, they can supplement and protect each other. Thus, a way to overcome the difficulties of the environment emerges. If there are no comrades, one must solve everything alone, which is an extremely difficult task for someone who does not have the ability to resolve the relationships around them.

Therefore, when faced with ups and downs, one must seek out comrades or teachers, entrusting their whole being to them, and when they can completely act as their representative, they can overcome the ups and downs.

Thus, when we feel lonely, sad, or isolated, we realize that it is necessary to find someone we can follow as a representative or to read scriptures or listen to the sermons of famous people to resolve our path.

To avoid difficult paths, it is essential to lead with a guide, but what is the next way to avoid falling into ruin? When faced with considerable difficulties, do not worry about those difficulties. Do not worry about ten difficulties but instead seek out a million difficulties and charge forward. In doing so, you will not only endure ten trials but will also be able to face a million trials. In other words, jump into the problem. Then, a reaction will occur, similar to an action. If you go with the strength of ten, you can stand, but if you charge with the strength of a million, a reaction will occur. Just as jumping from a height generates a force proportional to that height, the same phenomenon occurs.

You too. If you are struck in your heart and fall into despair and give up, you will be ruined. However, if you present an action to face a problem that is greater than the one you have encountered, God will not abandon you. When you are destined to go a certain way, if you place God at the center and step forward into a more sacrificial position, God will hold you.

Therefore, when you feel depleted in your spiritual life, the way to resolve it is to seek out a leader and openly present all your problems, taking the attitude of following them as their representative. The next method is to voluntarily seek out a more miserable position than the one you are currently in.

Then, you should reflect on the standard of your faith life in the Unification Church today. Have you merely gone back and forth to church, or have you faced trials from your family while practicing your faith? If you have faced trials through your husband, wife, or children for one year, two years, three years, four years, and so on, there will come a time when the path of purpose becomes unclear. There will inevitably come a time like a buffer zone. In that place, in that very form, you cannot escape. You cannot escape just as it is.

To escape that place, first, you must have a sincere heart for the purpose. If you had a sincere heart for the purpose in the past, you must extend that heart again and, no matter how extreme the trials may be, do not give your heart to the environment, but leave behind the seeds that can become leaven. If you lose that heart, there will be no way to recover.

To resolve a retreating position

If this method does not work, you must seek out a leader or teacher who can take responsibility for your life and speak frankly. Do not hold back; speak openly. In discussions, you should not only mention what is favorable to you and omit what is not. You must speak honestly. “Please be my representative. Lead me.” You must follow their guidance. In doing so, you become not yourself but their representative. That is the only way.

If that still does not work, you must take action. You should voluntarily go the way that is beyond the current cross you bear. If someone who has been struck in heart while evangelizing thinks they can resolve it by retreating to the rear, that person is foolish. Such a retreat will never lead to resolution. For such a person, the feeling of having retreated without heaven’s permission after going out to evangelize will always capture their environment. If you went out to evangelize and were struck in heart, what is the way to resolve it? You must maintain the desire to go out to evangelize again.

If you went out to evangelize but have no way to resolve it, then you should consult someone who has not retreated while evangelizing. If you have retreated after evangelizing, you should ask someone who has not retreated, “How did you fight? Please guide me.” The issue at this point is simple. They will instruct you on how to fight. Then you must absolutely obey that instruction. If you do it your way, you will not find the answer. Therefore, you must deny yourself to find the answer. The stronger you are, the closer you come to the way of resolution.

What is the next method of resolution? If you have gone out to evangelize in a certain area, district, or zone, and there are opposing individuals, you must voluntarily seek out those who oppose even more fiercely, those who are several times more vicious and hostile. There is no other way.

Then, what is the wisest method? In faith life, there will inevitably be trials. There will always be dark nights. Is there a way to prevent this? Is there a way to evade such trials and ups and downs? When considering this issue, there is indeed a way. What is that way? It is to live on behalf of God. Then, what does it mean to live on behalf of God? It means to love people.

When faced with suffering, to escape from it, you must carry your inner faith and, next, receive guidance from a leader, and then voluntarily take on even greater burdens.

So, is there no way to prevent such ups and downs from arising? If there is a way, it is simply to love people. It is the way to live for others.

If there are ten people, a wise person is one who lives for those ten. That person does not live with their own perspective but follows the perspectives of the ten. There is no persecution for those who follow. Those who follow do not strike. If you have sacrificed for ten people, you will not be caught until all ten are caught.

Living for others means there is no way to fall into ruin. 

In this sense, what did Jesus prepare during his three years of public ministry with the twelve disciples? He lived not for himself but for the disciples. The twelve disciples are a special model. They are a special representation of countless people throughout the course of human history. They are people of their time, but they can represent all of humanity across historical eras. Jesus raised these twelve disciples and lived a life of service for three years. What was that life of service? It was a life of sowing seeds and nurturing the sprouts that come forth. It was not a life for oneself but a life for others.

When those disciples who were served began to falter, Jesus would become despondent. When the twelve disciples abandoned Jesus, he made a decision for himself, saying, “Not my will, but yours be done,” asserting himself and placing the cross before God in prayer. Before that, he prayed for the three disciples. What would the content of Jesus’ prayers have been? First, it would have been prayers regarding the future rise and fall of the nation of Israel. Next, he would have prayed for those disciples who had followed him with sincerity for three years. And he would have prayed for the three disciples represented here, that they would not fall into ruin centered on purpose. In other words, Jesus did not pray for himself but prayed for the nation and wept for the representatives of the nation, the three disciples. However, when everything fell apart, the cross was determined. Jesus had to face the cross as his responsibility. This is something we must consider.

Therefore, a person who lives for others, that is, if they have lived for ten people, even if nine oppose them, one will stand by them. Among the ten, half...
Even if one opposes oneself, half of them supports oneself. It means that they will always be a fence for you. If I am invaded, there is a responsibility to protect me, and if I have worked hard on behalf of others, they will be responsible for that. Why? Because they have received grace. A person who cares for others, even if they have ups and downs, does not suddenly fall down all at once. There are those who go up and down, but among them, there are those who are rising. If I hold on to the rising person and support and sympathize with them, I can prepare for the time of darkness.

In religious life, the saying "Be meek and humble and sacrifice for others" means that God has granted us the utmost love so that we can develop without being invaded and escape from the ups and downs. 

For this reason, there is no one who lives for others and fails. Let’s say there is someone in the neighborhood who is in a pitiful situation without a penny, yet they bestow grace upon the entire neighborhood. Everyone in the neighborhood knows that this person’s daily life is miserable. If such a miserable person is invaded by even more miserable external forces, the neighborhood people will unite to prevent that misery. Isn’t it true that such things happen in our living sphere centered on human affection?

God, who has awakened ignorant humans, what does that mean? It means that such a person should not be invaded by external forces. Therefore, that environment becomes a protective nurturing ground and a hope that looks to the good. It becomes a foundation that can be left behind. This is because everyone knows this instinctively, and that heart is activated to protect that person. Similarly, a person who lives for others absolutely cannot fail. It is impossible for them to fail. Even if they try to fail, they cannot.

Why can’t they fail? It is because they are participating in a living sphere like that of a father. It is because that is the path God walks. The omniscient and omnipotent God does not say to humans, "You must serve me and obey me absolutely." It is the opposite. Because humans know nothing, they must be enlightened. They must be taught because they do not know how to walk the path. Is it easy to teach and guide?

You find it difficult to educate even one of your own children, right? That child is your own flesh and blood. When a mother sheds tears, the children can empathize and cry with her. When a father is sad and sheds tears, the children can naturally feel that sadness. Yet, despite this, guiding and nurturing them is extremely difficult, isn’t it? When we look at this, today’s humans are not the children of God. No matter how much God cries, they act as if they do not see. No matter how much God is saddened, they act as if they do not care. This is because humans are born of Satan’s bloodline. Rather, they praise God when they see Him sad. They rejoice and laugh when they see destruction. How much effort must God exert to guide and teach such humans? However, if God did not have the heart to care for and pity from one to a hundred, a thousand, or ten thousand, could He have held onto the providential history until now?

What is the story and position of God, who has led providential history until today? It is that with a heart of compassion, He knows, "If I do not intervene, they will perish. I am certain that destruction is not the purpose given to original humans." God knows that humans absolutely need Him, so He has come through the historical process, disregarding the path of suffering, and has educated countless humanity. This is God’s position.

So, what does it mean to live a life of sacrifice and service for others today? It means to have a heart of compassion. If there is a patriot, that patriot feels a deep compassion for the suffering and oppression of the nation, connecting the pain of the people to their own pain. They substitute the sorrow of the people with their own sorrow. Without such a heart, one cannot be a patriot who can remain for that country. Therefore, one must become a person who sacrifices and lives for others. The Bible also says, "What you do for the least of these, you do for me," and "Love your neighbor as yourself. There is no greater love than this."

True love. Today, Unification Church members say, "Let us love our country and love the will." They speak well. Before loving the country, love the individual. If you want to love the country passionately, first try to love the individual passionately. Before serving the country, serve the individual. Because the good of the country is a great good, before seeking the great good, seek the personal small good. Before the personal and individual goods can be combined into a great good, the purpose of the good of the country cannot be achieved. Therefore, the problem lies with the individual.

How many people have you truly loved since coming to the Unification Church? This is the issue. Over the years or decades you have attended church, how much have you loved others from the depth of your heart while standing in the position of the heart that your father sympathizes with? This issue determines how much love you will receive from God when you go to that world.

How many days have you fasted for one life? How many months have you shed blood and sweat for that life? The problem lies there. You say, "I love God. I love the country." But what does that have to do with you? Such words are empty words. Love cannot be established from a self-centered perspective. It is only when you advocate for that person, uphold their position, and establish their position that the word love is truly established. Isn’t that right? Do you say to someone you love, "Hey, you are my servant"? You elevate that person above all others and care for them, and love is established in the position of wanting to be with them. If you center on yourself and say, "You must do as I say," that is not love.

The love of parents for their young children is pure love. The parents, who know everything, are in a position where they know more than the child who knows nothing, and they are doing it for the sake of that child.

If there is someone who lives for ten people, when those ten people are blessed, that blessing becomes their own blessing. When there is a feast at the next house in the neighborhood, the person who lives poorly and runs errands in the neighborhood finds that feast to be their own feast. They can recognize that it becomes a foundation of joy for them. Therefore, when those ten people are blessed, even if the person who lived for them does not receive a blessing, they can still taste the shadow of that blessing. There is something to benefit from.

For this reason, the ideology of living for others is a formidable ideology. Good is for the whole and becomes the center of the whole. The position that seeks to bind everything together with one love is the place where the center of the whole is determined, and thus goodness is present. However, if one sweats and toils for oneself, even if they sleep soundly, they do not feel good. However, if one sweats and toils for others, they can sleep lightly. It becomes multidimensional. They feel, "I am not a bad person. If God exists, He cannot abandon me." If one centers on themselves and feels good, that is where it ends. "Today was good. I am full." From there, hunger begins. If one feels good for themselves, it ends, but the path of being able to feel good for others is endless. Therefore, they do not fail.

In your faith life, it is true that darkness comes, but to prevent that darkness, "Live for others!" is the message. Even if you come out for early morning prayer and pray earnestly, it is better to pray for the faith companions at the door of three households during that time than to attend early morning prayer for several hours. Even one minute is better. That is how one receives blessings. Without such an ideology, one cannot unify the world.

The path of faith cannot only be chosen for higher and more precious positions, so today, in practicing faith, it is emphasized to sacrifice and serve centered on such content, even if vaguely. You must understand this. What does this mean? It means that in our faith life, darkness will inevitably come, and sacrificial service is a natural bridge and a fortifying action to guard against that darkness. Therefore, we must recognize that God, who loves us, has taught us this principle. Why does this become a way to block darkness? Because it is contrary to the essence of Satan. It is contrary to the essence of evil.

What is the nature of evil? It is to live for oneself. If there are ten people, it seeks to put all ten people under its feet and use them. If that happens, they may follow for a while, but soon they will all run away. When they run away, they do not just leave; they take everything with them. They take everything away, leading to destruction. When they fall away, they take everything with them, so destruction is inevitable. However, a person who lives for goodness wants to bring something every time they come. That is their heart. Therefore, they prosper. Thus, you must clearly understand the turning point of prosperity and decline. This is the most necessary thing in faith life.

Even if you have a dark heart, do not pray centered on yourself, "Father, have mercy on me and remove my darkness." Rather, serve others. Look for the person among Unification Church members who is the most pitiful, and if there is such a person, think, "They are more pitiful than I am," and shed tears for them, and your dark heart will be revived. You must understand this adjustment method. Ultimately, it is the heart that cares for others. It is the position where God can sympathize and can take the same form as the direction of the operations that God is currently conducting. Therefore, one must live for others.

When looking at people, just as in traditional medicine there are four types, there are people of Yang quality and people of Yin quality. There are people with temperaments like the East, West, South, and North, and there are also people with intermediate qualities. They are all different. Some people say, "I dislike that person!" while others say, "I like that person!" I might feel nauseated just looking at that person, but others might like them just by looking at them. They are all different. Therefore, even unattractive women get married, and even unattractive men find wives.

I may say I dislike that person, but that is one-sided; it is not the whole truth. Others may like that person. What this means is that humans are not all one-sided according to their own thoughts. Because they have four-dimensional qualities, they are all different. Therefore, we must be in a position of caring for others centered on these four dimensions.

Jesus was also in a position of caring for others centered on the twelve disciples. The question is whether to care from the outside or from the inside. So, will we also be those who care from the outside or those who care from the inside? In other words, will we care while being loved, or will we love while caring? Will we care with compassion, or will we care while being loved? This is the question. Will we care with compassion or will we care while being loved? However, there is no way to care while being loved. Caring while being loved is being a servant. Is there such a thing as caring while being loved? It may seem like caring, but it is not true caring.

Therefore, when caring for others, will you care from the outside or from the inside? This makes a difference. In practicing faith, do not do it from the outside; do it from the inside. That is why Jesus, centered on the twelve disciples, said, "What I do for you is because I want to share my good things with you." If there is something bad, I will shield you, and when you are sad, I will comfort you. "Am I not working harder than you?" This is the correction. This is what parents do. Parents care for their children.

When parents care for their children, they do not do it from the outside but from the inside. It is valuable to care when those children are in difficulty. It is precious to care while being in a high position, in a central position.

For this reason, from the position of being a master, I love the members of the Unification Church. From the position of representing God, "If my hands do not intervene, that person will die. I may want to cast them out when I see them stumbling, but I cannot do that because they will perish." This is the heart of a parent. The preciousness of Jesus is that heart. Because He was in a position where He did not have to care, He cared, and from there, the heart of a parent and the heart of God sprout. That is not the heart of a human. It is not a self-centered heart. It is a higher dimension. You must think about these things.

The place where such a heart emerges is the place where God moves. Standing in the center of humanity on behalf of God, giving and praying for many people, and doing things that can bring joy to everyone is why all people like that person. Even when facing people, even in winter, there are those who correspond to spring, summer, and autumn in front of me. Isn’t that so? Even in the most discouraging situations, just seeing that person makes me happy.

It is the same in the world. If a parent has lost an only child, no one in the neighborhood can comfort them. At that time, it is fastest to travel the three thousand li of the peninsula with a bundle like Kim Sat-gat. While traveling and hearing the circumstances of this person and that person, they realize that they are not the only ones. There are people who are worse off than they are. Even though I have money to travel the three thousand li, when I see someone who is more miserable than I am, I can find comfort for my own sorrow. Even if I encounter a time like winter, I can find solace because there are people like spring, summer, and autumn.

The same goes for the entire Unification Church. Those who came to the Unification Church first are often the ones who are slumping and saying, "What is the will and what is this...?" So, new members see, "Look at those seniors; they are like that." When seeds are sown, sprouts emerge. The new members of the Unification Church are like sprouts. For cabbage to grow, the sprouts must grow, right? Similarly, for the Unification Church itself to grow, many such sprouts must emerge. Those people become the sprouts. However, if one sees that and says, "I cannot trust those people," then they are worse than the sprouts.
Therefore, we must step forward with the heart that says, "I will take the lead and create the sprouts." When we take that step, even if that person faces hardships like the sprouts, it does not become a problem. It is not a problem.

From this perspective, on one hand, it means that new sprouts are emerging. While the Unification Church may seem stagnant on one side, on the other hand, new sprouts are still emerging. Then that place becomes a spring season. Those who know how to seek that spring season where new sprouts emerge and take an interest in it will not fail. They can live alongside it. That is the principle.

To overcome the realm of darkness

The same goes for Reverend Moon of the Unification Church. When the members feel lonely due to a lack of people, they go to the mountains. When their hearts feel heavy, they compare the persecutions they faced in the past for the sake of their purpose with the persecutions of today. They compare the hardships of the past with those of today. They come to realize that today’s hardships are nothing compared to the past. Then why am I feeling weak over something that is nothing? It is because they were thinking of themselves. The conclusion is that they are feeling weak because of themselves. At such times, they need to correct themselves. You must know how to discern these issues in your faith life.

When darkness comes, do not lose the seed of heart for the purpose, that is, do not lose the leaven. You must have the heart that, having sincerely dedicated yourself to the purpose in the past, you will surely sow and reap magnificently when the time comes. You must have the heart to prepare for that and to break through the darkness. If you have such a heart, the purpose will not depart from you.

What will you do when darkness comes? It is difficult to do it alone. Therefore, you should seek a partner and discuss it. But what if you have no companions or teachers? Teach your children. The case of Jesus and the three disciples is just like that. When Jesus shed tears in loneliness, they shed tears with him. It is not just him alone; when three people shed tears together, it becomes a source of comfort. That is where recovery happens. Therefore, it is essential to have such relative companions or teachers. You must always keep this in mind.

Next, if you have faced tenfold persecution and entered darkness, you should enter a place of a millionfold persecution. You must take on the challenge. If you are in a place of tenfold suffering and God has left you, entering a place of a millionfold suffering will lead God to hold you again. Isn’t that right? When a wayward child leaves home, the parents think, “That child will come back because of their behavior and habits.” They are indifferent. But when that child is going to die, saying, “If I go out now, I will surely die,” the parents will block the child’s way. Will they not? They will stop them, saying, “Oh! You rascal!” and hold on to them.

Therefore, if you have entered darkness due to tenfold persecution, if you boldly step forward with your life on the line toward a millionfold trial, there will be recovery.

The turning point of rise and fall

Now, when you consider whether there is a way to prevent darkness from coming upon you, it is simple. Live for others. Live for ten people and for a hundred people.

Do not think that if you do this, you will be blessed, or that you will receive God’s grace this way. You should have the heart that says, “Since God goes this way, shouldn’t I also go this way?” and maintain a steady heart of sincerity. Even if you live your life with such a heart and go to the spirit world empty-handed, when the ten people you helped go to heaven, they will not let you remain at the bottom of hell. Those ten people will unite before God and say, “He is the center of our lives, our benefactor, and like a parent to us, so we must honor him in a more glorious place.” Thus, their glory can become your glory.

To be someone who does not fail

If you are a Unification Church member walking this path, even if the Unification Church fails, that person will not fail. Even if everyone falls away and only one person remains, you must have the heart to support that one person, discuss with them, sacrifice for them, and build a relationship with them. If you go out with such a heart, what will happen? Even if the Unification Church fails, there will be something that remains.

Just because everything that has failed is dealt with and processed does not mean that everything disappears. There will be something that remains. The last person to go will take the remnants of what has failed and make it their own. Do you understand what I mean? Even if it has failed, if there is still money left, they will inherit that. No one can oppose that. It is meant to be taken.

Such a person is a formidable individual. However, those who act according to their own whims in the middle will not be recognized by anyone. Those who endure to the end will be blessed. You can be blessed even in a place of failure. Even if you have to flee, you can take the capital for business with you. This is how you can think.

So, what is the way not to fail? If Reverend Moon of the Unification Church is someone who will fail, then be more loyal than him. Have a public spirit that is even better than my ideology. Then all the achievements that Reverend Moon has built up until now will come to an end through that person. If that person’s heart for goodness is absolute, God will say, “You are useful,” and guide them to a better path. He will not guide them down a bad path. Therefore, you must understand that those who move for the whole will not fail.

When you move forward centered on yourself, loneliness will come, and destruction will follow. However, if you sacrifice and serve for others, you cannot help but prosper. Sacrificial service will inevitably lead to prosperity. That is why the Unification Church conducts such operations until the nation is found. This is an extremely wise operation.

What do we have?

Recently, the teacher has been touring the regions of Gyeonggi-do and Gyeongnam, meeting with women. When he meets these women, they shed tears. Even though they see the teacher every morning at the headquarters and do not greet him, they cry with joy when they see him. Everyone! Have you ever heard me say that we should live while eating and playing? When have you heard me say that we should eat well, play well, and live well? Look. What good is living well? This is the only path we can take without failing. You must understand that the teacher has been guiding you with this in mind.

We have no nation. North and South Korea are divided in two. We must drive out the enemies that have settled in North Korean territory with our ability and sincerity. We must remove the corruption in South Korea with our strength. We must blow up the den of evil.

To do this, it is not about making proclamations. When the sun rises in the morning, does it declare, “I am rising”? When the sun sets in the evening, does it declare, “I will set”? At this point, we recognize that since the 12th and 13th centuries, humanistic ideologies began to develop, and by the late 16th century, humanism that denies the existence of God emerged. We know that having gone through such ideologies, we have now reached a desperate limit where we conclude that God is dead. 

However, the God that was denied in the past is not nonexistent, and the God that has been lost today is not dead. God must not disappear from humanity, so even when expelled from the boundary of denial and completely negated, God has broken through that denial and has continued to work throughout history. 

When we think about this, it is God's responsibility to seek a single path at this present moment. So where should we find the clue to this problem? It is not in the world of scientific results achieved through human society. If God exists, we must seek a new path under the religious foundation that has been denied. 

Therefore, how to stimulate and reproduce a new spiritual ideology in the era of human history is now the mission that religion must undertake. 

In light of this issue, we must first acknowledge the existence and value of God before finding the inherent value of humanity. Along with recognizing the existence and value of God, we must also recognize God’s presence, and we need a new religious world that can establish a relationship that allows God to influence our emotions and our personal character within our living sphere.

In this sense, today’s religious foundation must be equipped with new content that can deny the ideologies claiming that God does not exist and can turn the environment that denies God into a new positive force. The question of how to manifest that subjective power and motivation is undoubtedly the most important issue in the modern world.

Thus, what the Unification Church hopes for is not the ideology of entering heaven but the ideology of establishing heaven. In today's era, when humanity is in a desperate and extreme world, where they cannot even manage their own existence, there must be a religion that can present a new image with new meaning and from a new dimension. It is clear that the Unification Church must take on the responsibility of firmly establishing this position of religion.

Therefore, the Unification Church is not a religion that hopes to go to heaven but a religion that aims to realize heaven. You must have a faith that testifies to God, not just a faith that believes in God. This movement must arise in the historical end times, and the Unification Church must be the one responsible for such a movement. Thus, we must go forward by testifying to God rather than merely believing in Him. At the same time, we must also pioneer a living environment where we can live together with the testified God. This is what the new religion required in the historical end times should present. 

Moreover, this is the way that humanity can break through the limitations of the past and find a way that God can seek. This is not achieved through any civilization; it is accomplished through God as the motivation. If we can discover a religion that brings new joy to our hearts, allowing us to transcend all living environments and enjoy joy and glory even in the most difficult circumstances, then from there, we can dream of the spring world that humanity hopes for.

In that sense, we realize that a religion that can transcend the times, innovate the times, and stimulate all senses of the era in a new way is absolutely necessary for modern people today.

Rather than sitting quietly in meditation and facing trials, we need a lineup of believers who can represent the existence of God in the trials we encounter in all aspects of our lives, or at the crossroads. When we think about this, we realize that we, the members of the Unification Church, must embody such a figure.

The Unification Church has gone through over 20 years of history. We have walked a path where the hopes we longed for have not been fulfilled, but amidst this, we have groaned and stumbled. What is it that we have struggled with? It is the question of how to establish a relationship between God and ourselves.

The relationship between God and ourselves is the issue. That relationship must be stronger than any relationship or connection in today’s society. Our resolve toward God must be stronger than the loyalty of a patriot to their country, the filial piety of a son to his parents, or the loyalty of a virtuous wife to her husband. When we look at the difficult social conditions surrounding us, we must not retreat in the face of those challenges but rather possess the ability to overcome them and move forward. God needs individuals who can break through and advance rather than those who are caught up in the current society and cannot manage themselves. You must become such a person. Otherwise, you will not be able to become a harbinger of the new spring day. You will not be able to present a new purpose of hope or a coordinate of hope to humanity struggling in a globally difficult environment.

Therefore, what does the historical path of suffering we have walked for decades mean? It means that God has trained and prepared us to create subjective individuals who can break through the world struggling in the abyss of suffering. We must recognize that the path of suffering is such a period.

At this time of suffering, we must not be discouraged but rather hold onto hope for tomorrow. With that determined hope and resolved heart, we must not be overwhelmed by any environmental encroachments but rather counterattack. Thus, we should use the period of suffering to cultivate new pioneering capabilities, strengthen our self-control, and absorb the environment.

You must realize that the steps you have taken through 5, 10, or more years of faith have been to prepare you for the global stage of trials, to place you on the trial stage of tribes and nations within the same living sphere. And you must recognize that this is God’s love.

You should think that this trial is God’s loving hand that has trained you through a fierce process of suffering to create a group that will not fall in the face of increased trials when you step onto the trial stage of foreign nations beyond your own. If you think and resolve this way, then the steps you have taken until now will become a foundation that can shine before the hope of tomorrow. When we focus on reality, the greater the trial stage that approaches us, the more we must not be discouraged; rather, if we are resolute, it will become an absolute motivation that is essential for a new departure toward tomorrow. Here, whether it is a nation or a tribe, a single word can determine the motivation to embark toward a new world stage.

If we have made efforts to meet such a time, that time will be when the Unification Church surpasses the limits of the nation and enters a new spring season toward the world. Such a historical era will undoubtedly come before us.

However, just because it is spring does not mean that everything will bloom. Spring is a continuation of winter, and since it is connected to winter, there will inevitably be trials during that period. These trials are for welcoming spring. When we think about this, if we approach the trials before the hope of tomorrow with a strong and bold attitude, the trials that come will not manifest as strong and great trials but will gradually appear as smaller trials.

When we reflect on the days that have passed, the time when the Unification Church faced trials within the Republic of Korea was like winter. So what does that winter mean? We must consider that winter is a trial period that determines whether life itself can remain as complete life or not.

If the past trials of a seed are great, the life force that remains within those trials can become the essence of life that can welcome the spring day. When that is the case, as the earth rises and the sky lowers, when it receives the warm sunlight of spring, it will sprout as a new shoot. When that happens, that shoot will become the master of spring, the master of summer, and the master of autumn. Moreover, it cannot help but become the beloved entity of the one who planted that seed. This is an undeniable fact.

So what is the current moment of the Unification Church? It is the time to overcome the trial process on behalf of this nation and state. To put it in seasonal terms, it is the time when we have reached the boundary line of overcoming winter toward the beginning of spring.

Then, how noble are you, who have been trained in the past? How much can you extend toward the new spring, the new summer, and the new autumn? The issue is how much you can embody a life force that cannot be invaded by anyone, extending infinitely in one direction from your heart, and how you can possess a subjective self that can not only affirm that but also receive the recognition of others. This is the most important attitude you must have in welcoming spring.

If you can be such a person, then that spring has come for you, and praising the value of that spring means praising a new life form rather than the external spring itself. 

However, no matter how much spring has arrived, if there are no flowers blooming to stimulate joy and reveal glory, then that spring is worse than summer and autumn. Therefore, there must be flowers that can adorn spring beautifully and boast of spring as spring. Where there are flowers, there must be fragrance. Thus, we must become flowers that can emit fragrance, and to become such flowers, we must first be trees with life force.
A historic spring when God will come to us will surely arrive. From that perspective, when you look at yourselves, have you become a living tree that can bloom and spread fragrance? If you have become such a being, you will laugh at the strong winter that has passed.

In such a position, you will be able to judge the historical suffering through your service. And rather than letting historical suffering flow away as an element of lament, you will be able to absorb it as an element of joy and nourishment. Such a person will have a position of subjective strength.

From that standpoint, only those who can appear with an attitude to judge history and welcome a new era will be the ones who can greet the spring. This cannot be a natural conclusion. Therefore, the question is whether I can become such a being.

Today, as we move forward centered on our will, especially the long-standing members should recognize that now is not the time to discuss past events, but rather to discuss tomorrow and to discover ourselves that can be proud in the world of tomorrow.

As the cold and harsh winter passes, and as we move past the beginning of spring, we will be able to bloom, spread fragrance, and boast of our vitality. Therefore, today, rather than reminiscing about the past and admiring and boasting about the periods of trials and suffering, we should be able to boast of our own self that is preparing and looking forward to the hope of tomorrow. Without being able to boast of the authority of our moved selves to greet tomorrow, we cannot say that we have become beings that can welcome the spring.

Merely remaining as the self that has gone through the trials of the past, that winter process is not enough. We must become beings that can greet spring after passing through winter, overflowing with vitality and spirit, and be able to reach out in all directions with the hope of tomorrow, fulfilling the lost hopes of humanity in our time. If we cannot become such a being, we cannot be seen as a being that possesses life capable of welcoming spring.

When spring comes, flowers will bloom, and when flowers bloom, fragrance will spread. Then, not only countless saints and angels but also God will be able to start the freedom that can move.

When we think of the miserable lamentation that humanity has not been able to greet the joyful spring day like a garden with God, we must ponder how to establish groups of people who can bloom God's ideals centered on some religion that aims for the purpose of a new history in this miserable historical process, overcoming suffering and adversity.

For this reason, humanity has fought on as offerings, inheriting that purpose while becoming offerings. The joy of inheriting that purpose is indeed the spring.

Many humans have longed for that spring they could not taste, but we must ensure that we can finally experience and embody that spring. When we think of this, the Unification Church must move toward such a world. Because God is alive, He will surely lead us to that world.

The True Meaning of Suffering and Trials
The longer the trials are, the more they become the harbingers of liberation for that nation and people. And it is not in the environment at the time of liberation that we are welcomed, but in the position of welcoming the history after liberation.

God's will is to complete the restoration history. We should not feel joy at the boundary line where the human ancestors fell, but rather at the realm that has not fallen, the realm that transcends the fallen line. We must be able to feel joy in the eternal hope, and we must have the content and foundation that can connect us to the world representing the future to greet spring. You must understand that we should feel joy beyond that boundary where the human ancestors fell.

So, who are the people who can feel such joy? Those who live comfortably in their positions do not feel such joy. When hungry, even tasteless food feels delicious, and when full, even delicious food feels tasteless. We experience such opposing phenomena. Similarly, those who suffer can feel immense joy in even the smallest comfort, while those in joy cannot feel the same level of joy as those in suffering, even if they receive joy hundreds of times over.

Therefore, suffering and trials are not merely bad in some sense. They can stimulate good things and make them more worthwhile. Because of them, ordinary things can be placed on the absolute value standard. This is only possible in the realm of suffering.

You will understand when you find yourselves in prison or in a place of extreme famine. At such times, even a single bean or a grain of rice feels invaluable, worth thousands or millions. Similarly, suffering and trials are not bad. For those who have the strength, hope, and desire to establish the value of life amidst suffering and trials, those difficulties do not end merely as difficulties; they can become stimuli for joy in the future. Furthermore, not only joy in the future but also the hope of finding the land of hope... If you have the hope to overcome difficulties, you can realize the kingdom of joy from that position. Without overcoming difficulties, no hope can be realized, which is why God, who loves us, trains us to overcome the trials that lie ahead.

Thus, when we think of the training process, it does not end merely as training itself, but as a path of suffering that allows us to feel the joy of stimuli more valuably. Therefore, suffering is not bad, nor is difficulty bad. We must understand that it becomes the foundation of our happiness and the factor that allows us to inherit tomorrow's happiness.

When we look at the historical process, the protagonists of history are those who have fought while holding onto the hope of their nation, overcoming the peaks of suffering in that era. We know that such people are the protagonists of history.

Who are the saints? They are those who, upholding the heavenly will, deny the positive aspects of this human world, change the direction of the world, and overcome the trials of the environment by sacrificing themselves for the world of hope. We understand that saints are those who have done this.

The lives of such saints may seem miserable, but all the hardships they endured internally became the motivation to connect with the world of joy. When we consider this fact, we must understand that the Unification Church has walked the path of suffering not to destroy the Unification Church but to develop it into a church that can shine more brightly in the world, ready to greet the spring day of tomorrow.

How much joy have we felt amidst suffering? How much self-control and subjective capacity do we have to admire the kingdom of hope amidst trials? That becomes the motivation to overcome the realm of death or trials. If there is someone who has fought to feel joy while stepping over trials day by day, that person will be overwhelmed with hope when the time to greet spring comes. They will not be able to sleep or sit still; they will be compelled to spread their arms and proclaim that spring has come to the whole world, preparing and affirming themselves.

Then, the question is how many among the many people who believe in the Unification Church today exhibit such a figure. Can we find such a figure among the so-called long-standing members? It is indeed a sorrow that there are no such people.

If we have fought such battles, now is the time to become a being equipped with the details of further advancement and development. We must not have anyone who seeks or reminisces about that time of trials.

We should be overflowing with the noble spirit and attitude to accept the current position with a heart of joy and to continuously reach out toward the spring garden of tomorrow's hope. If there is sadness and despair in that self, God will not greet the spring day with such individuals.

Even if tomorrow may fail, that face, that heart, and that resolution should be filled with hope, brimming with the joy of welcoming a new morning. You must feel that this living foundation can connect with God, who can be moved by that feeling.

The question is how we will be able to raise our hands and praise before the universe, claiming that we have finally welcomed the joyful spring day. It should be a posture of praying before the Father, holding onto the Father's hand, and resolving to walk with the Father without letting go. This is what must be established in the Unification Church today. Without this, the Unification Church cannot advance toward the spring of tomorrow. However, when you think of the past where you stood in a negative position regarding the path of suffering, we are presenting this period once again to digest it positively. That is why we have deployed the wives of blessed families nationwide beyond the years 1970 and 1971. You must understand this.

This deployment is not meant to conclude anything. It is not to leave behind the historical sorrows of the Unification Church that have been criticized before this nation and people, nor is it to make them offerings to eliminate any conditions of indemnity. It is a heavenly love and compassion that presents a good opportunity for them to greet a new spring day and to overcome the past that could not be overcome while reminiscing about the old days.

If there are husbands receiving letters from wives on the front lines, they must understand that those letters are a clarion call. They are not letters from wives who went out to evangelize in the past, nor are they mere recommendations. Those letters are the good news that winter has passed and a new spring has come, an invitation to go toward a new nation. Therefore, you must be grateful and not rush to organize yourselves, for you will not inherit the coming future of the Unification Church's spring.

At such a time, we must recognize that God's command to us is both a testament to His greater love for us and a warning of the last days.

You will be able to know that the time has come to hear that spring is coming through the news conveyed by those wives. You will realize that the news they bring is different from that of 1960. You will also see that their movements are different, and you will understand that the position of the Unification Church has changed. Considering all these internal and external contents, we truly see that spring is approaching us.

How far should this spring's influence extend? It must not only reach the land of South Korea but also the land of North Korea. This is the issue. For this to happen, the sun that has descended below the equator must rise above the equator. Similarly, we must initiate a movement that allows the strength and influence of South Korea to reach North Korea.

While material strength is necessary to initiate this movement, spiritual strength must be even stronger to surpass North Korea. You must understand that how we present this will determine whether the spring that can unify North and South Korea will come upon the Korean Peninsula.

When we think of this issue, we have passed the time of praying only for South Korea as in the past. We must embrace our fellow countrymen in North Korea, more than 13 million in the five provinces, with our strength and capacity.

We must vigorously hold the flag of spring and melt the frozen land of North Korea, demonstrating our subjective capacity so that they can greet spring. We must not only unite the national subject but also combine with the relative land of North Korea and further fulfill our mission as a subject nation that can establish the appearance of Asia centered on Japan and China, allowing all of Asia to greet spring. We must start from the internal spiritual stage, not just the external stage of South Korea. If we can greet the spring of heaven with strong vitality that can infinitely extend, our entrusted mission will surely be fulfilled.

In the Unification Church, there have been trials that had to be overcome centered on the land of South Korea, but now there is a process of trials to greet spring even in North Korea. The land of North Korea has been in winter until now, and now is the time when winter and spring are confronting each other. It is not a time when winter confronts winter, but a time when winter confronts spring, which means that as spring comes, winter will recede.

As spring matures, just as it receives the heat of the hot sun, we must also become the maternal love that can inspire humanity, centered on the Unification Church and the internal united strength.

Therefore, even if greater and more numerous trials come than in the past, we must become beings that can overcome those trials and remain unaffected by internal issues. When spring arrives, there may be invasions and conflicts at the borders, but we must not be affected in our internal positions.

In such internal positions, spring will remain as spring, while externally we will stand in a position to welcome summer and autumn, but spring will gradually expand and begin to conquer the world.

When we think that it must be so, if a subject nation that can do so is determined, through that center, countless ancestors who have come and gone in the historical process will greet it with the joyful spring.

God, who has worked for thousands or even hundreds of thousands of years centered on the will of providence, will also welcome that day as an indescribable glorious day. How much God will desire that spring, how much the saints in the spirit world will desire it, how much the members of the Unification Church will desire it, how much our fellow countrymen in North Korea will desire it, and how much all humanity will desire it, we must consider.

Therefore, we must develop this movement of the new spring day permitted by God throughout the world, transforming the entire earth into a garden of flowers, so that a free heaven where God can be welcomed may appear everywhere. Without this spring coming to this earth, the hopeful summers and autumns, as well as the original times we desire, the era of fruitful civilization will not come.

we must understand how important our responsibility is to present a new spring, to initiate a new spring, and to make it a reality.
