In Search of the Path of Restoration
<Prayer> Beloved Father! Today is April 11, 1971, the 16th day of the lunar calendar, and it is the second Sabbath of this month. Please be with us this morning.

We know well that walking the path of a meaningful life with God as a life among the flowing years is an infinitely valuable life journey. Just as yesterday and today are different, today and tomorrow must also be different. 

We must think that where those passing days are welcomed as meaningful days in the journey of life, the hopes of humanity begin. 

As we welcome new days in the path of your will, how eagerly are you waiting for your will to be spread over this earth? How many paths of suffering have your children on this earth overcome to reach a day when they can do so? Father, we earnestly wish for you to come here.

As we reflect on the past ten years on this day, there have been days of sorrow that left worries before you. However, we know that you have endured.

We also know how much effort you have put into leading our church, and how much effort you have made to protect this nation and this people. We thank you for protecting our humble family and for keeping us under your grace until today, April 11, 1971.

When we ask how many things this year have made you happy and how many things have made you sad, we realize that there have been more things to make you sad than to make you happy. We must once again ask for your forgiveness. When we think about how careful your footsteps are as you come to us on a day of victory, we, your children, who have not been able to carefully follow the path of your will, have gathered here before you, so please forgive us.

As we enter this 1970s, we must think that your nation, your will, and all the purposes you desire must be fulfilled through insignificant human beings. We know that we, who are gathered here as your children, are those human beings. 

Before the will you desire, we may appear lacking, but because we are well aware of our shortcomings, we have a sincere heart that feels inadequate and wishes to become even a stepping stone before you through humility and self-sacrifice. Father, please look upon us with compassion and take pride in us. 

We earnestly hope that you will bless these individuals you have established, allowing that blessing to shine even more brightly. 

This morning, if there are those from various places in South Korea who are looking toward this place and giving thanks on the day of your grace, please bless them. If there are those who are determined to walk the path in the time of providence and the remaining historical journey, and who bless our families, churches, and nation, please bestow upon them all blessings.

We know that countless spirits in the spiritual world and our ancestors have worked for such a time as this and are eagerly awaiting a day of liberation and heaven on this earth. Father, when we think that we cannot welcome such a day without committing to the path of labor, please strengthen your children gathered here and allow their inadequate appearances to be presented as proud appearances before you.

Father, at this time, please hold our bodies and minds completely in your hands, and as if you have found the son you have longed for, may you rejoice. Please give us your commands in a gentle manner. Grant us a new mission. We must be allowed to achieve a fruitful life in this 1970s. Please bless the blessed families, and especially protect the young daughters who are on the front lines. You know all their circumstances, so please bestow your blessings upon them.

When we think about how many things we still have to do before you, we feel how heavy our responsibilities are. We thank you for being with us on this altar, and we hope you will continue to be with us.

We must not become debtors before you. Even if we exert all our strength in the journey of life, please let us be your daughters who do not owe you anything. Please bless the husbands and children who feel various hardships and worries in silence.

We know that we must devote all our sincerity in this year of 1971, so we earnestly hope that you will protect this poor nation. We sincerely hope that you will fully protect it so that it can live with your will.

When we ask who bears the responsibility for the division of the North and South, we know it lies with this people. We know it lies with the countless denominations centered on this people. When we think that we must bear the responsibilities that these denominations have failed to bear, we must resolve to fulfill the mission of pioneers for tomorrow with confidence. 

We must not become those who lose heart in the path of the pioneers today, so we earnestly hope that you will encourage us.

The day when the North and South are unified, the day when countless nations will praise and you will rejoice, must come soon. The day when your heavenly reconciliation can be established on the Korean Peninsula must come. No matter how strong evil may be, we know that where there are filial and loyal subjects who serve you, evil cannot invade. 

We must be able to recognize that the children gathered here have fallen short in their filial piety and loyalty. We must become one body and one heart. We know that on the day when we unite around your will, we will prosper, and on the day of division, we will perish.

The name of unification has been called the name of suffering until now, but from now on, it must remain the name of glory. When we think about the path that must be taken toward glory has already been set, we must feel the heavy responsibility that we must secure the foundation of unification today.

May this church become one, may your children scattered throughout South Korea become one, and may your children scattered throughout the world become one, so that the Unification Church can fulfill its responsibilities before this era, this world, and history without shame.

Father, now please take charge of the 1970s after 1971. When we welcome the 1980s, may it be a day when we can give thanks before you, and when we look back on the past days, may we be your sons and daughters who can truly draw a life of gratitude. 

We earnestly ask that you raise us up as blessed children who receive your blessings in fulfillment and are without lack as good children. 

We know that this April is the month of Easter, so please let everything be in your glory and allow a new spring to come upon this earth. We earnestly ask for this and offer all these words in the name of the True Parents. Amen.

<Words> Today is April 11, the second Sunday of April. I believe it is a day celebrated as Easter in many churches.

The Path of Restoration that Must Be Resolved
For fallen humanity, if there is no hope for restoration, that is, to return, it is truly despair, and humanity cannot find a world of hope.

Restoration has become the greatest sorrow for humanity. However, when we think that God is weaving our path to resolve this sorrow from behind, while tracing the good original position that has not been lost or expelled, we must give thanks. 

It goes without saying that the Father wishes to completely save humanity as soon as possible. He wants to accomplish the salvation of humanity quickly, but since the fall is a matter of heart and love, it has become entangled.
External problems alone cannot lead to restoration. You must understand that the path of restoration cannot be achieved without centering on love and forming connections based on it. 

That love must encompass the love of parents, the love of children, and the love of spouses. If there is anything the saddest for humanity, it is losing the love of parents, losing the love of spouses, and losing the love of children. There is nothing sadder than that. If there is a grievance, it lies there; if there is misery, it exists in that place. 

When we consider this issue, it is not only that humanity has lost the most precious love, but God has also lost the most precious love along with humanity. The fall of humanity is not a fall limited to individual beings; it has caused God to fall into a miserable state and has impacted all of creation. Due to that fall, the heart of God has been pierced, and humanity has had to bear the cross of suffering on the long path of restoration. We know that this has continued according to the providential time until now. 

The path of restoration requires the restoration of the individual first, then the family, and after restoring the family, the restoration of the tribe, nation, and world must follow. Today, starting from the individual to the ends of the world, or from the origin of history to the end of history, this fate of restoration continues to remain. 

The ancestors who have already come and gone on this earth are also destined to walk the path of restoration because they are descendants of the fall. The 3 billion people currently living on this earth are also in the realm of the fall, so they are in a position to resolve the fate of restoration. Even for the descendants who will come in the future beyond our time, if they cannot break through this realm of fall and cannot resolve it, the path of restoration will remain. That path will be repeated. 

Therefore, individual victory alone will not resolve that path. The victory of the individual must connect to the victory of the family, the victory of the family must connect to the victory of the tribe, the victory of the tribe to the victory of the nation, the victory of the nation to the victory of the world, and the victory of the world must connect to the victory of God. Furthermore, it does not end with the victory of God; a liberating heaven centered on God's love must unfold for everything to be complete. 

The reason is that if the source of restoration, which is bound by love, is not resolved through love, it cannot be achieved. This path is opened and these issues are resolved through love. That love is not the love in human relationships. In other words, it is not love between humans, nor is it love with any specific spirits. 

What is the motive of the fall? It is not the separation of human relationships that became the motive, but the separation of the relationship between God and humanity that is the motive of the fall. Originally, love should have started from God, not from humanity. The fall did not begin with love's connection initiated by God, but rather it started with humanity. Therefore, the fall began with a focus on humanity. 

To return to the original position from this human-centered standpoint, we must not advocate for love centered on humanity. In such a position, there is no way to return. Loving centered on humanity and presenting love centered on humanity may become an internal connection that can expand the foundation of restoration, but it cannot establish a relationship with the new world of God's heart. This is an undeniable fact when viewed in light of the principle of the fall. 

Then what is the love that was first established by God? The relationship between God and humanity is that of a parent and child. 

Who is God? God is not an abstract being but the one we can feel with our highest senses, the subject of the whole through our consciousness or all our sensory organs. Satisfaction begins through encountering Him, and the factors of happiness begin. Everything else cannot be a factor of happiness before us. 

Before children, parents can represent the joy of the whole and can be the center of happiness. Likewise, God must be that for humanity. God must be the center of our love, the center of life, and the center of hope. Everything that God passes through, moves, changes, and lives must not only be felt as God's but must also be inherited into human actions, and all of God's heart must be inherited into human hearts. 

Through that inherited heart, men and women must come together to form the bond of marriage. If the ancestors of humanity had received God's love and matured in joy without facing a day of sorrow due to the fall, and if they had received blessings in the realm of love centered on God, in other words, if they had held a wedding, that couple would not have become a wicked couple but would have undoubtedly become a good couple. 

If that had happened, God would have surely rejoiced. That joy would not have been a biological joy but a joy welcomed in the ecstasy centered on love, and that day would have been the day of happy beginnings for our human ancestors. That day would have been the day when humanity could laugh the happiest, rejoice the most, and boast the most. The day they raised their children with all their devotion would have been a joyful day for God, who stands in the position of a parent. 

That day was a joyful day for humanity and a joyful day for God, and the love of the couple realized in that joy must be a love that God could rejoice in. Thus, connected through joy, united through joy, the ancestors of humanity, who should have seen the beginning of joy, instead prepared a source of curse with sorrow, which is the fall. 

Although their departure from God's embrace was indeed sorrowful, the fact that they were expelled from the realm of God's love, which is the source of eternal life, is even more sorrowful. We know that falling into the realm of fall, which cannot be regained by any individual's effort, is the motive of humanity's tragedy. 

We must also reflect on the fact that humanity today is destined to become such parents. When faced with the sons and daughters born from such a couple, instead of meeting them with joyful faces, they are confronted with shame before God, bearing the grievances of the fall from a position contrary to future hope. The firstborn son of Adam's family, Cain, and the second son, Abel, were born in such a position. Abel must be able to overcome Cain, and without overcoming the difficulties of the parents, he cannot find joy. We must understand how miserable that position is. 

From this perspective, if God's love has established a familial framework flowing from God to the bond of spouses and the bond of children, then the love realized there is indeed God's love, the love of spouses, and the love of children connected together. The whole that harmonizes in the unity of God's love, the love of spouses, and the love of children would indeed be a happy place that God would rejoice in, that the ancestors of humanity would rejoice in, and that the descendants of humanity would rejoice in. How much has God longed for that place, and how much have our human ancestors wished for it? However, due to the fall, such a place has not yet appeared before humanity. 

That place would have God above and humanity below, where the vertical historical path spanning three generations from God to Adam and his sons could be nestled within God's love. It would be a foundation of indescribable joy and a foundation of God's love. 

As the ancestors of humanity, Adam and Eve would have wanted to boast about their children as soon as they became parents. When asking who they could boast to, of course, Adam and Eve would boast to each other, but they would also want to boast to the angelic world created by God before Adam and Eve. After that, to whom would they want to boast? They would want to boast before God. 

When they had children, if those children inherited a wonderful lineage and possessed excellent qualities both genetically and personally, how happy Eve would have been! The more adorable that baby was, the more that cuteness was not just something she felt for herself but something she wanted to boast about to God, Adam, and the world of future hope. Such a magnificent and wonderful love was to be realized, yet Eve found herself in a position where she had to lower her face before God, feeling ashamed. Instead of appearing with a dignified posture, she was in a repressed position, looking down at the ground, feeling the need to lament her own state. This is indeed an extremely tragic situation. 

This history has woven itself and spread horizontally, forming nations, forming states, and forming the world we live in today. Here, we must return again. What must we do to return? We cannot simply return. Descendants of bad ancestors cannot return beyond the good or bad achievements established by those ancestors. They must inherit them and return. 

From this perspective, the current Earth, where 3 billion people live, is a world of fall. Here lies the grievance of humanity. There is the grievance of 3 billion people worldwide. The grievance of humanity transcends nations and states. 

Not only is there the grievance of humanity, but there are also countless grievances connected to nations, states, clans, families, and individuals. You too are connected to a thread of humanity's grievance. You cannot escape from the great burden of humanity's grievance, as you are connected by a single thread to it. No matter how much effort you make or how much you struggle, no one has been able to cut that thread of grievance and overcome it. 

When considering that you are one being among humanity in such a position, and when reflecting on our lives today, cutting that thread of grievance from your individual self does not mean it is severed. Even if you cut that path of grievance from yourself, it still depends on your family; if you cut it from your family, it depends on your tribe. Even if you cut it from your tribe, it depends on your nation, and even if you cut it from your nation, it depends on all of humanity. 

Therefore, humanity must collectively bear the fate of resolving the miserable path of restoration. We must understand that individuals, families, tribes, nations, states, and the world must resolve this issue. 

If God exists, what should we demand? First, we cannot even think of demands for ourselves. Therefore, how do we overcome ourselves? The question is how to discover a transcendent self within the realm of humanity's grievance. The history, philosophy, and religion that have struggled until now have been tasked with this mission. 

When considering where the ultimate point that religion, philosophy, and all truth should seek lies, it has been vague until now. Philosophy has struggled to find the value and origin of existence centered on the problems of life, but what happens when that existence is discovered? When one discovers that existence, they will inevitably encounter the path of suffering, the path of hardship, and the path of adversity, which becomes an even greater issue. 

The reason is that because humanity has been immersed in the realm of grievance due to the fall, even if one sets a standard of "I am this," there is a significant problem to resolve afterward, as many obstacles and conflicts arise. What is that? It is a love centered on the universe or humanity that is greater than the problem of one's own life. When the issue of love related to the absolute God comes into conflict, the question arises: where should the standard for resolution be placed? This is a more important issue than resolving it centered on humanity itself. 

God does not want to impose greater responsibilities on humanity, so He has established philosophy and religion while considering the more miserable path of suffering that humanity will face in the future. God knows that the problem to be solved centered on God's love is more important than solving the issue of one's own life. Therefore, God must first take on the difficult problems and cannot help but relate to humanity's history in order to find the way to solve the issue of love that humanity must ultimately seek. That is why He first established religion to present God's love. 

Even if we have much to boast about, there is a limit to boasting in the presence of that love. Boasting is not eternal. What I possess will disappear with my physical body. However, when viewed through the lens of personality, if there is a person with content of global value, even if their life ends, their personality does not end there; it remains. 

What can sustain a worthwhile personality and connect the content of a valuable personality? This ultimately leads to the issue of love. How much did you love your compatriots? How much did you love your nation? When someone can claim they lived for their nation, the specific content behind that claim determines the standard of a patriot. 

What kind of filial child is the best of all? Is it a filial child of the Republic of Korea? Let’s say there is a filial child who has never existed in the history of the Republic of Korea. That historical filial child may be the best in the Republic of Korea, but when viewed on the global stage, how can we measure whether they are indeed the best of filial children? Just because they are popular or can respond to all external matters of their parents does not make them a filial child. The focus must be on the heart. 

The question is whether they were a filial child who honored their parents from a smooth position or a filial child who honored their parents from a position of contradiction and conflict. The more deeply one feels the content of human sacrificial heart in adversity, the more they become a global filial child. 

If only sadness remains in the universe, then all hopes and aspirations for humanity would be mere illusions. This universe would end in despair. If that happens, all our hopes would collapse into despair. Such hopes cannot be factors of happiness for humanity. 

So, what remains when the sadness of the universe passes and despair also passes? Is it the economic issues that humans desire, or is it the universal personality?

The teachings of Jesus
So who is the best in the world? Who will come in first? There is only one person who can be first. That person is Jesus. Jesus said, "God is my Father." I think that is truly well said. And He also said, "I am the only begotten Son." The term "only begotten Son" means He monopolized God's love.

Then He said to humanity, "I am the bridegroom, and you are the brides." Next, He said, "You are brothers." When God establishes a relationship with humanity centered on love, there is a cosmic harmony that unfolds. The husband will also say to cut off all external relationships and come back.

When we see this, when God calls us, does He say, "Bring all the things you had in the past with you"? He tells us to come after leaving everything behind. What should we first discard? We must start by discarding the things we love the most. What is the thing we love the most? It is our parents. After that, it is our husbands, then our children, our relatives, and our country—everything must be left behind.

That is why Jesus also said, "If you do not love me more than your father, your husband, or your children, you are not worthy of me." What does that mean? Is He asking us to bring those things with us or not? "He is saying not to bring them." Now that I understand that meaning, I ask you, Father, to look upon the groups of the Unification family who wish to live that way with compassion.

Regardless of how the world or the environment is, the path of restoration that you have taught us among these two paths is undoubtedly the way we must go, so we must become your sons and daughters who know how to settle all that we have before this path. 

I entrust the path we will take in the future to you. Today is a holy day, so please bless your sons and daughters scattered throughout South Korea. I earnestly ask that your hand does not leave the many children around the world who are praying while longing for their homeland. May your compassion be with all, and I earnestly request that you lead us as a light in our life journey, and I offer all these words in the name of the True Parents. Amen. 
          Selected Words of Rev. Sun Myung Moon <Volume 42>
